WOLAYTTA SOODDO YUNBBERESTTIYAN
ISSIPPETETTAA SAYINISENNE ASUMMA KOLLOOJJIYAN
WOLAYTTATTO DOONAA LUXETTA MACARAN
HAYYO BILAWU KANEBATA
(FUNDAMENTALS OF LITERATURE)
WLL 221 
LUXISSIYO MOOJUULIYA
Xaafidaara: Alimaayo Fiqira
Goydidaagee: Lissaanu Woldemaariyama
Baraataa 2007
Wolaytta Sooddo
Ha shemppuwaa sintta qofata:  Ha shemppuwaa tamaaridi wurssidoogaappe 
simmin tamaareti: 
?	Bila xifatiyaa birshshettaa yootana
?	Bila  xifatiyaa leemiso gidiyaabata yootana
?	Bila  xifatiyaa maadota zuleyana
?	Bila xifatee bari giddon woqqawu shaahettiyaakko qonccissana
?	Bila  xifatiyaa macaratu giddon de'iya issippetettaanne dummatettaa 
shaakkidi shiishshana. 
Ane bila xifate giyoobi aybakko be'anaappe kasetidi bila-eraa giyoobi aybakko qanttan xeelli simmoos. Bila era giyoobi issibaayyo de'iya saynisiyaawa era, woykko eraa pilggettaa woykko issibaa oottiyo hiillaaninne eran kumida oosuwa bessees gaana danddayettees. Gaasotaykka issibaa oottiyooy eraana woykko hiillaana gidiyo gishshataassa. Issi era oosuwa hanotay, qommoynne ciimmatettay dummatoppe attin ay oosoynne hannannaanne era poliyo hiillaa koyyees.                                                   
Leemisuwassi burqqiya woykko me'ida kushiya woykko tohuwa oyqqiya hiillanchchay he me'uwaa woykko burqqiyaa oyqqanawu koyro ayyo eray de'ana bessees. Hegaappe simmin issi asa kushee/tohoy burqqidaakkonne me'idaakko shaakki erees. Hegaappe simin me'o gidikko ba eraadan  me'ida naa''u meqettata issippe gatti simmidi harabaara gatti qachchees. Qassikka burqqe gidikko wora biida meqettaa zaaridi bari kase gamma sohuwan uttanaadan oottees. Hegaa hiillanchchay oottiyoy awu hagaa oottiyoo eray woykko hillay de'iyoo gishshataassa. Mattaa eessanawu, urqqaappe dumma dummabata medhdhi kessanawu, birataa qoxxidi dumma dumma miishshata kessanawu ha ubbawu A eray A eray de'ana bessees. Ayyo A eray A eray xayiyaaba gidikko polettana danddayenna woykko ubba yaa moorettidi shoraa/puulaa xayees giyoogaa. 

Issibaassi A eri baynna asi waaye baynnan puulaa naagidi yetta cenggurssaa kessi yexxanawu, misiliya misilanawu, mittaappe massi moliyoobata borettiyabi baynnan ootti kessanawu wayssennaba malatii? Hagawu zaaroy chii, wayissees. Keehi loyttidi ootti kessanawu, misilanawunne yetta cenggurssaa metoy baynnan kessi sabbanawu / yexxanawu waayissees. Aybissi giikko ootti bessiyo hiillay/eray baynna gishshataassa. Hageeta ayba balinne baynnan ootti woykko polidi bessanawu he eratu/ hiillatu keettaawa gidana bessees. Hodde bila era giyogee hageeta malatiya polota eta eeshshaadaninne qommuwadan eraanne puulaa maayidi shiiqanaadan danddayissiya hannannaa ogee qoncciyooba. Eraa koyyiya cora oosoti de'iyaaba gidikkonne bayratettan massi moliyoobatu eray, misiliyoo eray, yetta cenggurssaa eraynne xifatiyaa erati aahuwan erettoosona.Ha oyddu bila era macarcti ubbaykka eran polettiya puulaa maayida  eranchchaa oosoy polido asa na'aa de'uwa zaari bessiyaaba  gidida bantta giddon asaa na'aa de'uwa tumatettaa zaari bessiyaa asa na'aa guuggenne kushe ooso gidiyoogan eti malatettoosona. 
Eti ubbaykka bila era ooso gidiyoogan malatettikkonne eti shiiqiyo ogetun qassi dummatoosona. Massi molettiyaabati mittaappe, birataappe, shuchchaappe urqqaappe masetti kiyana danddayoosona. Misilee qassi qalamiyan, buruushshiyan, woraqataa bolli, mittaa bolli, curqqaa bolli hhm tiyettidi shiiqees. Sabay woykko yettay qassi cenggurssan shiiqees/aadhdhees.
 
Ha oyddu bila eraa macarati bantta aadhdhiyo woykko shiiqiyo ogetun dummatikkonne daro eeshshatun malatettoosona. Eti ubbaykka baaso eeshshatun malatettoosona. Eti ubbaykka baaso oottidi denddiyoy ha alamiyaanne ha alamiyaa giddon de'iyaa asaa. Eti asi bari heeran issoy issuwara oottiyo gaytotettaappe kiyiyaaba. Eti asaa na'aa de'uwan polettiyabatuppe beettiyaba. 
Bila xifatee qassi doonaa baggaara nababiyaageetawu shiiqees/aadhdhees. Ha sohuwan nu doonaa giyoo wode haasayaanne xifatiya oyqqees. Gaasotaykka xifatee haasayaa sohuwaan eqqiyaaba gidiyoo gishshataassa. 
1.1. Bila Xifatee Aybee?
Bila-xifatiya aybatettaa xeelliyagan dumma dumma wodetun dumma dumma qofatinne kuushshati imettiiddi takkidosona. Qassi bila xifate bila eara oosotu macaratuppe issuwa gidiyoo gishshatawu ikka daro adussa wodiya kanttidi yiidaba giyoogaa. Hegaa gishshatawu bila xifatiya aybatettaanne A xaafiyo ogiya xeelliyaagan dumma dumma wodetun dumma dumma asatinne citati bantta xeelaadan xeelaadan bantta ooso gophphiyaadan, banttawu malatidaagaadaaninne bantta eraadan woykko bantta hametissiyo qofaadan cora dumma dumma kuushshata immidi kanttidosona. Eti kase gi kanttidobata ha''i nuuni dentti xeellikko go'i de'enna gishshatawu hegaa aggi be''idi bayra gidiyabatukko ane kanttoos. 

Daro palanttiya qofatuppe guuttata ekkidi minonne lefa miyyeta be'idi daro eranchchati maayettiyobata xeellana. Shin eta xeellanaappe kasetidi issi tumanchchabaa xeellidi kanttiyaakko lo''o. Hegeekka aybee giikko bila xifatee keehi aahonne daro macaray ayyo de'iyoo gishshatawu ayyo ubba eranchchati maayettiyo xon''a birshshettaa immanawu danddayettibeenna. Dumma dumma eranchchati /cutati xon''a birshshettaa ayyo demmidi maayettennaadan oottiday I dumma dumma baggaara daro corabaara gayttiyo gishshataassa. Hanno gakkanawu mexile issuwa gidida ubba asi maayettiyo birshshetti beettibeenna; qassikka sinttanawukka beettana giidi ammananawu daro waayissees. Gido shin bila xifatiyaa giya qaalay naa''ubatta qonccissanawu maaddees, koyroykka xaafettidaba gidiyoo wode naa''nttoy odettidabaa bessanaassa. Daro wodiyaan “Bila xifate” giyaa qaalay bessiyoy asi pilggi xaafiyoobaappe biidi diccida saynise oosota gakkanawu de'iyaa xifate oosota bessanaassa; gido shin ha qaalay qassikka asi bari guuggiyaappe medhdhido xifate hiillata/qofata, danttota, diraamata, medhdhi xaafotanne chii medhdhi xaafota malaatanaassi go'ees.
           Meezziyaa
    Kaalli shiiqida daro palamissiya kuushsha qofatu bolli tobbidi intte qofaa issoy issuwaara 
      shaakkite. 
1.	Xaafettidabi ubbi bila xifate. 
2.	Kumetatettay, gitatettaynne ciimmatettaa eeshshay de'iyo ooso. 
3.	Bila xifatee asa na'a xalaali medhdhiyooba. 
Ane eta issuwa issuwa bolli aaho qonccisuwaa kayan kayan birshshidi xeelloos. 
I. Xaafettidabi ubbi bila xifate
Ha palama qofaa hemetissiyaa asati (citati) Girike qaalaappe yiida birshshettaa baaso oottidi palamoosona. He girike qaalaayyo anoy (Litera) yaagiyagaa gidishin A birshshettay xifatiya giyoogaa. Ha qofaa kaaletiya asati pitale meraa oyqqidi shuchchaa bollan, woraqataa bollan, karetta saleedan h.h.m. bolli xaafetti beettiya ubbi bila xifate yaagiyoogaa. Ubba coo dumma dummabutu bollan nu xaafiyo asa suntti, silkke paydoti, zaaroti, coo hada qofati aybinne attennan bila xifatiyan gophphetoosona.
Ha palamay naa''u baaso gidiyaabata ammanttidi xoonana danddayenna. Ha naa''u yiggi xeelliyoobatuppe issoy puulaa medhdhiyo hanotaa qofan yeggibeennaagaa. Ha ogiyan issi ay asinne ayba xifate meezzeenne baynnan biiriya woraqataara gattidikka oottikko bila era gidana hanees. Xaafanchchaa hiillay, eraynne meroy, xifatiya puulay, ufayssiyoonne tamarssiyooba ubbay yiggi xeelettennabata giyoogaa. 
Aybippenne bollaara bila xifatiyaassi denddo gidida asaanaa de'uwa bayrabanne baaso oottidi denddiyoobi ekettiyaaba gidennan atti aggees. Hegaa gishshatawu eranchcha asatanne eta oosotu gatiya xayssees. Keehi daro daafuran polettida oosotanne ubba qassi ayba qofanne aattana danddayenna coo qaacettidabata laggeyidi bila-xifate giyoogan ha qofaa akeekaa xayo malabay beettiyoo gishshatuwa hagee ekettenna qofa gidees. 
Ha qofaa naa''antto metoy qassi bila xifatiyaa mexile issi bagga xalaalaara xeelliyo hanotaa. Daro adussa wodetussi asa na'i bari de'uwan galla galla gayttiya bata, dosiyo ixxiyobata, metuwa, ufayssaa, dere asaara issippe gayttiyo gaytotettaa, wogaa meezziya, bar dichchaanne kunddettaa, bananne bari heeraa, yeletaa hegaadankka hayquwa h.h.m. haasaya xalaalan aattiiddi keehi daro layttatussi de'iis. Xifatee keehi mata wodetun yiidaba. Xaafettidi de'iyabata xalaalawu bila xifate giikko bala gidees giyoogaa. Ha palamaa qofay xaafettidaba xalaalaa bolli wudiyoo gishshatawu woykko haasayettida bila xifatiya bila xifate giidi ekkenna gishshatawu hageekka ekettiya palama gidenna. 
 	

 II. Kumettatettay, gitatettaynne ciimmatettaa eeshshay de'iyo ooso
Ha qofay issi izaawuppenne issi biittaappe kanttiya qofaa aahotettay de'iyooba. Kemettatettay (salo sa'a gufanttobaa) (universal) giyoo wode issi asa woykko issi biitta xalaalaa xeelliya yoho gidenna. Kumetta alamiyan de'iya asanaa xeelliyaaba. Ha yiggi xeeluwan issi xifatee alame ubbaa giddon de'iya dere asaa ubbaa xaaxi waaxiyanne xeelliya alamiyan awa awa biikkonne polettiyaabanne ekettiyaaba gidiyaabanne bari shiquwaninne ohettan keehi hittifironne ciimma qofa gididaageeta xalaalaa doori kessiichchiyaagaa. 

Ha qofaa issi baggaara xeelliyo wode tumukka alame asa ubbaa xeelliyaanne awuninne ekettiyaabaa, nabbabettidi go'aa immiyaabaa h.h.m. giyoode ha qofay nashaa/sabaa demmanaadan oottees. Gidoppe attin asi asa gidoogan asatettan malatettikkonne issi mala asaara de'iyo duussay, lagge tekinooloojiya dichchay, issi mala de'uwa maaray, wogay de'iyoogaa gidenna. Ubbaykka bari de'iyo sohuwaninne biittan issoy haraappe dummatiyo A wogay, doonay, taarikkee buquray de'iyoogaa. Issuwaagee haraayyo injjetenna ixxana danddayees. Issuwagee harawu mitettennan ixxana danddayees. Ubba qassi issoy haraagaa ixxananne shenetana danddayees. Hegaa gishshawu ha alamiyan de'iya ubba asaa de'uwa hanotan gayttiya bata, eta hulluuquwa ubbaa issippe lagge oottidi ekkiyoogee deexxiyaaba gidiyoogan ha qofay borettees. Diccidanne dichchaa bollan de'iya biittatun beettiya xaafanchchati ha qofaa maaran yiggi xeelettiyoo wode dichchaa bollan de'iyaa biittatun de'iya xaafanchchati xoonidi aadhdhana danddayenna gishshatawu lammachcha gidida xaafanchchati diccidi kiyennaadan teqqees. 

Ha qofay qassikka dichchan guyye attida biittati banttawu hanidaagaa (bantta wolqqaadan) bantta bila xifatiya bantta heeraa wogaanne de'uwa maaraa bessiiddi leddan leddan dichchiiddi beennaadan doomettan daganttiya yoho. Keehi diccidanne tekinooloojiya eran biida qofay de'iyo dereta (biittata) xalaalaa eta dichchaadan eta shaakkidi shoobbiyaanne nashshiyaaba gidiyoogan issi bagga asa xalaalawu baggattidi haraa oli aggiyaaba malatees. Xaafettida bila xifatetu xalaalaa ubbakka qassi keehi pilggetta qofaa oyqqidanne keehi gita geetettiyageeta xalaalaa shaakki kessiyaaba gidiyoo gishshatawu I asa xalaali medhdhidoba yaagiyaa baaso gidiya yoho xalaalaa borennan ekkidi kumettatettaanne gitatetta yaagiyaageeta bila xifatetussi qonccissodan ekkanawu metees. 
III. Bila xifatee asa na'a xalaalaba
 Bila xifatee aahuwan qassi bila eray de'iyoo (oosettiyo) baaso yohoy asaa. Hegaassa bila eray (bila xifatee) asa na'a xalaalaba yaagiyoogee. Bila era gidin bila xifatee asa na'i medhdhiyoo, asi garaadiyo, asay bari kahaappe medhdhi kessiyo ayfe. Hegaa gishshatawu bila xifatiya doomettay gidin dichchay asaa na'aara keehi mino gaytotettay de'iyooba. Asa na'i bari heeraa loytti akeekees; paaccees. Asaara issippe de'iyo de'uwa xeellees; paaccees, asaara issippe de'iyo de'uwa xeellees, baaga gidin haraa de'uwan gayttiyaabata bari wozanan oyqqees. Asay bari heeraara, meretaara banaara medhdhiyo korssikarssaa be'idi appe denddidi bari era oosuwa doommees. Bila xifate bari eeshshan keehi aahonne asa de'uwaara keehi oyqettidaba. Hagaa gidiyoo gishshatawu cora dumma dumma ogetuura birshshettaa immees. Qonccissoy qassi sinttanawukka kaalliyaaba. Hegaa gishshawu nuunikka haratu qofaa kaafiyoogan “asa na'aa pilggetta ayfe” giyagan maayettana. 
Dumma dumma bila xifatiya oosoti bila xifate gidiyooga xalaalan etawu issi eeshshay de'ees. Ha eeshshatuppekka bayratiyageeti: Etawu baasoynne eti de'iyo gaasoy asa na'a gidiyoogaa gidishin naa''anttoy eti xaafanchchaa mero ooso; hezzanttoy ha alamiya bollan de'iya asaa de'uwa gishshatidi eqqiyaba gidishin kaalliyaagee bantta cuuccuman tamaarissiiddi bantta medhdhiyo eran kaassoosona. Medhdhi oottiyooba gidikkonne xaafanchchati mal''ettoosonappe attin worddotokkona; issi hanidabaa bolli wottoosona. Hanana danddayennabaa medhdhokkonanne haniis gookkona. Nabbabiya asi ammanettiyoobaa xaafoosona. Haray qassi ay asa maabaraa de'uwaa allaalliya baaso oottidi xaafettana danddayoosonanne bantta giddon de'uwa, tumatettaanne puulaa issippe shiishshi oyqqoosona. 
                 2.1. Bila xifatiyaa Go'ata/maadotanne A aahotettaa
Hagaappe kase nu be'idoogaadan bila xifatee asaa na'aa de'uwaa giddon polettana danddayiyaa tumatettaa baaso oottidi denddiyoo gishshatawu nu de'uwaa A heregan zaari be'oosinne geeddaroos. I de'uwaassi herega. A giddoppe nu de'uwaanne nunatettaa bochchiyaabaa demmeettees. Asaa n'aa de'uwa zaari bessiyaa, de'oy meray ay malakko qonccissiya, asaanaa meretaa, asay asaara de'iyo hanotaa, asaa koshshaanne kahaa zaari bessiyaaba. Dere asaa de'uwa maaraynne meray istta, naa''a geetettidi qoodetti wuriyaaba gidenna. I keehi cora macaraara de'iya, keehi aahogidida duuqqin wurenna aaho abba mala. A xaafidi wurssana danddayiya asi de'enna. Asaa de'uwa giddon de'iyaa hulluuqoy, siiqoy, ixotettay, asaassi de'iyaa koshshay, demmiyoobay, xayiyoobay, makkaliyoobay, kehiyoobay, ashketettay, cinccatettay yeletaynne hayqoy, ammanoy, kaddiyo hanotay, geematettay, qonccetettay h.h.m. asa na'aa de'uwa garssan de'iyabata giyoobatuppe keehi guuttata. Eti issoy issoy birshshidi be'ana giyaakko qoodin, paydiininne zuleyin ollawu wuriyaaba gidokkona. Issi issi bila xifatiya daashshatuyyo etawu eta meray eta moray, shiishshiyo hiillaynne yesoy de'ees. Shiiqiiddi xifatiyaa meraadan aaho de'uwa ciimma hanotaappe dooridi, koyyidi beettiyabaanne qoncciyan yootettana danddayiyabata dooridi kessees. Issi bila xifatiya ooso giddon issi bayra allaalle xalaalay aadhdhanaadan koyettenna. Xaafanchchaykka issi oosuwan cora allaalleta woykko qofata aattanawu denddiyaakko issuwa issitoo haroode qassi haraa denttiiddinne wottiiddi qonccissiyo gishshawu he xifatiyawu shonggi de'enna. 
Ha qommo baggaara uttida hanotan shiiqiyoo wodiyaana bila xifatee dere asaayyo go'aa immiyoogee. Dere asaa beettiya tumatettaa, asi ammanana danddayiyoo de'uwa meraanne asatettaa eeshshaa hegaadaanikka kdaayyo alamiyan koyettiya seeraadan, meraaninne maaran shiiqiyo wode cora go'ati de'oosona. Hegaadaanikka nabbabbiyagawu he oosuwa ootti kessida asawukka go'aa immees giyoogaa. 
Hegaa xalla gidennan bila xifatee issi dere asaa doona gididi he asaa giddon de'iyaa wogaa, meeziyaa, muussaa, ushshaa, yeehuwaa, yettaanne de'uwaa maaraa hanotaa bessiyoogan gita beeraa kaa'ees. I asaa na'aa ha alamiyan de'iyaa dumma dumma cora meezetuura/aazetuura eretisseesinne A nababiyoogan beettiyaa ufayssaanne hayyuwaa demissees.

1.3. Bila xifatiyaa Boolimaa/mucuraa
Bila xifatiyaa mucuraayyo bessiyaabata naa''u dumma dumma eranchchati immiyoo qofaa ane xeelloos: 
(Bob Richard) yaagiyoo xaafanchchay bila xifatiyaa oosoy waayissiyaaba gidiyoogaa qonccissi makkidi ha oosuwaa boolimissanawu heezzubata qoppana bessees yaagees. Hegeetikka:
1. Issi issi yafaraynne polo gididi bali beettana bessennaagaa,
2. Xaafanchchay bari kumetta oosuwaa waati keexxidee? Eeshshaawata xeelliyaagan, taarikiyaa  
     shooqaa xeelliyaagan, birshshi odiyoo hanotaa loytti qonccissidee? Yaagiyaagaanne
3. Eraa (Intelligence) xaafanchchay baruyyo buzo gidida ba era maxaafaakko ehiidee? I bari 
      medhdhido oosuwaa /qofaa gelissiyoo hanotaa xeellees.   

Ha qommo eranchchaappe hara (Steve Anderson) yaagiyoo eranchchay qassi:

1. Payya eeshshaawata – xaafanchchay bari oosuwan go'ettiyoo eeshshaawati suure giigida keehi 
       minonne qoncce gidida gaasuwawu gidana bessees.
2. Xifatiyaan shiishshiyoo/odiyoo hanotay nababidi akeekanawu shugo/waayissennaba gidana 
      bessees. Nababanawu waayissiyaaba gidikko he xaafanchchay bari oosuwaa oottiiddi 
      de'enna. Yohota bessanaadan hanidi aggiigees yootiddi sugennan aggiigees giyoogaa. 
3. Kumettatettaa/aliyaa oduwaa – taarikee nababiyaa uraa issi tumatettaa bessidi malaaliyaa 
      hulluuquwan yeggidi bi erennasaa efaana bessees. Nababiyaagawu issi wurssi eribeenna 
      tumatettaakko efiyaagaa gidana bessees. 
1.4.	Bila xifatiyaa aybissi nabbabiyoo?
Issi asawu bila xifatiyaa nabbabiyoogee keehi cora maaduwaa immees. Ane asi bila xifatiyaa aybissi nabbabiyaakko amarida gaasota kaallidi xeelloos:  
?	Ha alamiyaa bila xifatiyaa bollay/oosoy asana xeelliyaaban oyqqibeennabi de'enna hegaappe denddidaagan haratuyyo de'iyaa xeelaappe, qofaappe, ammanuwaappe maaddiyaabaa demmanaassa aybissi giikko issi issi qofati coo haasayan woykko hada qaalan qonccokkona. 
?	Hara asaa wogaanne ammanuwaa pilgganawu-hanidi aadhdhidabaa timirtte (history) qassikka wogaa pilggettaa oottiyageeti (anthropology) nne ammanuwaa pilggettati asaa wogaanne ammanuwaa tamaarissiyoogaadan bila xifateekka tamaarissees.
?	Doonaa eraa luxanaassi maaddees-Bila xifatiyaa nababiyoogee asaa oorattanne lo'iyaa haasayaa hiillaa tamaarissees. Ha alamiyaan kaalettiyosan de'iyaa gita gita asa ubbay keehi lo'onne hara asaa oyqqiyaa/ufayssiyaa haasayay/doonay de'iyoo asata. Issi qaalay masunxxissees; issi qaalay pattees.
?	Lo'o kandduwaa/eeshshaa tamaarissees-bila xifatee issi yohuwaassi woykko hanotaassi ay mala payya zaaruwaa immanaakko/haasayanaakko korssiyaa immees gaana danddayettees.
?	Qaalaa kochchaa era aassanawu maaddees-ooratta qaalati ooratta qofaassi baaso. Issi ooratta qofay qassi ooratta eraa zal''anawu miishsha/baaso shuchcha. Eray qassi wolqqa.
?	Bila xifatee harata nu be'iyoogaadan nunatettaa zaari bessees- Bila xifatee nunatettaa paacciyoo miishsha. Bila xifatiyaa nababaydda nenatettaa ne qofaa ne eeshshaa demmaasa. Iita meezzekka gidana danddayees. I nuuyyo herega mala; nu kalluwaa/hanuwaa qoncciyaa kessidi bessees.
?	Nu guuggiyaawu ooso immanaassi/ufayssanaassi-Nu guuggee eranchchati oottido oosuwaa nashshiiddinne ufayttiiddi tamaarana bessees.
?	Bila xifatee taarikiyaassi oottido maaduwaa nashshanaassi-Biiree mashshaappe aadhdhiyaa qara. Bila xifatee biittaa laammana keena wolqqay de'ees. Urusiyaa, Chaynaa, Jarmanenne  Amerkkaa taarikiyaa leemisodan xeella xeella.
?	Asaa giddon de'iyaa dummatettaa be'anassinne nashshanaassi-Bila xifate nuuni ubba wode qeeri naatudan nunatetta xalaalaa gamma giiddinne nashshiiddi uttennaadan tamaarissees. Hara asaassi de'iyaa nuugaappe dummatiyaa xeelaakka nashshana bessees.   
Xaaxi waaxiyoo wode bila xifatee hageetussi nne hageetuppe hara corabatussi maaddana danddayees.
                                                               Meezziya 
I.	Kaallidi imettida oyshata nabbabi simmidi waattan waattan gididi tobboogaappe guyyiyaan etayyo gamma gidiyaa zaaruwa xaafidi shiishshite. 

1.	Bila xitatiya xaafanchchaanne misiliyaa misiliya eranchchan malatissiyaa Eeshshay de'ii? Qonccissite. 
2.	Bila xifatiyawu baasoy asaa giida; issi ammanttiya naqaashaa shiishshidi intte kifile laggetussi birshshidi yootite. 
3.	Bila xifatee tumatettaa, de'uwaanne puulaa maayidaba giyoogee woygiyoogaakkonne qonccissuwa shiishshite. 
4.	Xaafettidabi aybinne bila xifate gidana danddayenna. Ha qofaa kaafiya leemisuwa xaafi shiishshidi intte kifile laggetussi kifile giddon nabbabite. 
5.	“Medhdhi xaafidobatun xaafanchchay mal'etteesippe attin worddotenna” yaagiya qofaa intte guussan qonccissidi shiishshite. 
6.	Bila xifatiyaa Boolimaa/mucuraa naagabawu naa''u eranchchati immido yohoti dummatiyoonaayye malatettiyoonaa?  Awugee awugaara malatettii? Tobbite.
7.	Bila xifatiyaa intte aybissi aybissi nabbabiyaakko qonccissite. 
                           




   NAA"ANTTO SHEMPPUWA
2.	ODETTIDA/HAASAYETTIDA HAYYO XAAFO BILA
Shemppuwaa Sintta Qofata:
Ha shemppuwaappe simmin tamaareti kaalliyaa sintta qofata cuccumana: 
?	Haasayettida/xaafettida hayyo xaafo bila aybatettaa shaakkana. 
?	Haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaa garssan de'iya dummatettaa zuleyana. 
?	Haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaa eeshshata shaakkana. 
?	Haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaa qommotanne etawu de'iya maadota malaatana. 
?	Bantta asaa giddon de'iya dumma dumma haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilata shiishshana. 
?	Haasayan gidin xifatiyan haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaa go'ettana. 


















Ha shemppuwan bila xifatiya yara gidiya haasayettida/odettida hayyo xaafo bilaa timirttee shiiqiis. Ha sohuwaan Odettida hayyo xaafo bila giyagaanne haasayettida hayyo xaafo bila giyageeta laamiyaan go'ettana hegaa giyoogeekka Ingiliizettuwaa (Oral Literature) yaagiyaa qaalaa gishshatees giyoogaa.  Ha shemppuwaa garssan dumma dumma sima huuphe yohoti beetoosona. Hegeetu giddoppe haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaa aybatettay, haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaanne xaafettida hayyo xaafo bilaa bila xifatiya giddon de'iya dummatettay, haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaa eeshshati haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilawu de'iya maadoy hegaadankka haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaa macarata yaagiya ano yohoti denddoosona. 
Ha “bila xifatiyawu kanebata” yaagiya korssee bila xifatiya xaaxi waaxo akeekaa immana dandayissiyaaba gididi dumma dumma daashshatuwra eretissuwa oottiyaaba. Gido shin hegaappe aadhdhiyaagan issi issi bila xifatiya qommotun ciimma gidida laali besuwanne ootti besuwa polana danddayettenna. Haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaa yaagiyagaa ha korssiyan issi shempo xalaalan eretettikkonne kaalliya timirtte layttatun bana danddayidi issi korssedan shiiqiyoo gishshawu he wode assidi be'ana dandayettees. 

Gido shin ha shemppuwan haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaa xeelliyaagan xaaxi waaxo gidida qonccissuwaan aassennan eretettidi kaallidi de'iyaabata xeellana. Gidikkonne dumma dumma oosota  polanawu de'iyoo gishshatawu koshshiya keenaa giigettana bessees. 

Issi issi sima huuphe yohotu bollan qonccissoynne bessiya naqaashshatinne leemisoti shiiqiyo hanotati kaalloosona. Timirtetuppe kase shiiqiya denttetto oyshati, tobbe oyshatinne meezze oyshati kaalli kaallidi yoosona shemppuwa wurssettankka zaari oottiyo oyshatikka giigidosona. 
Yaaniyoo gishshawu tamaare naati kifile giddon polettiyaa tamaaruwaninne tamaarissuwan beegotti hashetiyaageeta gididi timirttiya cuccumaa demmana bessees. Kifile giddon shiiqiya meezzetanne dumma dumma oyshata ootiyoogeenne ootti bessiyoogeeti nu timirttiyaassi bayratettan shiiqiyaabata. Kifiiyan imettiya timirttiya heeran de'iya deriyaa giddon beettiya tumubatuura gattidi timiritiya minttiyoogeenne de'o immiyoogee ha shemppuwaassi bayrabanne huuphe gidiyaa yoho. 
2.1. Odettida /Haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaa  
Haasayettida/odettida hayyo xafo bilay hara asati xaafettibeenna bila xifatiya, dere asaa bila xifatiya, wogaa bila xifatiya, yaagidikka xeesiyoo xaafo bila. Hageetu bollan baaso gidiya sunttawu danddo qaalay haasayettiyaanne xaafettibeenna dere asaa buqura gidiyoogaa. Ha issi issi sunttatu giddon qofaa aahotettay woykko xunttatettay de'ana danddayikkonne ba go'an issuwa gididi Ingiliizetto doonan “Oral Literature” yaagiyaa qaalaa sohuwan gishshatana dandayiyaabappe attin etawu birshshettaa dummatetti baynnaagaa akeekana bessees. 
Asa na'i bari qofaa woykko bari oosuwaa pitaliyaa go'ettidi xaafiyoo hanotay mata wodiyaan beettidaba. Daro xeetu loyttatussi asay pitaliya medhdhidi xifatiya wogaa woykko seeraa kessidi go'ettennan de'iiddi daro adussa wodiya takkiis.

Gido shin kase wodiyaa asay xifate go'i doomettanaappe kase de'iya wodetun bari qofaa galla galla haniya hanotata, bari halchchuwa, wogaanne bari meezziya waati qonccissiiddi takkidee? 
Kaalliyaa yeletawu waatidi aattana/sheedhdhana danddayidee? Hagawu zaaroy keeni wayssiyaaba gidenna. Hegeekka asay doona go'ettidi haasayaaninne ootti bessiyooban qonccissiiddi, qassikka masettidi woykko oosettidi buquraaninne bariyoo de'iyaa ammanuwan bari yeletawu aattiddi takkissi yaagiyoogaa. Xifate meran gidennan doonaan odettiiddi oosettiiddi hegaadankka dumma dumma buquratun issuwappe issuwawu aadhdhiiddi yiida adussa wodiyawu meezzetettidaba giyoogaa. 
Ha kasenne adussa wodiya takkida bila xifatiya dere asaa oonatettaa qonccissiyaanne eta de'uwa dendduwa woykko doomettaa yootiya, banttawu de'iya xeelaa, bantta manttiyan de'iya wogaa qonccissiya banttawu de'iya issibaa pilgiyoonne haraassi bessiyo oge giyoogaa. Xaafettida bila xifatiya gidikkonne ayyo dendduwa gidiininne go'aa gidin I kiyidoynne shiiqiyoy ha ini dere asaassa gidiyoo gishshawu haasayettidanne xaafettida hayyo xaafo bilatu giddon dummatetti de'enna giyoogaa. Eta pulttoy woykko denddoynne eti naa''aykka issuwagidiyoogan hayyo xaafo bila giyoogaa. 
Hegaa gishshawu bila xifatee naa''awu shaahettees. giyoogaa: odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilanne xaafettida hayyo xaafo bila geetettees. Asa na'i bari de'uwaan, bari de'iyoo hanotata xeelliyaagan bariyyo siyettiyaabata, I akeekidobata woykko bana metidabaa  haraara haasayan laammidi shaakkiyoogan bari qofaa haraara laammees. Ha ogiyaan asa na'I bari oottana koyyidobaa oosuwan ootti bessees woykko polees. Asaa naati bantta heeraninne de'uwan haniyaabaanne de'iyaabaa bantta guuyguyan qoppidi dumma dumma ogiyan harawu aattoosona. Bantta issippe de'iyoo de'uwan bantta sooninne kareen go'ettiyoo dumma dumma miishshata medhdhoosona. Ha medhdhido miishshatanne banttawu de'iya ammanuwa go'etto sohuwara laali agiigokkona woykko xayssokkona. Eti bantta sintta yelettawu aadhdhana mala keehi mintti naagidi wottoosona woykko laatissoosona giyoogaa. Ha miishshati issi yeletaappe hara yeletawu aadhdhiyoy coo gidennan asay maaddiyaagaanne maaddennaagaa shaakki eridi anjjo gidiyabaanne qanggettidabaa shaakki akeekidi lo'uwaa iitaappe dummayidi pokko gidiyaabaa wogaappe shaakki kessi yeggiichchidi bantta ayyaanaama meezziyaanne haarettida miishshata oyqqidi kaalliyaa yeletawu sheedhdhiyoogaana. Ha ba wodiyaanikka sheerettida yeletay ba aawatuppenne ba aawaa aawatuppe ekkido wogaanne meezziya de'iyaagaadan ekkigiyooga gidennan qohiyaagaappe shaakkidi maaddiyaagaa xalaalaa maxi ekkidi qohiyaanne metiyaa meeziya xayssidi banttaa kayan medhdhi gujjidi etikki bantta naatuyyo aattoosona. Hegaa gishshassa odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilay dere asaanne aawatu eeshshanne laatanne anjjo geetettiyoogee. 

      2.2. Odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bila eeshshata 
Tobbiyoo oyshata: 
?	Odettida/haaseyettida hayyo xaafo bilay xaafettida hayyo xaafo bilaappe aybin 
   dummatii? 
?	Odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaa eeshshata giyoogeeti awugeetee? 
?	Odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bila eeshshatu giddoppe bayratiyaageeti  
    awugeetee?
?	Odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilay asaanaa de'uwa waati qonccissii? 

Odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaa uloppe be'anawunne eesuwan akeekana maadana mala xaafettida hayyo xaafo bilaara geeddarssi xeelliyoogee lo''o oge. Eti naa''aykka bila xifatiya macara gidiyoogaadaanikka eti malatettiyoo cora ogeti de'oosona. Gido shin qassikka eti dummatiyoo cora ogetikka de'oosona. 
Ha naa''u dumma bila xifatiya yarati malatettiyoonne dummatiyoo hanotata xeellanaappe kasettidi ane issi odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bila gidiya issi haysiyaa kaallidi xeelloos. 
                         Haysiyaa 
Hayseyiyoogaa: Haysee hanees. 
Ezgiyaagaa: Hanees.
Hayseyiyaagaa: Issi wode oyddu boorati bazzuwaan de'oosona.  
Ezggiyaagaa:  “Ero” 
Hayseyiyaagaa: Eta meray issuwaagee karetta; issuwaagee bulla; issuwaagee bootta; issuwaagee qassi zo'o. Oyddaykka zorettiiddi, “Issoy issuwaa naagana.” Yaagidi maacettidosona. Eti bantta maachchaa naagidi de'ishin eta maanawu, eta issippetettay wolqqaa diggido issi gaammoy de'iyaagee hagaadan yaagidi qoppiis. “Hay hegeeta waata shaakkada mooshsha?” yaagiis. Ba qoppidoogaadankka issi gallassi yiidi boorata, “Inttessi ubba galla meto ehiyaagee, ha bootta booraa; Intte giddon I baynnaakko intte saro de'ana shin, A gaasuwan intte qohetteeta.” Yaagidi cimmiis. Boorati hegaa siyido wode, “Tumakka” yaagidi he bootta booraa bantta giddoppe qaycidi yedettidosona. Yedettin barkka de'iyaagaa gaammoy oyqqidi mi aggiis. Bullay, karettaynne zo'o heezzatu xalaalay hebazzuwaan attidosona. Amarida wodiyaa de'iiddi, “Hay hageeta qassi waata shaakkada mooshsha?”  yaagidi qoppiis. Kaseegaadankka etakko yiidi, “Ta ishatoo, taassi ubba wode beettiyaageenne qassi taani inttena be'ana yiyoo wode inttena hirggissiyaagee ha bulla booraa. Intte giddon I baynnaakko, intte saro de'ana; shin A gaasuwan intte qohetteeta” yaagidi cimmiis. Boorati hegaa siyido wode, “Tumakka “yaagidi ha bulla booraa bantta giddoppe qaycidi yedettidosona. Yedettin barkka de'iyaagaa gaammoy oyqqidi mi aggiis. Karettaynne zo'oynne naa''atu xalaalay he bazzuwan attidosona. Eta uluwaa paacciichchidaagee amarida wodiyaa de'iiddi, “Hay hageeta waata shaakkada mooshsha?”  yaagidi qoppiis. Kaseegaadankka yiidi karetta booraa, “Ha zo'o booraa meray taassi haahuwan erettiyoo gishshawu, neeni A gaasuwan dagammoppa; nena gidikko, mittaa kuwan erettakka. I baynnaakko neeni saro de'ana; shin A gaasuwan qohettaasa.” Yaagidi cimmiis. Booray hegaa siyido wode, “Tumakka” yaagidi ba wurssetta laggiyaa, zo'o booraa, qaycidi yedettiis. Hegaappe guyyiyaan gaammoy daafurennan, dumma dumma de'iyaageeta oyqqi oyqqi miidi wurssi aggiis. 
Ekettidoy: Awa baqatoo yaagiyaa Wolaytta haysiyaa maxaafaappe

Meeziyaa
1.  Ha bolla haysiyaassee aattana koyyido bayra kiitay aybakko tobbite.
2.  Asa zoriyaa ekkiyoogee iitee lo'oo? Ha yohuwaan haasayite.
3. Ha haysiyaa giddon de'iyaa gaammuwaanne boorata aybaara/oonaara malatissana  
       danddayettiyaakko haasayidi kuuyite.
4. Ha haysiyaa kiitaara malatettiyaa hara haysiyaa koyyidi xaafi shiishshidi intte kifil    
         laggetussi nabbabite.
Ha bolla baggaara nu be'ido qantta haysee issippetettay asaawu gidin hara meretawu aykeena wolqqa gidiyaakko/maaddiyaakko bessiyaaba. I woni he boorati gaammuwaa zoriyaa chii giidi bantta issippetettan minnidaba gidiyaakko issoynne meetettokkona. Shin banttana qohiyaa zoriyaa shaakki erennan gaammuwaa zoree tuma malatin ekkidi meetetti wuridosona. Ha haysee coo beni wode hanidabaa nuuyyo aattiyoogaa xalaala gidennan hachchi nu de'uwaassi aattiyoo kiitaykka keehi gita.  Ane hagaappe kaallidi qassi odettida/haasayettida hayyo bila xifatiyaa eeshshatuppe amaridaageeta xeelloos:

1. Odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaa doomettay awudekko erettenna.
Cora naqaashati yootiyoogaadankka xifatee mata wode demettidaba gidiyoogee tuma. Shin odettida bila xifatiya eeshshay haasayaaranne oosuwaara oyqettidaba. Haasayay qassi ay wodenne awan doomettidaakko eranawu keehi waayissees. Ooni erii odettida hayyo bila xifatee asa na'i doonaa go''ettiyoogaa dommoosappe doommidi haasayettees gaana danddayettees. Shin hagee qassi xon''aa zaaro gididi hara oyshaa denttissennaba gidana danddayenna. Biitta bollan asa na'i doonaa go'ettidi haasayaa doommidoy awudee? Yaagiya hara oyshaa denttissees. Ha oyshaassi gamma gidiyaa tilla zaaroy keehi waayssiyaaba gidikkonne hagaa heeraana yaagidi zaarana danddayettees. Ha''i wodiya tekinooloojee gakkido pilggettan hara buqurata (miishshata) biitta giddoppe bookki kessidi eti takkido bariya/ layttaa erana danddayettees. Gidoppe attin dooni ayfiyaan beettenna, kushiyaanikka oyqettennaba qassikka bookettidi moogettiya buqura gidenna gishshatawu I awude go'an pee'idaakko erana danddayettibeenna. Yaaniyoo gishshawu doonaaninne haasayaa baggaara aadhdhiya hayyo bila xifatee awude doomettidee yaagiyaa oyshawu doonaa doomettay erettennaagaa gidaappe attin “I doomettido wodee hagaa gaanawu erettenna.” yaagiyaagee bessiyaa zaaro. Shin xifattida hayyo bila xifatee qassi taarikiyaanne wodiya qoodidi qatuwaarakka erettidi hiqqa wodiyaan hiqqa sohuwan doomettiis giidi wottana danddayettees. 

2. Odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaa aarettaa ogee oduwaana/haasayaana.
Ha qommo baggaara nu be'idoogaadankka odettida bila xifatetuppe issuwaa gidiyaa haysee ha sohuwaan xifate meran beettoppe attin I asaappe asawu aadhdhiyoo ogee doonaana. Oduwan woykko cenggurssan, haasayan, yettan, gereessan, koyzziyankka gidana danddayiyoo gishshawu odettida bila xifate geetettidi xeesettees. I qassikka durssan (bollaa qaattan), haarido miishshatun, daro wodiyassi issippe takkida meezziyan hegaadankka qassi ammanuwaanikka harawu aadhdhees woykko attees giyoogaa. 
Ane nuuyyo lo'o xombbe gidana mala odettida hayyo xaafo bilaa yara gidiya gereessaappe, zilaassaappe, gayruwaappe, qan''ishiyappenne leemiso haasayaappe leemisota kaallidi xeelloos.                           
Gereessaa
Issi izaawu shankkan woridi ufayssan uttidi laggee shiiqidaagaassi baagaanne ba zariyaa haydaa qonccissiyoo haqaa. 
    Issi qantta Leemisuwaa ane xeelloos: 
Laachoore Siime Dilinaa Diidimaxaa wallaccan
Waassida oluwa kooriyo Gaaggaabo Alggaaba giyo
Bulaa godaa gaaggiyoo Madalchchee worqqinaa Heeranno
Wodaajja giyo paannuwaa godaa ba kawuwaa Xoona
Qullidi sinaa walallan keexxiya Meegisonaa
Mentta daamawu nena oloolee!
           (Ekettidoogee: Manttaa Liissaano Wolddemaariyaamappe)
Meezziyaa
1.	Ane tamaaretoo haqommo gereessaa birshshettaa issippe tobbi simmidi intte asttamaariyaawu/asttamaareessinne kifile laggetussi denddi eqqidi pissiyaa tigite.
2.	Ane tamaareto inttekka hagaa mala gereessaa waattan waattan gididi xaafite. Inttena waayissiyaaba gidikko cima asaa oychchidi kaalliyaa kifiliyaassi ekkidi shiiqidi intte kifile laggeta gereeri sissi simmidi intte oosuwaa inttena tamaarissiyaagaassi/rissi sheedhdhite.
Zilaassaa
Zilaassay issi izaawi hayqqin A naati, A zaree, A dabboy shiiqidi I/A woridosaa, daalidosaa, gimidosaa, haarido paraa, issippe diccidanne worida laggiyaa qoodi qoodidi qarettiiddi/kayyottiiddi goobatettaanne minotettaa qonccissiyoo haqa macaratuppe issuwaa.

Ane kaallidi Manttaa Liisaanu Wolddemariyaamappe ekettida issi qantta zilaassaa akeekidi xeelloos.
Taawawu Gooceenaa goobawu! Dagoye Siimee
Patinaa gulbba Kambbaataa allenaa Kumaaloo
Cuggaa salgeedon worbbo Handdiisonaa paatiyaa

Maydda eessaappe uyayidda daashshiinawu shin 
Simi asa immada ba...
(Ekettidoy: Manttaa Liissaanu Wolddemaariyaamappe)

Meezziyaa
1.	Tamaareto ha qommo zilaassaa bollan inttiyoo qoncibeennabay de’ikko intte laggetuura tobbitenne inttena tamaarissiyaagaa/ro oychchite.
2.	Tamaareto ha qommo zilaassaa malaa hara naa''aa gidiyaagaa xaafana danddayeetii? Inttena waayissiyaaba gidikko cima asaa oychchidi kaalliyaa kifiletussi ekki shiiqidi zilaali sissi simmidi inttena tamaarissiyaagaassi/rissi sheedhdhite.
Ceequwaa
Gayroy issi asi bari minotaa gutaran gayriyoo haqa macara.
Leemisuwaa:
Amaado Arusee Hiiriitinaa
Hirggenna wozanaa godaa
Away diishin Eqqa Bizzan yelettidi
Aaway diishin wonchchooro woxaluwan shakkidi
Kawotan wonjjalaa kessiyaa tana
Duzzee Hiiriitinaa dada korimaadan
Demmosaara kanttiyaa Daamootee
Laa neeyyo asho maayidan waatti oonee?
(Ekettidoy: Manttaa Liissaanu Wolddemaariyaamappe)
                            
Meezziyaa
3.	Tamaare naatoo ha qommo ceequwaa loytti nabbabidetii? Ha ceeqoy obaa yootiyaaba malatii? Tobbidi kuuyite.
4.	Ane A malaa hara ceequwaa xaafana danddayeetii? Inttena waayissiyaaba gidikko eriyaa asaa oychchidi naa''aa gidiyaagaa kaalliyaa kifiletussi ekki shiiqidi inttena tamaarissiyaagaassi/rissi sheedhdhite.
3. Odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilay issuwaappe haraayyo qanttan 
        aadhdhiyaaba  
Yootiyaagawu ezggiyaagawukka guugge giddon oyqettidi gam''anawu injjetiyoy issi odettiyaabay qantta gidiyoo wodiyaana. Odettida hayyo bila xifatee issuwaappe harawu qantta wodiyaan aadhdhiyaaba. Xaafettida hayyo bila xifatiyaadan eridi wurssanawu cora gallassatussi, saaminttatussi, aginatussi takkokkona. Guuggiyaappekka xayirggokkona giyoogaa. Leemisuwaassi naachchay, qiree, xooringgee, gereessay, gayroy, ceeqoy, h.h.malatiyaabati qantta wodiyaan issuwaappe haraayyo aadhdhana danddayoosona.

Keehi adussa gidida bini wode hayseti woykko odoti de'ikkanne xaaxi – waaxiyoo wode odettida hayyo bila xifatee qanttan aadhdhiyaaba leemisuwassi qommo baggaara de'iya hayssiya nabbabidaba gidikko issi utettan nabbabi wurssi aggida. Keehi adussa wodiyakka ekkibeenna. I qantta gidiyoo gishshawu haraasi zaarettidi ha taarikiya yootanawu koyyiyaakko daro waayssenna woykko dogettirggenna giyoogaa. 
                                                       
4. Odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilay polettiyaaba/bollaa qaattaa oosuwan 
   beettiyaaba 
Odettida hayyo bila xifeetiyawu oosuwan beettiyoogee anoba. Issi odettida hayyo bila xifeetiya mucuray oosuwan beettiyoobatettaappe shaahettidi shiiqiyaakko awu ayba puulinne de'ana danddayenna. Aadhdhana mala koyettida kiitaakka aattenna aggana danddayees giyoogaa. Odettida hayyo bila xifatee poliyaagaa baggaara issi moottan /biittan/ woykko dubbushan shiiqi uttida asaa sinttan yootettiya, yexettiya woykko durssaadan oosettidi be'ettiyabappe attin xaafettida hayyo bila xifatiyadan woraqata looli uttidi issi asan nababetiyaba gidena. Hegaa gishshawu odettida hayyo bila xifatee shemppo/de'o demmiyoy galchchaa woykko yaa'ida asaa sinttan oosettidi polotiyoo wodiyaana. 

Odettida hayyo xaafo bilan qoncciya cora issi dere asaa giddon haniyaabati de'oosona. 
Leemisuwawu ekkikko: bullachcha keettan yexeettees, durettees, ufayttettees. Qasi asi hayqqido yeeho keettan zilaalettees, yeekettees, afuxxeettees, waasettees. Ha'i wode iita meezze gididi attiiddi attiiddi yiisippe attin kase wode gidikko agunttan stnttaa puuzi puuzidi yeekkeettees, tira bubuxeettees. Toorawu woykko olawu biiddi goobatettaassi gereerettees; ceeqqeettees. Shankkawukka biiddi gereeriyoogee ceeqqiyoogeekka de'ees. Qaxxarankka miyobay uyiyoobay giigees; anjjeettees. Qan''ishiya kaassay, oychchiyageenne zaariyaagee wogaa naagidi kaa'iyoogee, haysiya hayseyiyoogee hara eziggiyageetti kaalliyoogawu ubabawukka seeraynne wogay de'ees. Goynuwa sohuwa /woosa keettatukko biyoo wodiyan gidinkka asawu de'iya hulluuqoy, maayiyoo maayoy, eta sinttan beettiya eeshshay dumma. Gifaataa aginan Wolaytta asaa layttaa laammiyoo aginan ufayssan/Goda Yesus Kiristtoosa yeletaa wodiyan, Meechchaa/Epiphany baaliyaan Kirsttoosa Kaquwaa baaliyaan, A dendduwan h.h.m. dumma dumma baaletun de'iya kaassay ufayssay, qassikka kayyoy ubbaykka keehi malaaleesinne issuwa bonchchi simmiyoo wode haray amoyees. Ubbabaykka bari wogaanne seeraa kaallidi polettanawu dumma dumma meray de'ees giyoogaa. 

Leemisuwassi issi asi duranaayyo koyro bari cenggurssaa keessidi yexxees woykko hara yexxiya asi aara de'ana bessees. Ha duriya asi qassi bari bollaa qaattidi issi sohuwappe hara sohuwawu xeellanawu lo'iya ogiyaan yuuyyiees woykko guppiyoogee appe naagettees giyoogaa. 

5. Odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilay Dere asaa dureta
Odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilay dere asaa dureta ayyo keettaawi baawa. Leemisuwassi ane kaallidi de'iyaa guuliyaa yeettaa xeelloos. 
               Onakko onakkoy awa biidee? 
               Shaafan guuliya goochchees. 
               Guuggiyaa ankkoy dafees. 
               Anhay kariyaa naagees. 
               Shiyaa looliyan qachchees…
               					
               					

     Gifaataa baaliyan wosolluwaa wode naati yexxiyoo yettaa
            Ta kushee kuula kurchchuchchee
		Kuraachchee waassa denttettee….
		________________________________
		________________________________

Yaagiiddi bees. Hageetinne hara dumma dumma yettati Wolayttan ubbasan kataman gaxariyan Wanchchen, Bolooson, Hobbichchan, Dugunan Kinddon, Oofan yexettishin/geetettishin siyettees. Gido shin ha bolla yetta danttuwa guuliyassa yaagidi eta xaafanawu/medhdhdanawu/giigissanawu un''ttida asi, etawu keettaawa gidiyaay oonee? Ooninne de'enna. Hegaassa Odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilay dere asaa dureta ayyo keettaawi baawa yaagiyoy.

Ha qommo baggaara beettiyaa danttoti guuliya kaassaa wodenne wosolluwaa wode geetettiyaa/yexettiyaa yettata gidishin ooninne awudenne awaaninne go'ettishin be'eettees. Eta xaafiday oonee? etawu keetaawi oonee? yaagiya oyshi mule kahankka yeenna. Gaasoykka etawu keetaawi erettenna. Eta awan, ooni, awude go'ettidaakko eranaagee dandayettenna. Asay dumma dumma sohotun kaa'ishshin siyidoogaa guussaa doommi aggiis woykko issippe sididi yexxiis giyoogaa. Hegaa gishshasa ubaykka bari siyidoogaa bari manttiyan go'ettiyoogaa doommiin aakki aakki erettiyoogee. Eta ooni awude awan medhdhidaakko erettenna gishshataassa odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaayyo keettaawi dere asaa yaagiyooy. Hagaa hiqqakoy xaafiis; hegaa qassi haray medhdhis gookko etayyo pulttoykka keettaawi dere asaa. Hegaa gishshawu ay asinne ha odettida /haasayettida xaafo bilaa luxi eridi eta go'ettana danddayissiya hanotan go'ettikko oychchiyay baawa. 
Leemisuwawu issi yeehuwa sohuwan A soho gidenna ufayssaa yettaa yexxikko hankko kayyuwaan de'iyaa keettaa asay phalqqetta qofaa denttidi yoohuwa woykko palamaa kessana danddayees. Hegaayyo keettaawi dere asaa gidiyoo gishshawu deree bari miishshaa naageesinne issuwaa issuwaa suure maaran mankkan go'ettees giyoogaa. Gido shin xaafettida hayyo xaafo bilaa keetaawi he A koyro woraqataa bolli wottida xaafanchchaa. He xifatee xaafidaagaa miishsha giyoogaa. A medhdhidaageenne koyro xaafidaagee A gidiyoo gishshawu hara asi go'an peeshshennaadan higgiyaan teqqana danddayiyoo maatay de'ees. He keettaawaassi A oosuwa haray ekkidi babaa oottennaadan A maatay naagettidaagaa. He xaafanchchaa shenee baynnan darissiyoogee, ekkidi harabaa xaafiyoogee woykko corayiyoogee higgiyan oyshissees. Shin odettida hayyo xaafo bilawu  I xaafiis yaagiyo keettaawi baawa. I dere asaa dureta /miishsha giyoogaa. A ooninne awaaninne awudenne go'ettana danddayees. Oychchiyaayikka de'enna. A go'ettennaadan diggana danddayiyaa asi de'enna. Qommo baggaara nuuni be'ido guuliyaa yettaynne wosolluwaa kaassay obakkonne erettenna. Ha danttuwa kaassaa siyida/ erida asi awanne biidi go'ettin diggiyay de'enna. 

AQan''ishiya kaassaa
Qan''ishee odettida bila xifate yara gidiyaabatuppe issuwa. Qan''ishiyaa kaassay naa''u asaa/citaa giddon polettiyaa keehi lo'iyaa kaassa qommo. Qan''ishiyaa kaassaa giddon keehi baceessiyaa/cashshadan haniyaa zaarotikka de'oosona. Gido shin hegan yiilloy/lanccee/ooshshi baa aybissi giikko I kaa'iyaageeti maayettidinne dosidi kaa'iyoo kaassa. Ha kaassan koyro oyhchiyaagee “Nena qan''ishe” giyoo wode naa''anttoy/zaariyaagee “qayshe” yaagees. Zaariyaagee eriyaaba gidikko zaaruwa yootiidi xoonees. Shin zaaruwaa erenna ixxikko “mokkaas/mokkis” yaagidi oychchidaagaappe zaaruwaa siyees giyoogaa.
Leemisota:
Lm. 1: Arkka: Maaraa nena qan''ishe.
	Maara: Qayshe, Arkkaa.
	Arkka: Maqi mitta gaada shibba.
	Maara: Mokkaas.
	Arkka: Maahe aada gaada qaachcha.
Lm. 2. Maatafo: Imotaa, nena qan''ishe.
	Imota: Qayshe 
	Maatafo: dembbaa dereqqa 
	Imota: Mokkis 
Maatafo: deelliyaa borkkota.
Lm. 3. Ajjuuto: Nena qan''ishe
	Ciishsha: Qayshe
Ajjuuto: Saluwaa baanawu paraa koora
Ciishsha: Mokaas
Ajjuuto: Niyaayiyoo maanawu santtaa loolla.
Lm. 4. Dalggito: Bii Yallisee nena qan''ishe 
Yalliso: Qayshe Dalggitee; tana danddayana gaada kaa'ay?
Dalggito: Ashoy yiyoode miicca
Yalliso: Acoy yiyoode yeekka.
Cita ooso
1. Qan''ishiya kaassaa hagaappe kase kaa'i ereetii? Oonaara, awan?
2. Waattan waattan gididi leemiso gidiyaa intte hagaappe kase eriyoo qan''isheta ichchashu 
       daqiiqawu kaa'ite. 
3. Wolaytta giddon kaa'ettiyaa daro sha'an qoodettiyaa dumma dumma qan''ishetuppe issi 30ppe 
          guuxxennaageeta xaafi ekki ehiidi intte asttamaariyaassi/asttamaareessi sheedhdhite.
                          Leemiso Haasayaaa
Leemiso haasayati asay haasayiiddi bari haasayaa kaafiyaa woykko bishshiyaa woykko qanttan kuuyyiyaa maado gidiyaa haasayata woykko guussata. Ane Leemiso haasayatuppe issi guuttata xeelloos:
Leemisuwaa:
1.	Kattay baynnay kana, kahoy baynnay kayso.
2.	Hadee baynnawu hanqqoy baa.
3.	Amanettido mashshay tiriyaan me'ees.
4.	Bawu qaxxara gellennay, asa ayfe oyqqees.
5.	Deeshshay ba liiqo inxxarssan ohaa mees.
6.	Killiyan xaamatida beexee olomuwaan meqqees.
7.	Inxxarssaa liiqoy carshshaa kanttees.
Meezziyaa
1.	Ane tamaare naatoo ha qommoora de'iyaa leemiso haasayata ay mala haasayaa giddon go'ettiyaakko qonccissite.
3.	Inttekka ane qoodan laatamanne ichchashaa gakkiyaa dumma dumma leemiso haasayata kaalliyaa saamminttawu xaafi shiishshidi intte asttamaareessi/yassi sheedhdhite.

 6. Odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaayyo laammettiyoo hanotay de'ees. 
Odettida hayyo bila xifatiyawu laamettiyoo hanotay de'ees giyo wode issi hayttan siyettidabaa woykko ayfiyan be'ettidabaa woykko guuggiyan oyqettidabaa simmidi harawu yootiyo/aattiyo hanotay de'iyo gishshawu koyro bari siyido qaalaata issuwa issuwa hassayidi gaana danddayettenna gishshawu harawu shiishshiiddi qaalataa laammiyoonne bari qaalata go'ettidi yoottiyo hanotay de'ees. Hegaassa odettida hayyo bila xifateeiyassi laamettiyoo hanotay de'ees giyogee. 

Issi leemisuwa ekkiyaba gidikko issi haysiyaa issi asi ezggidi siyidoogaappe guyyiyaan koyro assi yootida asi yootidoogaadan gidennan qaalata dummayidi yootiyoogee attenna. Issi asi bari siyidi yootiyo qaalaa koyro siyidoogaappe ay dummatikkonne laamettana koshshenna issibay ha haysee oyqqido woykko aattana bessiyoo kane qofaa woykko cuccumaa. 
         7. Odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilay issi sohuwaappe hara sohuwaa gakkiyo                                  
              hanotay laafa. 

Odettida/haasayettida hayyo bila xifatee issuwappe harawu aadhdhiyooy issi siyida/ be'ida asi hemetti hara sohuwa biidi harawu yoottiina woykko bessiina. He asi ha bila xifatiya harawu aattanawu issi asi de'iyoo sohuwa gakkanawu biidi haraa ayfiya be'iiddi 
yootees/bessees. Xaafettida hayyo bila xifatiya gidiyaakko issi kuttan daro sha'u koppiyaan issitoo daroogaappe simmiin dumma dumma sohuwaa keehi qontta wodiyaan gakkees. Mexi issi gallassan daro sohotuuninne cora asaa kushiyaan gelissanaagee keehi laafaba. Leemisuwawu “Ethiopian Herald” woykko “Addis Zemen” woykko hara hara xaafetti giigiyaageeti hachchidan cora payduwaan darissikko wontto malan toophphiyaan de'yaa ubba dalgga manttetussika gakkoosona. Odettida hayyo bila xifatee hagaappe keehi dummatiyogee I assi asaara ayfiyan gayttennan ixxikko issi asappe harawu aadhdhiyoo qaadi de'enna. Hegaa giishshin ha''i wodiya tekinoolooje gidida eraaadooniyaanne televizhiniyaan aadhdhiyageeta xaaxi waaxenna giyoogaa. Hegaa gishshassa odettida hayyo bila xifatee xaafettida hayyo bila xifatiyaadan haraakko eesuwan gakkenna giyoogee.  
                                            
8. Odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilay cita ooso
Odettida hayyo bila xifatee cita ooso giishin issi odettida hayyo bila xifatiya harawu aattanawu baa giishin issi odiyaa asanne issi ezggiyaa asa woykko issi poliyaanne issi be'iyaa asa keshshees giyoogaa. Issi asi ba barkka yootananne ezggana woykko xeellana danddayenna. Leemisuwaassi yettaa ekkikko, yexxiya asi woykko duriyaa asi asi baynnasan coo yexxenna woykko durenna. Hara ezggiya asi woykko xeelliyaa asi woykko kushiyaa baqqiya asi de'ana bessees. Hegaa gidana xayikko melasan issi asi yexxees gaana dandayettenna aybissi giikko koyettiyaabay kumibeenna giyoogaa. Ha ubba asay shiiqidi issippe gididi poliina assi puuli de'iyooy. Hegaassa odettida bila xifatee cita ooso issi asi hara asaara gididi poliyoobappe attin ba barkki polana danddayennaba giyooy. 

   9. Odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilay hayqqennaba 
Odettida hayyo xaafo bilay hayqqennaba gidiyoo gaasoy asa na'i ha alamiyaa bollan de'ishn doona go'ettiyoogee/haasayiyoogee woykko issoy issuwara haasayan gayttiyoogee attennaba. Asay ha alamiyaa bolli doona go'ettiiddi de'aappe sinttan ha bili xayiyaaba gidenna. Odettida hayyo xaafo bilaa xayooynne hayqoy asa na'aa dooni salo sa'a guffanttoppe xayiyoogaara oyqetti uttidaba. Asa na'i biitta bollappe xayana yaagiyoobi qassi qofettennaba. Issi yeletay hayqqiyo wode hara yeletay kaallees woykko hara yeletay tohettees. Hayqqiyagaappe ooratta yeletay laattees. Issuwaappe issuwawu sheerettiyoo hanotay qanxxettenna. Hegaa gishshawu odettida hayyo xaafo bilay hayqqennaba giyoogaa.
 
10. Odettida/haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilay wudiyooy aadhdhidanne ha''i wodiyaana 
Odettida hayyo xaafo bilay aadhdhida wodiyaaninne ha''I wodiyaan wudees. Issi hayssiya  leemisotto ekkidi xeelliko doommiiddi “Beni wode issi qaariyaanne issi gaamoy ………….” Yaagidi doommees. Awude? Beni wode. Daro wode hayseti doommiiddi beni wode, Beni issi galla, beni Amaadon, h.h.m. yaagettidi doomettoosona aybissi giikko eta 
aadhdhida kase wodiyaabaa minttiyoo gishawu. He haysee odetti makkinnikka wurssettan hagaadan haniis giida woykko yaanidosona geetettees. Ha haysee /hanotay hachchi haniiddi de'iyaabanne wontto/sinttanawu polettana de'iyaabee? Gidenna. Aadhdhida wodiya baaso oottidi denddees giyoogaa. Polettidabay kase wodiyan hani aadhdhiichchidoogan aadhdhida wodiya bessees giyoogaa. 

A Taarikee beni wodiyaa baaso ottidi denddiyaaba gidikkonne ha''i woykko hachchi ezggiyaa asawu yootettees. Beni wode de'ida asaa de'uwa hanotay ha''i ezggiiddi de'iyaagawu aadhdhees. Hachchin gididi ezggiyaagee aadhdhida hanotaappe kase dere asaa de'uwaappe cuccumaa/ tumubaa/ bari de'uwa maaddana danddayiyaabaa, era gidiyaabaa demmees giyoogaa. Hachchin de'iyaa banatettaa, dere asaa hanotaa kase wodiya hanotaara yiggi xeellees. Iitanne lo'o woykko maaddiyaanne maaddennabaa paacci kanttees. Hegaassa odettida/haasayettida xaafo bilay aadhdhida wodiyaninne ha''i wodiyan wudees giyoogee.              
                     



               Meezziya 
1.	 Issi intte eriyoo hayssiya ekkidi odettida hayyo xaafo bilay aadhdhida wodiyaaninne ha''i   
      wodiyaan waani baasettidaakkonne sinttanaa wodiyaara waani gayttennaakko 
      birshshidi zuleyite. 



2.	 Odettida hayyo xaafo bilay laamerettiyoo eeshshaa intte eriyoo issi leemisuwa       
    immiyoogan bessite.  
3.	Haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilay asanaa de'uwa maaraara wokko oonatettaara aybissi gayttii? Qonccissite. 
4.	Darosan ha''i wodiyan xuufiyan xaafettidi dumma dumma sohuwawu aakki aakki biiddi de'iyaa odettida hayyo xaafo bilati xaafettida hayyo xaafo bilaara qoodettiyoonaayye odettida hayyo xaafo bilaara paydettiyoonaa?  Oyddaa oyddaa gididi citan tobbidi xaafidi shiishshite. 
5.	Ha''i wodiya tekinooloojjiyan leemisuwawu eraadooniyaninne televizhiniyan aadhdhiya odettida hayyo xaafo bilati issisaappe harasaa aadhdhiyoo hanotay laafa giya qofaara maayettay? aybissi? Birshshada yoota. 
6.	Odettida hayyo xaafo bilay cita ooso gidiyoogaa dumma dumma odettiyaa bila xifatiya qommota ootti bessiyoogan eta seeraa citan gididi kifile giddon ootti bessite. Intte ekkiyoo leemisoy aybanne gidana danddayees. Lemisuwawu, yettaa, hayssiya kaassaa, hoolliyaa yetta h.h.m. Hayyanintta denddi eqqidi ootti bessanawu guyye gooppite/yeellatoppite.
7.	Issi dooni yelettees. Dicceesinne hayqqees. Hara baggaara qassi odettida hayyo xaafo bilay hayqqenna geettees. Ha na''u phalqqetta qofata waatada sigettuutee? birshshettaa zuliyaa shiishsha. 
10.	Odettida hayyo xaafo bila yarati issuwaappe harawu laatettiyoo (aadhdhiyoo) ogeta 
 Hagaappe xadeera odettida hayyo xaafo bilaa laatati aawaappe naatukko qassikka naatu naatukko odo xalaalan gidennan hara meraaninne ogiyaan aadhdhi laatettiyoogaa gidiyoogaa be'ana. Hegaadaanikka issi issi aadhdhiyoo meraa giddon xaaxi waaxettiyaabatakka kuuyyana. Ane odettida hayyo xaafo bilati yeletaappe hara yeletawu aadhdhiyoo ogetanne eta hanotaa meran meran shaakkidi be'oos. 
       A. Buqura meran aadhdhiyoo hanotaa
Buqura meran aadhdhiyaabati kase aawati yootiyoogan woykko yexxiyoogan woykko haasayidi akeekissiyoogan aadhdhiyaageeta xaaxi waaxenna. I xaaxi waaxiyooy miishsha meran leemisuwaassi issi heeraa asay bari eraa go'ettidi bari kushiyaan urqqaappe, mittaappe, birataappe harabaappekka medhdhi kessi go'ettiyoobata. Hagaa mala dumma dumma buqurati asay benippe doommidi bari kushiyan massi molidi, qoxxi kessidi go'ettiiddi takkido era oosota. 
 tooray, gonddallee, cachcha zayyee, dinkkee, karaabee, diittay, bulee, gosee, arggubbee,                                                
hachchi yeletay qassi wogaa miishshata giidi bari soon maaran mankkan qaqqi wottiyoo alleeqo miishsha.





Misilya 1        Buqura meran aadhdhiyaa wogaa 





  

                                                                                                 


 Wolaytta keettaa
      Karaabiyaa, diittaa, pulaaliyaa, cachcha zayyiyaa, uldduuduwaa

                                 Gonddalliyaa                                             Marccuwaa



                             
 Urqqaappe merettiyaabata quuliyaa, sheetaa h.h.m                                       
      



                                                     
 
                                                    




 Tooraa


Ha qommo bagaara nuuni be'iyoo miishshati karaabee, gonddallee, tooray, uldduudoy, kadoynne qambbaray, dinkkee,h.h.m hara cora miishshati eta misilee hagaappe qommo baggaara beettiyoogeetinne harati hadiya dunguzay, ayllee, xikkee, bullukkoy, kutay, hayttan wottiyoo belecay, siiriyaan wottiyoo dundday, beni wode asay zal''iyaawu go'ettido marccoy, kushiyaan wottiyoo sagaayoy, biraadhdhiyaan wottiyoo migidoy, huuphiyaan qachchiyoo bawunddee, qassikka dumma dumma ushshati parssoy, m

aattay shochchay, yeesoy, yeelehchchay, yeelettay dinddoy, essay, woga kattati, itimaappe giigiyaagee m

uchchoy, unccaappe giigiyaagee baacciyay, banggaa buraatoy, daatta bambariyaara miyoogee qayye ashoy, waxayay, gugoy, qoociqoocoy, hegaadankka shukkaaree, gaalla donoy, boyyee, boynay, sawo bambbaree h.h.m.  cora yootin wurenna hara asay dumma dumma sohuwappe yiidi be'in alenna hara corabatikka de'oosona. 
             B. Maabaraa Meezziya (folk custom) 
Ingiliizettuwaan folk custom qassi nu doonan maabaraa meezze giyoogee kase aawati banttawu mintti oyqqidi de'iiddi yeletawu aattiido ayyaanamanne ayyaanaama gidenna ammanoti meezeti wogatinne goynoti xaaxi waaxettiyoobata. 
Woogay goynnoy, sabay, xoomay, ufayssay, hayqoy, denddoy, haattaa meechchay, gifaatay, eeqay, bitay, murunnoy, qaallichchay h.h.m meezzeti buqura giddidi beettiyoo merata. Hageeta malatiya goynobanne goynoba gidenna ammanotinne goynoti dere asaa giddon aakkidi de'oosona. Hageetu malati asaa meezziyaadan issuwappe hara yeletawu aadhdhiyaaba. 

            C. Durssa qaattaa/ootti beesiyo qaatta (Artistic dance) 
Durssaa qaattan xaaxi  waaxettiyaageeti woga yettata, durssatanne bollaa qaattata. Hagaadan dumma dumma dere asaa giddoonikka dumma dumma muuzunqqati dalggidi beettoosona. Durssa qaatta giyoogeetippe issoy issoy issi dere asay bari wogaa yettaa giddon oottiyoo durssay A eray de'iyoogaa bessanaassa. Leemisuwassi viiduwan duuqetti uttida duumma dumma dere asaa durssaa woykko maayyuwa maayyiyoo hanota be'idi hagee wolayttattuwa, hagee Haddiyyattuwaa, hagee Sidaamattuwa, Hagee Oroomottuwaa, hagee Geediyottuwa, hagee Guraagettuwa yaagidi shaakki erana danddayettees.
Misiliyaa 2
Durssaa qaattaa (ootti bessiyoo) era leemisota

                                         Nu mayzza durssa bilaa
Haray atto shin yettaa cenggurssaa siyennan, yexettiyaa doonaakka erennan issi dere asaa maayuwaa hanotaa be'idi hagee hiqqa biittaagaa/ asaagaa gaana danddayettees. Woga yettay hachchi merettidaba gidennen benippe doommidi de'iyaaba. Issoy issuwaappe bee'iiddi  eraa ekkiiddi bari wogaa durssaa loyttidi dumma ogiyan liiqees giyoogaa. Onanne “dendda issi biittaa wogaa durssaa dura” giikko issi asawu hagee waayissiyaaba, Aybissi giikko dumma dumma dere asawu dumma gididi harawu wayissiya durssa og'eti /hiillati de'oosona. Issuwawu issuwawu A eray A eray de'ees. He issuwawu issuwawu A eray boynna asi co'u giidi durana danddayenna. Hegaa gishshassa eti ootti bessiyoo era qaatta geetettidoy. 
                  Meezziya issuwaa (Buzo ooso) 
1.	 Odettida hayyo xaafo bilay asaa na'aa duussawu ay mala era immana danddayii?  
      Leemisuwan zemppissada ne zaaruwa qonccissa. 
2.	 Odettida hayyo bila xifatee cenggurssaappe kareera hara ay ogiyan aadhdhana                          
      danddayii? Eta zuleyada birshshettaa imma. 
3.	 Odettida hayyo xaafo bilay adussan aattiyoogawu ayba qohoy /iitatetti de'ii? Hayyannaa  
       qonccissada shiishsha. 
4.	 Intte heeran oosettiya bullachchaa, qaxxaraa, yeehuwa, oosuwa h.h.m hanotatuura  
      gayttiya oosuwa denddo oottada I waani polettiyaakko qonccissa.                                                            
5.	 Odettida hayyo xaafo bilaynne doonaa doomettay woykko meretay ay mala ogiyan 
       gayttana danddayiyoonaa? Birshshada yoota. 

























HEEZANTTO SHEMPPUWAA
3. XAAFETTIDA HAYYO XAAFO BILAA   
Ha shemppuwaa sintta qofata:  Ha shemppuwaa tamaaridi wurssidoogaappe 
simmin tamaareti: 
?	Xaafettida hayyo xaafo bilay aybakko A birshshettaa yootana 
?	Xaafettida hayyo xaafo bilaa macarata shaakkidi zuleyana
?	Danttuwaaninne yeda xifatiyaa giddon de'iyaa dummatettaa yootana
?	Danttuwaanne yeda xifatiyaa eeshshata birshshidi qonccissana 
?	Medhdhi xaafuwaanne chii-medhdhi xaafuwa dummatettaa yootana
?	Medhdhi xaafoy bari giddon oyqqiyoobata shaakki eridi eta meran meran shaakkana
?	Xaafiyoo hiillata akeekidoogaappe guyyiyaan dumma dumma xifateta ekkidi paaccana woykko bori nashshana
?	Dumma dumma dantotanne yeda dirssateta/ xuufeta xaafana.









Hagaappe guyyeera de'iyaa sohuwaan odettida hayyo xaafo bilanne xaafettida hayyo xaafo bila geetettidi naa''awu shaahettiyoogaa be'idi kanttida. Odettiyaa  hayyo xaafo bilaa aybatettaanne A eeshshatakka aahuwan wudidi xeellida. Ha''i kaallidi xaafettida hayyo xaafo bilaa loyttidi xeellana.  Ha xaafettida hayyo xaafo bilay bariyyo qassi naa''awu shaahettees. Hegeetikka medhdhi xaafuwaanne chii-medhdhi xaafuwaa geetettoosona. Etikka bantta giddon dumma dumma cora meraanne macarata oyqqoosona. Kaallidi de'iyaa qonccissuwa ane xeelloos. 

                                                                  Bila Xifatiyaa

             Xaafettida hayyo xaafo bilaa                Odettida hayyo xaafo bilaa
                     

     Medhdhi                             Chii-medhdhi
     xaafuwaa                              xaafuwaa

Xaafettida hayyo xaafo bilay danttuwan woykko yeda xifate meran xaafettidi beettiyaa era ooso. Xaafetti uttida woykko xifate meran beettiyaa ay xifateenne bila xifate geetettana danddayees gaana daanddayokko. Aybissi giikko bila xifate giyoogee issi halchchuwan ohettida allaalliyaa hoolliyaa gattanawu xifatiyaa seeraa, wogaa, meraa naagidi qoncce gidida qaalatun uttida bari giddon asaa de'uwan polettana danddayiyoo meran shiiqidaagaa. Bantta shiiquwaanikka naa''awu shaahettoosona. Issoynnee koyrroy issi de'iyaabaa, geetettidabaa qoncciyaan be'ettidi ammanettana danddayiiyaabaa, gujoy baynnabaa, mal''ettennan de'iyaa tumaa beessiyoogaa. Qassi naa''anttoy de'iyaa tumatettaa gujji mal''ettidi medhdhidoogaa. Woykko baynnabaa de'issidi gujjidi shiishshidoogaa. 

Issi hanida tumatettaa ayba wotoynne gujoy baynna walaha giyoobi gelennan I hanidooriden woykko polettidooriden shiishshiyaagee chii-mmedhdhi xaafuwaa giyoo bila xifatiyaa yara. 
Chii medhdhi xaafoy tuma gididabaa xalaalaa xaafi oyqqees. Hegaa giyoogee seeri, maari, mankki baynna, nabbabiyaa asa salettiyaa mal'enna xifate giyoogaa gidenna. Ciimma qofaa oyqqidanne nabbabiyaa asa hulluuquwaa haaridi wozanappe nabbabanaadan oottiyaa puulay de'iyooba. I issi allaaliyaa aattiyoo wode dendduwaappe/doomettaappe biidi poluwaa gakkanawu I kaalliyoo A shiishshuwaa ogee /hiillay de'iyoonne xifatiyaa wogaanne maaraa kaalliyaaba. I keehi puulatti xaafettidi asa wozanan geliyoo hanotay de'ees giyoogaa. 

Chii-medhdhi xaafoy gujoy, wotoy, worddoy baynnan yohota leemisuwaassi asaa na'aa hanotaa, asaa naa pilggettaa hanotaa, heeraa moottaabaa, tumatetaa xaafidi shiishshees. Timirttiyaawabati, gaazeexaabati, dumma dumma eraa aattiyaa xifateti, issi asaa de'o taariketi, issi biittan dichchaa hanotati, biittatu wogati, issi biittaa utettaa hanotatu birshshettati, pilggetta ooso ayfeti, dumma dumma asaappe shiishshi oyqqiyoo odoti, wogatinne, maarati, eraadoniyaan, televizhiiniyaan, interneetiyaninne dumma dumma hara ogetun aadhdhiya asaa giddon polettida odoti, ayissuwaa/haaruwaabaa, deretettaabaanne Ikkonoomiyaa hanotatura gayttida dumma dumma birshshettata hegaanne hegeeta malatiyaabati chii-medhdhi xaafuwaa giddon xaxii waaxettiyaabata. 
Hara baggaara qassi xeellikko medhdhi- xaafoy asi bari kahaappe pulttissidi xaafiyoobappe atin I tumu hanettidaba woykko polettidaba gidenna. I issi polettibeennabaa woykko hanibeennabaa malatissidi, xaafanchchay barippe medhdhi gujjidi, asa de'on polettana danddayees giyoobata tumatettaappe keehi haassennan malatissidi baynnasaappe bari kahan medhdhi kessidi xaafi shiishshiyooba. 
                                                                  
I hanibeennanne beettibeenna medhdho ooso woykko worddo ooso giyoogaa. Ane kaallidi medhdhi-xaafuwaninne chii-medhdhi xaafuwan de'iyaa dummatettata xeelloos. 

Medhdhi-xaafuwaanne hii medhdhi xaafuwaa dummatettaa bessiyaa zaraa

Chii-medhdhi xaafuwaa	Medhdhi-xaafuwaa
-Tumu hanidaba woykko polettidaba	- Tumu hanidaba gidenna woykko 
  hanibeenna, polettibeenna, 
- Gujoy woykko wotoy de'enna 	- Daro gujoy woykko wotoy de'ees. 
- Xaafanchchay bari be'idobaappe 
  siyidobaappe xaafees. 	- Xaafanchchaa guugge xalaalaappe 
  pulttees. 
- Giddon woxxi qaaxxiyaabati 
  (eeshshaawati) bollan tumu de'iyaa woykko  beettiyaa asata.	- Eeshshaawati xaafiyaagaa 
 guuggiyan merettidaba, Tumu biitta 
 bollan de'iyaa asa gidokkona. 


Ha pude zaran de'iyaa chii-medhdhi xaafuwanne medhdhi-xaafuwa dummatettata be'ida. Medhdhi xaafuwan tumatetti de'enna woykko medhdhi xaafoy worddo yaagiyaa asaykka de'ana danddayees. Gidoppe attin medhdhi xaafoykka baaso oottidi denddiyooy issi dere asaa giddon hanana woykko polettana danddayiyaa tumatettaa. He issi dere asaa giddon hanana polettana danddayiyaa tumubaa bolli gujjidi, wottidi, mal''ettidi wordduwaakka walakkidi xaafiyaagee bari aattanawu halchchido kiitaa woykko qofaa aattees giyoogaa. 
Medhdhi xaafuwaa dirssatiyaa giddon cora bila xifatiyaa macarati woykko merati de'oosona.  Hegeetu giddoppe danttoy, adussanne qantta medhdhi- xaafoti, kaassati hegeetinne hegeeta malatiyaabati de'oosona. 



                     Meezziyaa Issuwaa 
1/ Issi xifatiyaa nabbabidi medhdni xaafo woykko chii-medhdhi xaafo gidiyoogaa shaakki erana 
    danddayettii? 
2. Medhdhi xaafuwaa xaafanchchatinne chii-medhdhi xaafuwaa xaafanchchay dummatiyoo 
     eeshshati de'iyonaa? Intte zaaroy “ee” gidikko waanidi? “Chii” gidikkokka waanidi?
3. Chii-medhdhi xaafuwaappenne medhdhi xaafuwaappe nabbabiyaa asassi go'a immiyaagee 
    Awugee? Intte zaaruwaa ammanttiyaa naqaashan amppissidi shiishshite. Citan gididikka 
     tobbite. 
4. Shemppuwaa naa''an odettida hayyo xaafo bilaa eeshshata geetettiyaageeta be'ida. Ha 
    eeshshata ekkidi xaafettida hayyo xaafo bilaa eeshshaara gatti xeellidi eti tumukka 
     dummatiyaa dummatennaa shaakkidi erite. 
5. Dirssatee bari shiishuwan dantto meran woykko yeda xifatiyaa meran aadhdhees. Danttonne 
   yeda-xifate geetettiyaageeti bantta meran ay mala hanotay de'iyoogeetee? Issi yeechchappe 
   darenna leemisuwaa xaafi ekki yiidi ha qofaa qonccissite. Hayyanaa asttamaariyaanttoo/renttoo 
   tamaaretu oosuwaa wudidi xeellite.
           












OYDDANTTO SHEMPPUWAA 
4. DANTTUWAA
  4.1. Danttuwaa 
Ha shemppuwaa sintta qofata: 
Ha timirttiyaa wurssettaappe simmin tamaareti: 
?	Danttuwa aybatettaa shaakkidi erana. 
?	Danttuwaaninne yeda xifatiyaa giddon de'iyaa dummatettaa yootana. 
?	Danttuwassi de'iyaa dumma eeshshaa zuleyana. 
?	Dumma dumma danttota nabbabidi birshshattaa immana. 
?	Bantta doorido huuphe yohuwaa bolli dumma dumma danttota xaafana. 













Ha shemppuwa garssan dantto giyoobi aybakkonne ayyo imettida dumma dumma birshshettata danttoy yeda xifatiyaappe aybin aybin dummatiyaakko issi issi huuphe yohota, danttuwaa eehshshatanne I shiiqiyoo ogeta hegaadanikka dumma dumma dantto qommota be'ana. 
Ha timirttiyaa shiishoy kane gididabatuura eretissiyoo woykko xaaxi waaxo qofata immiyoo hanotappe attin issi issi suuppa qaalata giddo gelidi xeelliyoo hanota gidenna. Aybissi giikko kaalliyaa timirtte layttatun ha yohotun aahuwan intte loohettana de'iyoo gishshassa. Hegee gakkanawu intteyyo hagee muleera ooratta gidenna mala geetettidi gelodan maaddanawu shiiqiis. 
Ha shemppuwan huuphe yohotussi bessiyaa birshshetati, qonccissoti dumma dumma meezze (kifile giddo) oosotun amppettidi oosettoosona. Danttuwaa nabbabidi akeekisiyoogee, xaafettida danttuwaa birshshidi yootiyoogee, buzo xaafidi shiishshiyoogee, Ubbay polettana de'iyaa allaalle. Hegaa gishshawu ha timirttiyaa akeekanawu beegottidi kaalliyoogaa koshshees. Ootti bessiyoo hiillata meezzetiyoo hanotaykka de'iyoo gishshawu giigettana bessees giyoogaa. 
Simi qommo baggaara be'an kajjeelidoogaadan danttoy de'uwaabaanne meretaabaa xaaxi waaxidi keehi qantta, siqqinttanne siitettida qaalatun qonccissiyo haasayanne xaafo bila. Danttoy aattana qoppido huuphe yohuwa ma''ettidinne mucuridi shiishshiyoo oge. I mucurettidi haasayettiyaagaa woykko nabbabettiyaagaa gidiyo gishshawu yettaaranne durssaara bees. Danttoy nashshana koyyidoba nashshanawu, toochchanawu/ keewushshanawu koyyidobaa too chchanawu/ wozanaa miidabaa qonccissidi qaretissiya ogiyan shiishshanawu go'iyaa era/bila ooso. 
Danttuwan yafaraa /yafaranxxuwa giyoogee issi maaran wodhdhidi keettaa shociyaa pitaliya (cenggurssaa) gakkanawu de'iyaagaa oyqqees. 
   Leemisuwaa:          Issoy issuwa siiqoos 
                          Kaaloy bayraa bonchchoos.
Had anttuwa giddon naa''u yafarati /yafaranxxoti de'oosona. Issi issi yafaraa wurssettan de'iyaa cenggurssay keettaa geetettees. Issi yafaray keettaa shocciis giyoy he yafaray injjetidi baappe pude baggaara woykko duge baggaara de'iya cenggurssaara (pitaliyaara) issi mala gidiyoo wodiyaana. Ane kaallidi issi keetta laaliyaa yafaranxxotu leemisuwa xeelloos. 
Leemisuwaa:
          Asaa na'aa ubbaa morkkee 
          Hiyyeesatettay nu giddoppe haakko. 
Ha bolla danttuwan de'iyaa naa''u yafaranxxoti keettaa laalidosona. Aybissi giikko eti pitaliyaan gidin cenggurssan issuwa gidokkana. Koyro yafaraaxxoy “kkee” giya pitaliyan woykko cenggurssan wuriyoo wode naa''anttoy qaasi “kko” yaagiyaagan wurees. Yaaniyo gishshawu eti dumma. 
Shin ubba yafaratu wurssettan de'iya cenggurssati issi mala gidikko keetta timiis (guphiis) geettees. Ane kaallidi danttuwa qommota /shaahota xeelloos. 

4.2. Danttuwaa Qommota
I)	Humma danttuwaa 
II)	Cigichcha danttuwaa 
III)	Ceeqo danttuwaa 
IV)	Yetta danttuwaa 

Ane eti ay malakko issuwa issuwa birshshettaara kaallidi be'oos. 
I. Humma Danttuwaa 
Ha danttuwa shaahoy daro meezetettida danttonne ay asinne danttanawu danddayiyo dantto qommo. Leemisuwa: 
                       Laa maataa oyqqiyo wode asa aybee laammiyay 
                      Ayba shooshshee dukki kase eehshaa moogiyay? 
  
   II. Ciggichcha Danttuwaa
Ha danttoy qommo danttuwaadan keehi adussa hanotan danttettiyaaba gidenna. Hagee qanttan danttettiya dantto qommo. I qommo shaahuwappe guuttaa danttanawu wayssennan aggenna aybissi giikko qantta danttuwaa xaafiyoo wode qalamiya laggeyanawu/milatissanawu keehi shugo gidenna.

                   III. Ceeqo Danttuwaa 
Ceeqo dantto asaa na'aa minotettaanne beeraa qonccissiya dantto qommo. I issi asi woykko issi deree aadhdhida issi wodiyan woykko ha'i oottiiddi de'iyo nashissiyaa oosuwaa yootees. Ane kaallidi dumma dumma leemisota xeelloos. 
Leemisuwaa 1.  Bootta gattan toggiya gaammoy 
                        Morkkiya moogiya minoy 
                        Bari meran ceeqqiya goobay 
Ha qommo leemisoy issi asa woykko issi dere asaa minetettan. Ceeqettidi asi yexxiyo waayissikko ane guutta keena birshshattaa be'oos. “bootta gattan teggiya gaammoy” giyo yafaray bessiyoy beni wode Wolayttan keehi mino/gooba gidida shankkanchchati shankkan minnidi soodduwa kanttidi Humbbooraa shankkatidi abbala kanttidi hachchi Miraabe geetetti xeesiyoosaa ubbaa pinni kiyidi he ubba giddon worin wurenna do'aa hiixxiiddi bii biidi bootta gattan (nech-sar) giyo sohuwan keehi wolqqaamaanne cora do'ati de'iyo sohuwan shankkatidosona. Ha koyro yafaray hegaa yootees. Kaalliyaagee he wode asay morkkiyaara olettidi xoonennan aggennaagaa bessiyaagaa; wurssettan uttida yafaray kase wode wolayttan asay ceeqqiiddi leemisuwassi do'aa shankkan caddikko “Karetta Kolayttawu” yaagidi bari meeran ceeqqiyoogaa yootees.

        Gattan gagaamiyaagaa

            VI. Yetta Danttuwaa
Ha danttoy bari giddon cora qommo yetta danttota oyqqees. Leemisuwassi yettanchchati yexxiyo danttoti, masqqalawu yexxiyo danttoti, siiquwawu yexxiyo danttoti hegeetanne hegeeta malatiyaageeti aani xaaxi waaxettoosona. Ane kaallidi yetta danttuwaa leemisota xeelloos. 
                                                                
Leemisuwaa 1:
           Ta allaalliyawu yaasi sooddo qeeraa 
           Siiquwan kunddaas hay taaro poora 
           Ta gediyawu waatay meennabaa mizay 
           Mulssiyoo yooshshiyoo hanttaariyo bessay 

           Coo baassan keessay la ta eriyo Sooddo 
           Immada yaa ekkay yambbullo shooshsha daamiyo 
           I guyyiya sinttaa aappunaa ay ga paydoo
           I qim''otuwa xeelaa waatada woyga dogoo 

           Wonttimaattan Woybo woggaa wotaa shokkaas 
           Gasuubba kanttada Hobbichchawu baas Baddan kiyaas 
           Bodditte Ciishshaani 1 bayyada beettaas gooshshaa machchaas 
           Zataa lal'aydda ay shemppiyaanaa haarakkan kiyaas
           Gulggula Woliilaani 2.guuttaa gitaara gan'amettaas
           Humbbo Shaagaani 3 na'iyaa xayin shayaa duuxxaas 
           Wanddaara Bizzaani 4 tukkiya gophphiyan muqaattan koyyaas. 
           Saamintta qeeraa Sooddo giyan waasuwaa cooshshaas. 
Qonccissuwaa:
1.	 Ciishshaani1-Masqqaynnin
2.	 Woliilaani2-Oruwaani
3.	 Shaagaani3-Hamuusiini
4.	 Bizzaani4-Arbbiini
Hagaanne hagaa malatiyaa daro dumma dumma danttoti yetta danttotu giddon xaaxi waaxettana danddayoosona. 
Guyye baggaara nuui be'ido shemppuwan bila xifatiyaa aybatettawu mexi-issi/tilla birshshettaa immanawu xaafanchchati metootidoogaa denttida. Danttuwaa bilaa gidiinikka A era ciimmatettaappenne eraa macaraawa gidiyoogaappe denddidaagan A dummatettay keehi aakkidi beettees. Hagaa yuushuwan Asfaa Zarihuni giidoogaa ane kaallidi xeelloos.
        Ha bila xifatiya sheeshsha gidiyaagee 
        Era-oosuwaa layttatun daro taarikee 
        de'iyoo adussa wodiyawu de'idaba gididoogan 
        wodiyaan wodiyan denddiyaa pilggettatun 
        danttuwaa xaafiyaagaadaninne bila-xifatiya 
        eranchchatu dummatettaadan, xeelaa 
        dummatettaadan ubbaykka banttawu 
        beettidaagaadan dumma dumma birshshettaa 
        kuushshata immiiddi takkidosona. Hagaappe 
        denddidaagan ubbaa xaaxi-waaxiyaaba gidida issi
        tilla kuushshaa hagaa giidi yootanawu keehi deexxiyaaba. /1992: 73/       
                              
Ane naa''u aaho oyshatun loyttidi tobboos. 
1.	Danttuwaa bilaa issi xaaxi-waaxiyaa issi tilla birshshettaa immana danddayettibenna gaaso gidiyaa danttuwaa eeshshati aybee aybee?  
2.	Naa''anttoy qassi yaatin ha qofaa waatidi shiishshana danddayettii? 
Danttuwaa bilaa qassi hara bila xifate macaratuppe shaakkiyoogan aygiidi sunttanee? Danttuwaa bilaayyo issi tilla birshshettaa/kuushshaa immanawu danddayettibeenna geetettidi qofettiyaa gaasoti cora. Hageetuppekka koyroy danttoy adussa wodiyawu takkida era ooso gidiyoogan daro wodeta pinnidi yiidoogaa. Naa''anttoy danttuwaa xaafiyaa asatu xeelaadan, meezziyaadan danttuwaassi de'iyaa birshshettaa akeekay dumma gidiyoogaa. Heezzanttoy, danttuwaa nabbabiyaa dumma dumma asatu bolli I peeshshiyoo dumma dumma hulluuqoy/akeekay immiyoo dumma birshshettaa. Oyddanttoy, danttoy hara bila xifatetu maacaratuura xeelettiyoo wode ayyo de'iyaa go'aynne A utetta/ meretaa eeshshay dummatiyoogaa. Ichchashanttoy qassi  dumma dumma wodiyaan denddiyaa dumma dumma cora eranchcha asati bantta wodiyaan bantta wodiyaan dumma dumma birshshettaa immiiddi takkidoogaa, gidishin kaalliyaageenne wurssetta qofay qassi hara bila xifatetuppe dummatiyaa ogiyaan doonan xifatiyaankka aadhdhiyoo hanotay de'iyoogaanne adussa wodiyawu asaa naa wogaa qonccissiiddi takkidoogan dumma dumma wogay de'iyoo dumma dumma dere asawu I immiyoo birshshettay cora gididoogaa. Ha gaasotussa hanno gakkanawu dumma dumma eranchcheuti mexi issi tilla birshshettaa danttuwaa bilaassi immana danddayibeennay. Ha aaho dummatettati issi meraa oyqqidi ubba eranchchatussi, ubba asaa wogatussi, ubba sohotun, ubba ooratta gidi denddiyaa qofatussi, hegeetanne hegeeta malatiyaa gaasotussi issi mala birshshettaa immana danddayettenna gishshawu ubba biittaa asawunne ubba eranchchaawu oottiyaa issi tilla birshshettay de'ana danddayibeenna. 
Ubba xaafanchchatikka banttawu beettida ogiyaaninne hanotan A qonccissanawu malikkonne eti ubaykka denttiyoo qonccisso gidiyaa ano qofati de'oosona. Ubba eranchchati malikkonne eti ubaykka denttiyoo qonccisso gidiyaa ano qofati de'oosona. Ubba eranchchatuppe ekettida danttuwaa bilaa birshshettaa kawushsha oottidi ha''issi ekkana danddayettees. Hagee ubbay mayzziyaa qofaa medhdhanaassappe attin danttuwaa birshshettaa kuushshay hagaa gaanaassa gidennaagaa erana bessees. 

Meezziyaa
1. Kaallidi de'iyaa Asttamaariyaa Gamo Yohaannisa danttuwa wudidi xeelli simmidi 
   ha danttuwan aadhdhanaadan koyettida huuphe qofay aybakko tobbidi intte kifile laggetuura 
   intte qofaa shaakkite. Danttoy ekkana bessiyoo eeshshata ekkidaakkonnekka paaccite.

                                      Doonaa
Inxxarssay, achchay, menttershshay
Eti issippe maadettidi heezzay
Wogaara medhdhido cenggurssay
Haasayaan xaafuwan naa''u ogiyaan qoncciyaay
Ba de'uwawu koshshiyaabaa asi go'ettanawu
Issoy issuwaara qofan maayettanawu
Asi go'ettiyoogee hayttan siyettiyaagee
Doonaa geetettees ubbawu kanettiyaagee.

Kehabaa oottanawu iitaa maqqanawu
Aadhdhidabaa haasayanawu xaafidikka wottanawu
Hanana diyaabaakka hegaadan odanawu
Doonaa koshshees asi ba qofaa shaakkanawu

Ooninne qoppidi odi merissoogee 
Xoqqa ziqqa gaanawu naqaashay de'iyoogee
Dabbotan bollotan asawu gishettaagee
Issoynne baawa doonan dummatiyaagee
Asoo doona ubbi mexi issi lagge.

Doonawu meretay mankkay de'ees
Haasayawu xaafuwawu ubbawu wogay de'ees
Doonay  asadan yelettees, diccees
Haasayiyaabi xayiyoode qassi mule hayqqees.

Wodee ehiido timirttee nu biittaa geloosappe
Issi doona xalaalan timirttee imettoosappe
Hara doona ubban digettidoosappe 
Hara doona ubbay tooshettidoosappe
Qoodettiis layttay dariyaagee xeetaappe

Ha yohuwaa pilggi akeeki xeelliyoode 
Kase kawoy araatan kallachchan uttaagee
Ba sheeshshaa ba doonaara bonchchissoogee
Hara kochchaa A doonaara ubbaa toochchoogee
Bessanna naaqoy I nuna naaqqoogee.
Duuhay baynnan moogiis biittaappe A xayssiis
Tumaa eriyaa Xoossay nu tumaa I kessiis.

Toophphiyaan de'iyaa hara doonan
Balidi haasayikko timirtte keettan 
Cayettida warettida tuma gidennaban 
Daro wodiyaawu huqqunnettida bessennaban.

Issi doona xallay xoqqa gidin
Hara doona ubbawu sohoy xayin
Huqqunniyaa kawoy ayssiyoo aysuwaan
Nu doonaa yedhdhi moogidi 
Hara doonaa aassi dichchidi
Huqqunnaa qambbaran geli waaxettidi
De'ida daro layttaa Xoossawu magannidi.
Wanccay kumin huqqunnaa qambbaray me'iis;
Naaqetta doonatus leela qammay wonttiis.

Toophphiyan de'iya ubba doonawu 
Ba doonan tamaaranawu xaafanawu, 
Maatay imeettiis koyyobaa oottanawu
Saaba pitaliya xaph 33(zzaa)
Issuwawu issuwawu de'iya 7un qottaa
Haa, huu, kushiyaara hi, ho, giida 
Shaakkidi eranawu daro barchchiya be'ida
Ha saaba pitaliya qommuwa metuwaa
A qoodaa a qottaara
Asa ubbay shaakkidi ero giyoogan 
Wan-E, wan-B, wan-S, wan-D, giyoogan 
Issi kifilee shaahettin oyddu sohuwan 
Tamaaridosona daroti kase wodiyan 
Issi kifiliya oyddu layttan 
He metuwaa tuggaape shemppida 
Laatine pitaliya xapho (34)ddaa xallaa 
Hara waayssiya macaray baynnaagaa 
Ha''i kawuwaa chartteree ehiidoogaa 
Nu qaalan xaafanawu injjetiyaagaa 
Qantta wodiyan eranawu metennaagaa
Saaba pitaliyaadan adussa wodiya ekkennaagaa
Hammu giidi ekkida laatiine pitaliyaa 
Nu qaalan xaafanawu injjetiyaagaa 
Keehippe anjjoos ha maataa immida kawuwaa.

Bantta doonaa xoqqissiyaageeti 
Hara doona ubbaa toochchiyaageeti 
Giidosona hara doonay haatta pinttenna 
Ubbaykka siyda baaxiyaakka doommida 
Xoossaa wossida gallassaa naagida 
Xoonuwa demmida keehin ufayttida 
Laatine pitaliyaa wogaa kaallida, 
Nu aayee nu aawaa doonan xaafiyoogaa, doommida.
 
Nu doonay waayissenna eranawu metenna
Saaba pitaliyaadan adussa wodiya ekkenna
A lo''otaa eranawu shiiqa doomma be'a 
Laatine pitaliyan ne doonaa xaafada meezzeta 
Wolayttawu Oroomuwawu Sidaamawu
Ne doonan tamaaranawu xaafanawu
Ne wozanaa qofaa aassa qonccissanawu 
Laatine pitaliya go'ettada ne doonan xaafanawu
Doona ubbay lagge gidiyoogaa markkayanawu 
Qaadaa demmideta intteyyo hashshu!

Intte aayyee; aawaa doonan tamaarite,
Intte buzo wogaa issippe dichchite 
Gallassan gallasan minnidi oottite 
Asaban alleeqiyoogaa hegaa aggiigite, 
Intteyyo di'iyaaban go'ettiyooga meezetite 
Wontto yeletaa laatissiyoobaa oottite 
Intte sunttaa kehan hassayssiyaaba qoppite 
Tumaa pirddite qofan maayettite 
Zigirssaa, shaahotaa, baceessuwaa aggite.
   
 Asa maado xallaa naagi uttoppite 
Intte wolqqaa peesha, oottiyoogaa aggoppite 
Deexxiya metuwan dari un''ettoppite 
Intte wolqqaappe dariya metuwa, xoossawu yootite.
 
Pino kawotaa chartteree 
Doona ubbawu laggetaa maataa immaagee 
Asi ba doonan xaafo, tamaaro giidaagee, 
Nu morggiyaappe deexo qambbaraa denttaagee, 
Nuussi koshshiyaabaa  kunttanawukka d'iyaagee, 
Nuna  ufaysiis, laggetaa ehiidaagee.  

       Goshshanchchaattennee
Miixaa naagiyaa minuwaa yeliyaagee
Biittaa oottidi bari cawan aqiyaagee
Oottidi duretiyaagee odidi mayzziyaagee
Zerettaa wodiyaa ubbaa luxi eridaagee
Bar mehiyaa payyatettaa xeellidi eriyaagee
Asa ubbi A minotaa woraabana bessiyoogee
Goshshanchchaa gidennee dere ubbaa tookkiyaagee.

Kariyaan mittaa lo'uwaa kuwawu tokkiyaagee
Darkkon daro uuttaa aloy giday de'iyoogee
Pituwan oshan bari gadiyaa araddissiyaagee
Meezziyaan gidikkokka bari gadiyaa naagiyaagee
Zeriyoo cakkiyoo wodiyaa asa oychchennaagee
Bar cawaa oosuwaappe kalli mi de'iyaagee
Baappe palahiyaa murutaa giyawu shiishshiyaagee.

Ba eran ba cawan bana ayssiyaagee
Awudekka kalli miyay kabbashennan diyaagee
Kawo peeriyaa giiraa wodiyaara giiriyaagee
Worddobaa lagidi tumabaa haniyaagee
Deriyaan Xoossaanikka ubban dossettaagee
Goshshanchchaatenne Toophphiyaa tookkidaagee
Goshshanchchaatenne Toophphiyaa tookkidaagee!
(Ekettidoy: Manttaa Gaammu Yohaannisappe)

     4.3. Danttuwaa Eeshshata 
Danttoy issibaa woykko issi oosuwaa gitayidinne orddissidi, qofaa minttidi aattiyoo hanotay de'iyoo guutta doorettida qaalatun xaafettiyaa darobaa bari giddon tucci oyqqiyaa (siqqintta) bari yetta cenggurssan asaa hulluuquwaa eesuwan haariyaanne bochchiyaa mata gidida era ooso.
Danttoy bariyyo de'iyaa qaalatu utettan asaa wozanan eesuwan geliyoogan daro aaro bari hoolliyaa gakkiyaaba gidiyoogee aahuwaan odottees. Ha eran bari xaafettido halchchuwaa hoolliyaa shociyoo hanotay issi baqqaara qanttatettaaranne darobaa barigiddon tucci oyqqiyoo (siqqintta) gidiyoo eeshshaappe denddidaagaa gidiyoogee qoncce. (zarihuna 1992:74) 
Dumma dumma xaafanchchati danttuwaa aybatettay hagaa yaagidi odiyaageeti wottiyoo danttay yeda xifatiyaappe dummatiyoo eeshshata anotettan denttidi etan sima sima birshshettaa immanawu ha xadan zulettida danttuwaa eeshshata bayratiyaageeta. Ane kaallidi de'iyaa I yeda xifatiyaappe dummatiyoo eeshshata xeelloos: 
1.	Qantta/siita 
2.	Qaalatu dooruwan wudees
3.	Giraameriyaa wogaa kanttana danddayees. 
4.	Eeso 
5.	Bila haasayati ayyo miishshata 
6.	Siqqintta /bari giddon darobaa tucci oyqqidaba 
7.	Cora I shiiqiyoo meratatinne ufurettati de'oosona. 
8.	Qofaa issippetettaa naagida yafaratun shiiqees. 

Ha danttuwaa eeshshata qanttaaninne xaaxi-waaxo qofan kaallidi be'oos. 
                   Meezziya Naa''aa 
Kaallidi de'iyaa oyshata heezzan heezzan gididi tobboogaappe simmidi gamma/likke zaaruwa xaafidi shiishshite. 
1.	Danttoy qantta/ siitonne siqqintta woykko bari giddon darobaa tucci oyqqidaba 
yaagiyaa qofaa yeda xifatiyaara gati xeellidi kuuyite. 
2.	Danttoy qaalatu dooruwan wudees yaagiyoo hanotaa qonccissanawu 
      issi leemisuwaa shiishidi akeekissite.
