3. Danttuwaa ufurettata geetettiyaageeti aybakko hara xombbe 
     maxaatata shiishshi xeellidi zuleyite. 
4. Danttuwaa bila oosuwayyo issuwa gidida ubbay maayettiyoo tilla birshshettaa immana 
      danddayettibeenna hanota dumma dumma xombbe maxaafata nabbabidi qantta qonccisso 
     xifatiyaa shiishshite. 
      5. Danttoy yeda xifatiyaappe dummatiyoo bolla meraanne garssa meraa/eeshshaa qonccissite.          
          Issi leemiso gidiyaa danttuwaanne issi yeda xifatiyaa shiishshite. 
6. Issi huuphe yohuwaa dooridi issi danttuwaa xaafoogaappe guyyiyan bolla baggaara uttida 
    danttuwaa eeshshati waani aani beettiyakkonne qonccissite. 

1.	Danttoy minjja/siita (bari giddon darobaa tucci oyqqiyaaba) nne eeso.
  Bari giddon darobaa oyqqees yaagiyaagee issi danttuwa giddon de'iyaa qaalati bantta giddon   
 corabaa oyqqiyoogaanne issi  birshshettaappe bolla yidiyaagaa oyqqiyoogaa malaatees. Danttuwa giddon de'iyaa qaalati mexi issi qofaa xalaalaa oyqana mala  naagettokkona. Eti siqqintta (bantta giddon tucetti oyqettidabaa) woykko tuhetti uttidabaa birshshiyaakko keehi coraba gidana danddayiyaanne keehi aaho qofaa oyqqiyaba gidiyoogee be'ettana koshshiyaaba. Issi naa''u woykko oyddu kuriyaara de'iyaa danttoy yeda xifatiyan birshshidi xaafiyaakko he danttuwan de'iyaa hanotaa laammennan xaafanawu woykko wottanawu unddenna yeehchaa xaafissees.
 
Meezziyaa
Ane kaallidi de'iyaa naa''u yafaran giigida danttota yeda xifatiyaa wu laammite.
1.	 Aaya aawi xayin asa na'awu sari 
         Na'a dichchawu de'uwawu ooni etappe darii? 
2.	Deriyaayyo yelettiis deriyaayyo de'iis
Dichchaayyo woxxiiddi ogiyaan hayqqi xayiis.

Ha pude baggaara nu xeellido dantotussi naa''u na''u yafarati de'oosona. Eta yeda xifatiyaakko laammiyoo wode keehi aduqqoosona giyoogaa. Ha yafaratti mexile tammanne naa''u qaalatuppe  merettidi shiiqidosona shin ha qaalaturaa aadhdhiyaa qofay/kiitaynne issi asaa guuggiyan merettiyaa misilee/ aadhdhiyaa kiitay keehi aaho. Issi asi aawi woykko aaya kehiyoo kehatettaa, eti banttana siiqiyoo hanotaa, aaya baynna ixxikko woykko aaya kichchaychchikko de'iyaa metoy, tuggay hassayettidi cora qofaa ezggiyaageetu guuggiyawu aattees giyoogaa. Aaya aawi baynna guutta na'aa/yiiraa ooni aayodan/aawadan mishettidi dichchii? Ooni qarettii yaagiyaa oyshay siyiyageetu guuggiyan merettidi aaro qofaa medhdhees. Aaya aawi de'iyoo wode naatuyyo de'iyaa ishalo duussay, kaassay, hombocettay, ufayssay, seesay, naachchay ubbay guuggiyakko yees. Shin aawi aaya hayqqido na'i ha ubba ufayssaa, lo'o de'uwaa xayido gishshatawu iita qohettees. Hegaa gishshawu daro aassidi benibaanne ha''ibaa yuushshi aatti qoppidi bari giddon woykko bari guuggiyan keehi qohettees. Ha I woykko A bari guugge giddon qohettiyoo  hanotaa kessi bessanaagee danddayettenna. 
Qontta /minjja/siita giyoo wode qaalatu payduwaa coratettaa woykko guuttatettaa bessees. Danttuwa giddon qaalati hirayso gidokkona. Payya giyoonne qofaa keehi birshshana danddayiyaa doorettida qaalati geloosona. 

Danttuwa giddon payduwan keehi guutta gidida bantta giddon corabaa oyqqida qaalati doorettidi geloosona. Danttoy qofaa birshshidinne laalidi yootena. Koshshiyaa koshshenna qaalaa danttoy bori giddo gelissidi soho oyqqenna. Shanddaa shaaraa bari giddon oyqqenna gishshassa danttoy siita/qantta woykko minjja giyoy. Ha pudeera nu be'ido danttoy tammanne naa''u qaalatuppe merettiis. Shin yeda xifatiya meran xaafettiyaakko keehi daro qaalata wurssees giyoogaa. Eeso giyoo wode naa''ubaa bari giddon kuuyyidi oyqqees. Koyroy nabbabiyoo ogiyaa gidishshin haray qassi ayfiyaa xeelaa (xeellidi essuwan guuggiyan oyqqiyoogaa bessees). Leemisuwawu issi yeda xifatiya ekkikko issi nabbabiyaa asawu de'iya nibaabiya eray hanidoogaadan eeso gidikko eesuwan, lodda gidikko loddan qoodiiddi nabbabi wurssana danddayees. Nabbabiyaagee bari eraadan nabbabidi wurssees. Gido shin danttuwan nabbabuwaa ogiya nabbabiya asi A gidennan danttoy I bariyyo waati nabbabanaakko kaalettees. 
Danttay nabbabbettiyoo wode paca qofa qashotun beettiyaa qalametu yesuwan amppidi I bariyyo koyyiyoo yetta cenggurssaa giddo gelissees giyoogaa. Danttuwaa hanotaadaaninne A qommuwaadan dumma dumma yetta cenggurssaa koshshees. Nabbabettishin A yetta cenggurssay me'ana woykko mooretana bessenna. Hegaa gishshawu koyro yafaraa nabbabanawu kessido yetta cenggurssay xayennan woykko eqqennan de'ishin naa''antto yafaran de'iyaa koyro qaalaa xeesanawu eesotidi pinni aggeettees. Danttuwa nabbabiiddi eqqi eqqidi woykko shemppi shemppidi gidenna. A qonttatettay woykko shochchay naagettidi issippe eesuwan nabbabettishiina A kiitay meraa ekkidi merettiyoy. Issi danttuwaa issikuttan nabbabidi wurssi aggana xayikko A kiitaa oyqqana danddayettenna. Issi danttuwaassi issi baggaa nabbabi simmidi hankkuwa simmi nabbabana giikko kaseegee akeeekettenna. Yeda xifatiyaadan shaakki shaakkidi issi baggaa hachchi haraa hara saaminttan, attiyaagaa qassi haroode nabbabanawu hanenna. Hagaassa danttoy eeso yaagiyoy. 
Hara eesoy ayyo qassi issi xeelon ekkidi guuggiyan oyqqiyoogaa. Danttoy loddan heeraa moottaa xeelliiddi nabbabbiyooba gidenna. I issikuttan issi xeelan ekettidi eesuwan geetettidi eesuwan wurana bessiyaaba. Hegaa gishshawu danttuwa nabbabiyaa assi danttoy eeso giyaagaa bari guuggiyan wottidi bari ayfiyaaninne guuggiyaan issuwa nabbabosaara kaalliyaagaakko pala eesotidi kanttees. 
2. Danttoy qaalatu dooruwan wudees.
Ay xifatiya xaafiya eranchchaa gidikkonne A eray likettiyoy ba be'idoba woykko siyidobbaa woykko aattana koyyidobaa bariyyo beettidaariden hara nabbabiyaa asawu aattiyoo eraana. Hagaassi polettidabaa I polettidoogaadan hanidi asaayyo bettanaadan oottiyoogaa. Hegaayyo qassi doorettida keehi qonccissiya murta (kulkka) gidiyaa qaalati doorettiyoogee baaso. Danttoy qantta/minjja/siita, qassikka siqqintta (bari giddon corabaa oyqqiyaba) nne eeso yaagiyaa eeshshata ekkidoy A xaafanawu xaafanchchay qaalata dooriiddi keehi un''ettiyoo gishshassa. Danttoy bari giddon ay ogiyaanikka go'enna woykko payya birshshettaa immenna qaalata  ekkenna. Haray atto shin issi paca qofa qashuwaasikka maaddenna qaali dola gelenna. Hegaa gidikko danttuwa eraa oosoy bari halchchido sintta qofaa hoolliyaa shocennan gilqqidi atti aggana danddayees. Hegaa gishshawu danttoy asawu issibay gelenna ixxin asi metootennaadan woykko qaalati gelennan /akeekettenna ixxidi waayissennaadan qoodan keeehi guutta gidida payya qaalan koolettidi shiiqana bessiyaaba. Tumukka danttuwa giddon puuli baynna, qofaa aassi bessennanne asi salettiyoo qaalati beettana bessenna. I qoncce gididi minotettay de'iyoo maxetti kiyida asaa hulluuquwa eesuwan haariya suullaappe punettidi geeyyida gisttiyaadan qaalatun giigidi he qaalatikka bantta sohuwan bantta sohuwan giigaageeta gidana bessees. 
3. Danttoy qofaa issippetettaa naagida yafaratun shiiqees
Danttuwassi kare bagga bollaa xeelliyoo wode yafaratun uttiya, yetta cenggurssa malaban nabbabettiyaa kuushshan shociyaaba. Ha guussay tuma gidikkonne aahotettinne ciimmatetti bayna birshshetta gidana hanees giyoogaa. A kumetta eeshshaa qonccissoppoppe attin daro wode danttoy kuushshan shocees; yafaran yataran uuttees qassikka I yetta cenggarssan nabbabettees. Ha qommo baggaara nuuni giidobati tuma gididi de'ishin issi danttoy kuushshan shocido gishshatawu, shaahetti shaahettidi yafaran uttido gishshatawunne yetta cenggurssan nabbabetido gishshatawu danttoy kunttana bessiyoobata kunttiis gaana danddayokko. Aybissi giikko he maaran maaran uttida qanttanne doorettida qaalati qofaa issippetettay woykko gaytotettay (coherence) de'an koshshees. 
Leemisuwaa:
 Shufuro laggee pattennabaa zerees
 Umaa shaafay nuugee balgguwa baniya goggees. 
Ha bola yafaranxxatun ayba issippetettinne baawa. Koyroogee Pattenna laggiyaabaa yootiyoo wode kaalliyaagee qassi Umaa shaafaabaa yootees. Qanttan danttuwan de'iyaa naa''u woykko appe bolla gidiyaa yafaranxxotussi issippetettay de'ana bessees.

Hagaappe nu akeekiyoobi aybee? Danttoti bantta qanttatettaa naagidi, yafaranxxotun uttidi, bantta qalamiyaa yesuwaanne kuushshaa shochchaa naagidi uttikkonne etan kumettatetti woykko polotetti baynnaagaa akeekana bessees. Gaasoykka ha yafaranxxotun qonccida qofati issippetettan, issoy issuwaara maadettennan coo uttidosona. Hegaa gishshawu dantto meran uttida xifatiya hagee polo dantto yaagidi qoppana danddayettenna. 
 Ane kaallidi hara leemisota xeelloos: 
                1. Abbaayaa giddo namisetta hawulaashshuwawu 
                    ta mehiyaa meennaadan ta neeggo hadarays. 
               2. Saluwa iray bukkin deree dembbay lo'ees. 
                   Melida shullida dazzay ubbay haa aacana.  
               3. Yaagaara haagaara ne coo dafettishin 
                 wodiya harggee nena equwan wori aggana. 
Ha qommo baggaara nuuni be'ido leemisotussi qalamee, paca qofa qashoy, yafaray, yetta cenggurssay h.h.m. ubbay de'oosona. Hagaappe kase nuuni be'ido leemisotuura xeelliyaaba gidikko hageetussi qofaa issippetettay keehi mino. Naa''antto leemisota xeelliyoo wode. Payduwa issuwan de'iyaagee koyro yafaranxxuwan abbaayan de'iyaa namisettida hawulaashshuwa denttees. Kaalli qassi he namisettida hawulaashshoy A mehiyaa meenna mala hadarees. Heggaa gishshawu kase nu be'o leemisotoppe qofaa issippetettay de'ees giyoogaa. Etawu qofaa issippotettikka de'ikkokka issi dantuwawu de’ana bessiyaa kumetta eeshshaa oykkibeenna woykko maayibeenna. Gaasoykka eti kuushshan shocibookkona. Hegaa gishshawu issi lo'o danttoy yetta cenggurssaanne qanttatettaa naagida, qofaa issippetettay de'iyoo /oyqqida yafaranxxo oykidi issi attanawu woykko sissanawu kuyyidobaa gitayidi, puulayidinne orddissidi bessana koshshees. Kaalli laalli uttida naa''u qofan issippe de'iyaa/ qofan malatettiya yafaranxxoti xoqqu yaagiyaa issi kuriyaa medhdhoosona. Kuree naa''anne naa''aappe bolla gidida yafaranxxoti issi mala qofaa qonccissiyoo utettaa mera. Haagee yedaxifatiyan issi xifatiyaassi issi mentto mala oyiyoogaa. Issi menttoy bari giddon cora qofa qashota oyqqeer. He qofa qashoti ubbaykka mexi issi ano yohuwaa bolli wudoosona giyoogaa. Danttuwaassi issi kuriya giyoogee ha menttuwaakka mala. 

Issi mala qofaynne malatettiya yohoti ussippe shaahettidi uuttidosona. Kuriya yiyoya hagaa issi mala yohotinne qofati issippe issi kuriyan uttoosona, kuriyan kuriyan shaahettidi. Hagee qassi danttuwassi dumma eeshsha. Yafaranxxoti kuushshan shocidogishshawu qalametu yesoy naagettido gishshatawunne etawu yetta cenggurssay giigido gishsha xalaalaassi kumetta gidida issi qofaa aattees gaana dandayettenna. 
Ane kaallidi Gabayyo Biraanu kuruyaa xeelliyaagan woygidaakko xeelloos. 
     “ kuree- issidanttuwa giddon de'iyaa citan citan 
       uttida yafaranxxoti qofaa issippetettay woykko 
       utettaa issi mala hanotay woykko qofaanne 
       utettaa issippetettay de’iyoo yafaranxxotuppe
       merettiyaaba.” / 1999:198/ 
Nuuni qommo baggaara be’ido “wolayttawu wogade dees” 
Yaagiya danttuwan kure geetettidi shaahettidaageeti naa''u eeshshata: yafaranxxotu qofaa issippetettaanne azmmaachche de'iyooba gidiyoogan kunttana bessiyaabaa kunttidi beettiis. Hara danttuwa eeshshati:

 ( yafaranxxotu yesoynne kuushshaa shochchaa) geetettiyaageeti kaalliyaa   
  timirttiyan aahuwan be'ettana de'iyaabata. 
                   Meezziya Heezzaa 
Naa''u naa''u tamaare de'iyoo citata medhdhidi ha oyshatun tobbidi gamma zaaruwa immite. 
1) Issi danttoy dantto geetettanawu ayyo aybi aybi kumana bessii? 
2) Danttuwa kure geetettiyaabi aybee? Issi danttuwa leemisadan ekkidi A 
   kureta birshshidi bessite. Etawu de'iyaa qofaa issippetettaakka yootite. 
3. Danttoy qaalatu dooruwaa bolli wudiyoo hanotay ayyo ay mala eeshshati minnidi 
    beettanaadan oottidee? 
4. Yesuwanne yetta cenggurssaa naagidi kuushshan shocenna shin qassi  qofaa issippetettay 
    de'iyoo naa''u naa''u yafaranxxoti de’iyoo usuppun danttota xaafidi shiishshite. 
5. Yesuwacnne yetta cenggurssaa naagidi kushshan sohociyaa issuwan issuwan naa''u 
   yafaranxxoti de'iyoo ichchashu danttota xaafidi ehiite. 

Kaallidi danttuwa minjja/qantta hanuwa, bari giddoy darobaa oyqqiyoo hanotaa, eesotettaa, misiliyaa meruwaanne bila haagayata bari giddon oyqqiyoo hanotaa, doorettida qaalata go'ettiyoo hanotaa qonccissidi bessanawu maaddana mala issi “ Wodiyan” giya danttuwa ekkidi A gidduwaa be'oos. 
    Nena bonchchidaa banchchiyaagoo
   Nena kariyaagaa kariyaagoo 
   Oonanne awudenne eqqa naagennaagoo 
  Ne agga kanttaychchin oonne gakkennaagoo. 
      Nenaara biiday bonchchettiis duretiis
      Asa na'a ubbaappe wolqqaamiis duretiis 
      Nena go'ettennay metootiis hiyyeesiis
      Ogiya doonan uttidi woossanaayyo kiyiis. 
Ne taayyo alleeqo ta nena bonchchana 
Neeni taayyo miishsha ta nena minjjana 
Ne tawu siiqo lagge nenaara de'ana 
Ta guyye attikke nenaara paallana 
   Alleeqo miishshadan neeni bonchchottennee 
   Eessaa lliuwaadan neeni mal''ottennee 
   Dosetta buquradan neeni saaphottennee 
   Daannadan pirddanawu neeni geeshshottennee. 
Ha danttuwa nabbabin nuuyo siyettiyaa sissaa, beettiyaa misiliyaa, aadhdhiyaa kiitaa xaafanchchaa qaalatunne bilaa go'ettuwa ubbaa ane birshshidi xeelloos, Ay danttuwaninne birshshettay nabbabbiyaa izzawudan dummatana danddayiyoogaa hassayana bessees. Gaasoykka danttuwa giddon de'iyaa qaalati corabaa bantta giddon tucci oyqqidaba gido gishshawu dumma dumma nabbabbiyaa asalou dumma dumma aaho birshshettaa immana donddayees. 
Ha danttuwa geluwan bollan xaafanchchay “Nena bonchchidaa bonchchiyaagoo” yaagiiddi denddiis. Wodee bana go'ettennaagaa aggidi bi aggiyoogaa, I oonanne eqqi naagennaagaa, wodiyaa ooninne sinttatana danddayennaagaa koyro kuree yootees. Naa''antto kuriya ekkikko wodiyaa suure go'ettida asi boncchchettido hanotaa, wolqqaamoogaa, duretoogaa, wodiyaa go'ettibeenna asi metootoogaa, hiyyeesoogaa, manqqidi woosawu kiyidoogaa qonccissees. 
Heezzantto kuriyaa xeellikko, xaafideeagee bariyyo qaalaa gelishin be'eettees. “ Neeni taayyo alleeqo ta nena bonchchana” gaagees, nena minjjana, nenaara de'ana, nenaara paallana gees. Aybissi giikko wodiycaara biida asay/ go'ettida asi bonchchettiis lo''o xekka gakkiis. Hegaa qommobaggaara de'iyaa naa''antto kuriyaan yootiis. Wurssetta kuriyaan wodiyaa neeni bonchchottennee, neeni mal''ottennee, neeni saaphottennee, neehi geeshshattenne yaagiidi A lo'otettaa markkettees. 
Xaafanchchay dumma dumma bilatakka go'ettennan aggibeenna. Leemisuwassi koyro kuriyan koyro yafaranxxuwan doommiiddi “nena bonchchidaa bollchchiyaagoo” yaagiiddi doommiis. Asa gidenna haasayana danddayennabaa, ayfiyan xeellanawu beettennabaa A siyana danddayennabaa ‘nena’ yaagiiddi xaafanchchay doommiis. Hagee qassi bilatuppe issuwa gidiyoogan Nenotto bilaa geetettidi erettees. Qassikka wurssetta kuriyan xaafidaagee “ alleeqo miishshadan, eessaa ililuwaadan, dosettida buquradan, daannadan” yaagiiddi hara geeddarisso bilaa go'ettishin be'eettees. Xaaxi – waaxiyoo wode xaafanchchay wodee band go’ettenna wraa kawushshiyoogaa, bana go'ettidawu dureta, misshsha gidiyoogaa qonccissidi yootiyoogaappekka aaruwaa bariyyo wodiyaa bonchchanawu woykko go'ettanawu qaalaa gelishin be'eettees. Yaaniyoo gishshawu ha danttuwa nabbabbiyaa dumma dumma asawu dumma dummabay guuggiyan mislettanawunne dumma dumma akeekay merettana danddayees. 
Ane Burunjje Bungge yetta dantotuppe issuwa gujjidi xeelli makkidi meezze oyshatukko kanttoos. 
(Batta) Gattan toggiyaa gaammoy 
        Gaammuwaa yeliyaa maahee 
        Wuuwwuy wolay woddiis 
        Wuuwwuy zarphphee me'iis 
       
       Ta azinaa shemppiyoo maaro
       biittay kocan denddo 
       wodee xeetidi tammiis
       ta taro am''e taaro 
       ta taara am''e taaro 

       laametto taayyo layttay 
       yibbaata gido he wogay 
       menttan gaytto laatay 
        Haakko ayiso azinay 
        Piti piti ayiso azinay 
       Shari shari ayiso azinay. 

    Kochchooroy assawu baggay 
    Kiisiyaara danccuwara boottay 
    Cuuchchay gonddoy loshay 
    ta sunttaa cayida boozay 
    bawutay waanna miizzay 
    ba xallaa sabbiyaa curqqay 
    eeyyatu xeessay hawu''ay. 

    zino baynnaagee kuttoy 
    kanaa kaalliyaagee tunay 
    guyye ashaagee bullay 
    ajaajjee looxxay loshay 
    kareera kafaafa puusoy 
    buleera goseera manqqoy 
    maallado worddo xoossay 
    omarssi kayso kanay. 

Oottenna ootenna yibbaata aysettiyoo wogay 
tookkenna tookkenna allagaa ta azinaa miixay 
yelenna yelenna zeerusaa maahiyaa qanttay 
attenna attenna ta gishshay ta zuussawu qommoy 

O booree O baaraa qolchchii? 
O miixay O miixaa toochchii? 
O wogay O wogaa kammii…

Baa maakka baa maakka allagawu ta naatu wolqqaa
 kaallakka kaallakka singgakka ta peenuwaa baanaa 
 cayakka cayakka toochchakka ta naatu sunttaa 
menttakka menttakka mooraaliya hay ta soo denttaa. 

Ha danttuwaa giddon daro dumma dumma cuccumati de'oosona. A nabbabbiyaa dumma dumma asi bariyyo dumma dumma birshshettaa ekkana danddayees. Aani qassikka bila haasayati zuguyaan haasayidobatikka de'oosona. 
Ha yetta danttuwan xeelliyoo wode issi iita asaa be'eettees. He asi keehi huqqunnettido gishshatawu xaafanchchay “ wuuwwuy wolay woddiis, wuuwwuy zarphphee me'iis” yaagidi asaa shiishshanawu waassishin be'ettees. Ha ayso azinaappe denddidaagan “ ta taaro am''e taaro laa meto taayyo layttay haakko ayiso azinay yaagidi xaafanchchay qanggees. 
Ha ayissiyaa asi bari iita ayisuwan assaa ayissana koyyeesinne bari wogan haraa wogaa kammana, bari miixan haraa miixaa toochchana koyyees. Bari aysannawu koyyiyoo amuwan de'iyaa asi haratussi iita gidiyoogaa ha danttoy akeekissees. Xaafanchchaykka tishshi oottidi cayees. puuziyaa ajay, godaa wurssiyaagee xonttay, zadaluwaa qaattida dulloy, miichchiiddi 
miyaagee Umay, sunttaa cayida bozzay, bawutay waanna miizzay. Ba xallaa sabbiyaa curqqay kareera kafaafa puusoy, bulleera goseera manqqoya h.h.m. gees. Ayssi giikko ha asi asaa iita qohees; asi erennan xonttaadan asaa de'uwaa taarikiyaa qohees. Sunttaa bashshees. bari xalaalaa sabbees. I kareera kafaafa shiini buleera goseera manqqo. Hagaadan asaa toochchiiddi, qassi bari xalaalaa sabbiidi lo'o malatiiddi biittaa dichchaappe guyye ashshiyoogaa yootees. 

                  Meezziyaa oyddaa 
Kaallidi heezzu oyshati shiiqidosona. Eta naa''an naa''an gididi tobbidoogaappe simmin kaallidi de'iyaa gallassawu oottidi shiishshite. Intte ha oyshatu yuushuwan kifile giddon tobbanay xaaxi waaxo gidida waati ha meezzziyaa ootti polanee giyoobappe attin ha''i doommeeta giyoogaa gidenna. 
1) Issi danttuwa xaafanawu huuphe yohuwaa dooridi danttuwaa kumetta eeshshaa kunttiyaa issi payya danttuwa intteppe xaafidi intte asttamaariyaassi/reessi shiishshite. Kifile giddonikka denddi eqqidi intte kifile laggetussi nababite. 
2) Laybireeriyaa biidi dumma dumma xombbee maxaafatuppe wochchidi  issi inttena ufayssiyaa danttuwaa xaafidi/ duuqqi ehiidi kifile gidon intte laggetussinne asttamaariyaassi/reessi yetta cenggurssaa naagidi nubabite. 
3) Bila haasayati danttuwaassi gita maaddiyaaba. Dumma dumma maxaafata nababidi ichchashaappe bolla gidiyaa bila haasayaa qommotanne eta meretaa qonccissiyaabaa xaafidi shiishshite. 

4.4. Danttuwa Uferettata 
      Tobbiyoo oyshata: 
1.	Danttuwaa ufurettaa giyoogee aybee? 
2.	Danttuwa ufurettata yaagiyoogeeti aybee aybee? 

Ufurettata yaagiyoo wode issibay merettidobata woykko issibay merettanawu miishshadan ekettidabata /go'ettidobata gaana danddayeettees. Danttuwa ufurettata giyoo wodekka danttoy merettiiddi bari giddon oyqqidobata gaanaassa. Issi keettay keexettanawu ayyo darobay koshshees. Leemisuwawu Goday, meegay, gattay, tuussay, yuushuwan eqqiyaa zaaro mittay, qoree, qosilettay, ifittay, zanddiiday h.h.m mule ubbaykka issi Wolaytta keettaa keexxanawu de'ana koshshees. Qorqqoro keettawukka hegaadan abay ayyo shiiqana koshshees.  Hegaadankka danttoy keexettiyoo woykko merettiyoo ufurettati de'oosona. Hegeetikka: 
?	Qalamiyaa 
?	Paca qofa qashuwa 
?	Yafaranxxuwa
?	Yetta cenggurssaanne (rhythm) 
?	Kuriyaa
Ha danttuwa meretawu koshshiyaa miishshati koyettiyaa keenaaninne eti gelana bessiyaa sohotuninne hanotatun gelidi beettana xayikko, he danttoy kumetta gidana danddayenna woykko I paca gididi attees giyoogaa. 
Ayyo bessiyaa danttuwaa ufurettatuppe haray atto shin mexi issoy paccikko haray A sohun eqqees/ geelees yaagiyoobi de'enna issuwawu issuwawu danttuwa meretay dumma gidida A maadoy A maadoy de'ees. Issoy paccikko hari de'iyoo gishshatawu aykko baa geetettenna. Ha qommo baggara nuuni keettaa keexxanawu koshshiyaabatuppe leemisuwawu godi paccin, woykko, meegi, woykko zaaro mitti paccin keetti maara keexettana danddayettennaagaadan giyoogaa. Issi issi ufurettay danttuwaassi hari eqqana danddoyenna sohuwan eqqidi keehi gita go'aa immees giyoogaa. 
Eti essippe oyqettidi issi danttuwassi shemppo immoosona. Hegaa gishshawu danttoy denddiyoodenne qofettiyoo wode uferettati denddoosona/qofettoosana. Aysi giikko danttoy ufurettati baynnan eqqana danddayenna. Cora danttuwaa ufurettati de'oosona. Eta issuwawu issuwawu dumma dumma eeshshatinne go'ati de'ikkonne eti ubbay issippe gididi lagge danttuwa kooloosona. Danttuwa ufurettata xeelliyaagan eti awugeetakkonne Asfaa zarihuni immiyoo birshshettaa ane xeelloos: 
“Danttoy laggetida issi mala adussatettay de'iyoo yafaranxxotun 
uttiyaagaa gidishin issi issi yafaray qassi yafaranxxo 
geetettees. He issi issi yafaranxxoy issi mala yesoy de'iyoo 
paca qofa qashotun shaahettees. Paca qofa qashoy issi 
shemppuwan woykko issi kuttan nababettiyaanne issi 
mala qalamiyaa oyqqida qaalatu shiiqogidishin
“siitoy/minijatettay qassi “paca qofa qashotunne
 qalametu yesoy kuuyettiyooba gidishin danttuwa
 kuushshaa shochchawu keehi aaho baggay de'iyooba. 
Shochchay danttuwa bilan kuuyettida cenggurssaa, 
qaalaa woykko paca qofa qosho zaaretonne lagge
 gidiyaa qofa qashotunne yafaranxxotu zuppiyan 
merettiya, issi giigida issi mala wodiya likkiyan 
geetettiyaaba. Xaaxi waaxiyoo wode shochcha giyoobi 
beettiyoy qofa qashotuninne yafaranxxotun de'iya 
qalameti banttawu de'iya yesuwaan issuwa gidiyoo 
wodiyaana. Ayyo yesoy issi mala gidana xayikko 
shochchaykka shoraa xayees. Shochaassi shori 
xayikko qassi danttuwa bilan koyettiyaa yetta 
cenggurssay woykko cenggurssan beettiyaa 
shonggay xayi aggees. / 1992: 78/ 

Ha dayttuwa ufurettatu aybatettaanne eeshshaabaa xaaxi-waaxo gididanne qantta qonccissuwa kaallidi xeelloos:

1.	 Qalamiyaa (meter)
Qalamiyaa giyoogee hara suuppabawu shaahettanna danddayenna wurssetta gidida cenggurssa ubbaappe keehi guutta gididaba. Qalamee issikuttan geetettiyaanne appe guuxxiya kifilee baynna danttuwaa ufurettaa.yafaran woykko paca qofaa qashuwan beettiyaa qalametu yesoti/ paydoti yafaranxxuwaa adussatettaaynne qanttatettaa, paca qofa qoshuwa ahotettaanne xunttatettaa, danttuwa shochchnaanne siitaa woykko qanttatettaa, yetta cenggurssaanne yafarata xaafiyoo hanotaa woykko ogiyaa kuuyyoosona. 

Leemisuwaa: 
                  ?  ?      ?  ?  ?  ?   ?  ?   ? ??   ?
                  Hachchiini minnikko qanttaani gixxikko        6/6
                   ?   ?   ?   ? ?  ?    ? ?  ?   ?  ? ?
                  Oosuwaani minnikko cawaani genccikko   6/6

                   ?  ? ?   ? ??   ?  ?  ?   ? ? ?
                  Nu de'oy mal''ana xumabay poo'ana.    6/6

?      ?       ?    ?      ?     ?      ?        ?    ?    ?   ?     ?
Ha  chchii  ni    mi    nni   kko    Qan    ttaa   ni   gi   xxi   kko        6/6

Ha bolla baggaara be'idoogaadan dumma dumma danttotussi qalamiyaa qooday dumma dumma gidana danddayees. Ha pude leemisuwan de'iyaagee usuppunay usuppunaara (6/6) giyoogaa aybissi giikko issi issi paca qofaa qashuwaa qalamee usuppuna usuppuna gidiyoo gishshataassi. Hayyanintta Loohissiyaagoo/ree ha yohuwaa bollan ahho qonccissuwaa immanaadan qofissays.

Meezziyaa
Ane tamaaretoo kaallidi imettida issi kuriyaawa danttuwaassi aappun qalameti de'iyaakko ootti bessite. 
         Xoossi immin asi diggii?
         Xoqqan kaqqin kani ekkii?
         Taani dosin asi diggii?
         Xoossi giikko naa''ay deana 
         Baso oyttiyo issippe maana. 

2.	Paca qofa Qashuwa
Issi yafanranxxuwaa giddon beettiyaa qaalatu giddoppe cenggurssay   qanxxettennan issi shemppuuan woykko yetta cenggurssan geetettiyaa woykko nabbabbettiyaa issippe de'iyaa qaalata paca qofa qoshoy issi yafaranxxuwaassi baggaa woykko issi yafaranxxuwaassi gidduwaappe shaakkidoogaa gaana danddayettees. Leemisuwaawu ane bolla danttuwaa paca qofata xeelloos. 
                  Hachchiini minnikko                Qanttaani gixxikko        
             
                  Oosuwaani minnikko               Cawaani genccikko   

                  Nu de'oy mal''ana                     Xumabay poo'ana.    
 
Ha bolla bagga danttuwaa kuriyaan de'iyaa yafaranxxoti qofa qashuwan shaahetti shaahetti uttidosona. 
Ane issi yetta danttuwaappe ekettida issi kuriyaa leemisuwaawu ekkoos:

Aybawu tana oohiyawu immay 
Siiquwa lissuwan ta ashuwa shocay 
Shemppuwan kaa'ay worada pattay 
Ta hayqqiyoode haahuwan xeellay?
Ha danttuwaassi koyro kuriyan naa''u paca qofa qashoti de'oosona. Hegeetikka “aybawu tana” giyaageenne “oohiyawu immay” giyaagaa. Koyro paca qofaa qashuwa issitoo kiyida shemppuwan nabbabbiigeettees; naa''anttuwakka hegaadan. “ Aybawu tana” giya koyro paca qofa qoshuwa giddon ‘y’ nne “wu” siyettokkona eti mitetti attiigoosona. Attida hara xeesettiyaageeti qoodettiyoode oydda. Naa''anttoykka hegaada “Oohiyawu immay” giyaagaa giddon “yawu” nee ‘y’ siyettokkona/qoodettokkona. Hegaa gishshawu naa''antto paca qofa qashuwanikka oyddu qalameti de'oosona. Muumeera ha koyro yafaran hosppun qalameti de'oosona. Ha koyro yafaran hosppun qalameti de'oosona, Hegaa gishshatawu haguwu 4/4 qalameti de'oosona giyoogaa.
                                 3. Yafaranxxuwaa (verse)
Yafaranxxoy haraba gidennan issi danttuwaalsi issi kumetta yafaraa giyoogaa
Ane kaallidi de'iyaa heezzu kuree de'iyoo danttuwaa xeelloos. 

Ne guuggiyaappe eraa pulttissa aliyaagoo,
Xumida ta de'uwawu xomppedan poo'iyaagoo,
Gallassan gallassan tana xomoosiyaagoo,
Neeppe aadhdhanaadan tana minttettiyaagoo,
Ta woyga galatoo geeddariyaay baynnaagoo.

Saluwaara paalliyaagawu payleettiyaayyo aaway,
Saynisiyaa pilggettawu mucuraayyo baasoy,
Hargganchchaa pattiyaagawu dottoriyaayyo denddoy,
Gooba goshshanchchata denttettida minoy,
Neeppe hari oonee dere ubbawu poo'oy?

Ne bonchchoy xoqqu go oosanchchatu giddon,
Ne qooday palaho ubbatookka payduwan,
Beeray neegee aaho nu biittaa dichchanawu,
Sinttanawukka minna deriyaa kaalettanawu,
Sabay neessi bessees merippe merinawu.

Meezziyaa
1.	Tamaaretoo ha bolla danttoy obaa yootii?
2.	Issi issi kuriyaan yootottida kane qofatu bolli tobbite
 Ha danttuwaassi aappun yafaranxxoti de'iyoonaa? Ayyo tammanne uchchashu yafaranxxoti de'oosona. Issi danttuwaassi guutta giishin naa''u yafaranxxoti de'ana danddayoosona.                                           
Issi mala woykko mise qaalatu cenqqurssati issi danttuwaa giddon ubba qassi issi issi kuriyaan zaaretti zaaretti yiyoo hanotay shochchaa  geetettees. Shochchaynne mucurettay/siqqintta hanotay  issoy issuwaa giddon qoomettidi beettiya meretanne zaaretti zaaretti yiyoo yesuwaa wodiyaaninne yetta cenggurssan kuuyettidi shiiqiyoo hanotaa. 
Issi doomettan de'iyaa paca qofa qashuwaa nababanawu go'ettiyoo wodeenne geeteettiyaa yetta cenggurssay wurssettan de'iyaa paca qofa qoshuwa nababanawu go'ettiyoo wodiyaara lagge gidana bessees. Hagee qassi danttuwaa giddon de'iyaa qalamiyaa yesuwaa laggetettaa koyyees giyoogaa. Ha shochchaynne mucurettay issippe gididi biyaa issi mala wodiyaan simmi simmidi yiyaaba. 

                     4. Yetta cenggurssaa (Rhythm)
Issi paca qofa qashuwan beettiya qalametu yesuwaappe danttuwa nabbabanawu woykko gaanawu koshshiya shonggaara de'iyaanne asa wozanaa bochchiyaa cenggurssa giyoo hiilla. Paca qofatu giddon beettiyaa qalametu paydoy dariyoogaaninne guuxxiyoogan kiyiyaa yetta cenggurssay keehi dafettanawu woykko qaammidi qanxxettana danddayees. Lo'o yetta enggurssay de'ana mala qalametu paydoy, sochchay keehi maaddiyaaba giyoogaa.
Ane kaalliidi dumma dumma qalametu yesoy de'iyoo dumma dumma yafariyoo hiillati shiiqido odettiyaa danttota woykko yetta danttota xeelloos. Ubba danttotakka kaalli kaalli be'eana. 
                         Oosuwaa
 Oosuwa ayssi kariyoo issuwa haraappe dooriyoo
Oosuwaa ayssi toochchiyoo shaahuwaa ayssi medhdhiyoo
Ooso ubbay lagge lagge wottidaagee
  Mizi ushshidaagee mayzzi gixissaagee
  Neegan neegan minna deree hoola gaana
Neeni yaynettan sinttawu sinttawu baana.                    
                        
Ha pude baggaara nu xeellido danttuaassi issi issi yafaranxxoy aappun qalametuppe merettidee? 

5. Kuriyaa (stanza)
Kuriyaa giyoogee issi danttuwaa giddon beettiyaa naa''anne appe bolla gidiyaa paydoy de'iyoo shaahetti shaahetti uttida yafaranxxoxa malaatees. I issi mentto mala gaana danddayettees. Ane kaallidi issi siiqo yetta danttuwa ekkidi A giddon woqqu kureti de'iyaakko xeelloos. 
                
  Waanoo Yooshshee
Waanoo yooshshee ne wogay wottenna 
Waanoo yooshshee ayissenna peeshshenna 
Waanoo yooshshee uyennaani mattottays 
Waanoo yooshshee ne siiquwa harggays. 

Aybawu tana oohiyawu immay 
Siiquwa liissuwan ta ashuwa shocay 
Shemppuwan kaa'ay worada pattay 
Ta hayqqiyoode haahuwan xeellay 

Ne biyoode ne yiyoode kaallaysi 
Qoppaydda arggoora awaa moogayis 
Omarssan hiittan nebaa harggayis 
Ne bay denddiyoode gooshshaa qaaqqays. 

Qoppikke giin ne attakka. 
Tu gullottin ne geemmakka 
Kushiya immaas biikke awukka 
Duttan uttaas heggaa ekka. 

Taayyo xalee ne danccuwan dees 
Ta amuwa koshshaa ne kahay erees
Garsseera haaya ta sotuwan seellees
Uttiin  eqqin taayyo nebay bettees.      
                           
Ta ayfiya afuttay caggenna 
Menttees tawu heqqunttay simmena 
Yibbaa qachchiya maraccee tawu deenna. 
Ne bayinnan ta suuttay oottenna. 
                 ( Manttaa Burunjje Bunggeppe) 
Ha danttuwaassi aappun kureti de'iyoonaa? 

5. Laame bila Haasayaa ogeta/Hiillata (Figures of Speech)
Laame haasaya ogeti issibaa qonccissiiddi xaafettidoogaadaana gidennan hara dumma ogiyaan qonccissoosona. Laame haasayan issi nabbabiyaagee xaafettidaba/qaalaa xalaalaa xeellidi akeekana danddayenna hegaappe aadhdhidi qoppana/pilggana bessees giyoogaa. Etikka bantta giddon kaalliyaageeta xaaxi-waaxoosona:
1. Geeddaro (Simile): Hagee naa''ubaa laggeyi/geeddari xeelliyaagaa gidishiin kaalliyaa      
    qaalatanne eta malatiyaa hara qaalata go'ettees: ….dan,  mala, malatees.
   Lm. Hagee na'ay ba aawwaadan haasayees.
          Ta siiqiyaa kiitanchchaa malatawusu.
                Manjjuri godare mala.
2. Laamenttaa (Metaphor): hagee bila haasaya qommo gididi naa''ubaa geeddariiddi issuwaa eeshshaa harawu muumeera immidi laammi aggees. 
Lm. Ta siiqiyaa kiitanchcha. (bari siiqiyoo kiitanchchaara laammiis)
        Manjjuri godare. (Manjjura giyoo asa godariyaara laammiis)
3. Asumma (personification): Hagee bila haasaya gididi asa gidennabaa, shemppoora 
       de'ennabaa woykko ayfiyan beettennabawu asa eeshshaa immiyoo hanotaa.
Leemisuwaa: 
       Kaamee keehi horddofees.
      Mittay yeekkees.
4. Nenotto bilaa (Apostrophe): Hageekka bila haasayaa qommotuppe issuwaa gididi issi matan baynna asa, woykko hayqqiichchidabaa, woykko asa gidennabaa asadan nena yaagidi malaatiyoo/haasayissiyoo hanotaa.
Leemisuwaa.
      Laa deriyaa daamootaa ne baree woyseeshsha?
      Saluwawu ne iraa nuuyyo aybissi diggay? 
5. Xoqqissuwaa (hyperbole): Hagee issibay hanidobaappe woykko polettidobaappe keehi 
      xoqqissidi haasayiyoo bila. 
Leemisuwaa: 
           Taani neeyyu xeetu sha'utoo odiini ne siyabaakka.
          A bari siiquwaa maccaamiyan ta wozanaa daakkaasu.
6. Ziba haasayaa (Irony): Ha bila haasayay aattiyoo kiitay I yootiyoo qaalaadana gidennan 
      Phalqqetta ogiyaan aattees.
     Leemisuwawu: 
              Issi keehi zawi baynna ordde na'iyoo “Bii lee'e misqqiiqee” giyoogaa mala.
             Issi keehi qantta asa “ Laa xonggollawu” yaagiyoogaa.
7. Laame suntta (Metonomy): Hagee issi erettida sunttaassi hara keehi erettibeenna/lame sunttaa 
   immiyoo hanotaa qonccissees. 
   Leemisuwawu: I Maataa koyyees gaanawu, I oydiyaa koyyees. Giyoogaa.

Meezziyaa 
Tamaare naatoo ha qommo baggaara intte be'ido lee bila haasayatussi issuwawu issuwawu ichchashaa ichchashshaa gidiyaa leemisota kaallidi de'iyaa kifiliyaassi ekki ehiidi intte asttamaariyaassi/reessi sheedhdhite. 



ICHCHASHANTTO SHEMPPUWAA
5. MEDHDHI  XAAFUWAA
Ha timirttiyaa sintta qofata: 
Ha timirttiyaa wurssettan tamaareti: 
?	Medhdhi xaafowa aybatettaa yootana. 
?	Dumma dumma bila xifatiyaa qommotussi naqaashaa cuccumana. 
?	Dumma dumma medhdhi xaafotu meraa shaakkana. 
?	Dumma dumma medhdhi xaafotu giddon de’iyaa shiishuwaa dummatetta zuleyana. 
?	Dumma dumma adussanne qantta medhdhi xaafota nabbaboogaappe simmin eta                                
    dummatettaa eta eeshshaara qonccissana. 
?	Medhdhi xaafotu meruwaa woykko xaafuwaa meezzeetana. 












5.1. Medhdhi Xaafuwa  
Ha kifiliyaan dumma dumma medhdhi xaafo qommotubaanne eta meraabaa tamaarana. Medhdhi xaafuwaninne chii-medhdhi xaafuwaa giddon de'iyaa dummatettaabaakka be'ana. Qassikka kase shemppuwan be'ido yeda xifatiyaaninne danttuwaa giddon de'iyaa xaafuwaa meraa woykko hanotaa dummatettaa akeekan. Yeda xifatiyaa meran shiiqiyaa medhdhi xaafotu eeshshaa be'ana. Ha shemppuwan aadhdhiyaa timirttiya kumetta akeekaa demmanawu intte (tamaareti) loyti hashetidi oottana bessees. Imettiyaa imettiyaa meezzettun loyttidi intteyyo siyettiyaa qofaa la'a gididi qonccissana bessees. 
Ha huupphe yohuwan xaafettida qofaa polo akeekallawu ha moojuuliyaa giddo xalaalan xaafettidabay gidenna agaana danddayees. Hegaa gishshawu untte ha huuphe yohuwan xaafettida hara hara maxaatata laybireeriyaa biidi nabbabbana bessabbana bessees. Hagaappe kasenu be'ido shemppotun dumma duma bila xifatiyaara ohettidi de’iyaabata be'ida. Appe kaalliyaa getun bila xifatetu qommotuppe issuwaa gidiyoa odettidabatanne xaafettida bilaxifatiyaa yara gidiyaa danttuwaa pilggida. 
Ha shemppuwan qassi kane gidida yohota bila xifatiyaappe kare kiyennan dumma dumma hara macarata be'ana. Haratuppe aattidi yeda xifatiyaa meran aadhdhiyaa dumma medhdhi xaafotu giddoppe adussanne qantta medhdhi xaafotu bollan wudana. 
Bila xifatee bri giddon odettidabata, danttuwa, tiyaatiriyaa, adussa medhdhi- xaafuwa, qantta medhdhi xaafuwa oyqqiyoogaa kase be'ida. Eti ubbaykka issippe malatettiyoobati de’ikkonne bantta shiiquwan meran qassi dummatoosona. 
                                                          
Utettaa (form) giyoogee issi issi bila xifaiyaa maearay shiiqiyoo woykko giigiyoo meraa giyoogaa. Leemisuwawu yeda xifatee yetta cenggurssi, mucuriyoobi baynnan yeda xaafettidaba gidiyoo wode gassi danttoy qalamiyan, paca qofa qashotun, yafaranxxotun, shochchaan yetta cenggurssotun h.h.m. mucurettidanne guutta qaalatun shiiqees. Hegee ayyo giddo hanotaa. Kareera xeellikko qassi woraqataa bolli gaxaappe gaxan gakkanawu xaafettenna danttuwaa maaraadan kuriyaan kuriyaa shaahettidi yeechchaassi/ woraqataassi giddo gillan uttiyoo/ xaafettiyoo hanotay de'ees. Shin yeda xifatee yeechchaa bolli gaxaappe gaxaa gakkanaashin kumidi xaafettees. Bari tobbanawu denttido hoophe yohotu bolli aaho birshshettaa immiiddi corabaa daro sinttatun / yeechchatun xaafees. Tiyaatireenne A malatiyaaseeti qassi koyro yeechchaa bolli xaafettirggidi gutaran asaa/ galchchaa sinttan oosetti/ poletti be’etiyaaba. Ha shiiquwaa ogiyaa nuuni utettaa (form) yaagiyoy. 
Ohettay xaafidobati bantta giddon oyqqidobatanne eta asaayfo aattiyoo yoho. Ay medhdhi xaafuwaanikka issi dogettana bessennabay utettaanne ohettan dummayidi be'ana bessennaagaa aybissi giikko era oosuwan aadhdhanawu xeyettida qofaa I aadhdhanaadan koyettidabaa A utettay kuwyyees/ woykko utettaynne attana koyettid qofay shaahetti xeelettokkona lemias issi qofay aaho birshshettan qonccidi xaafettanaadan koyetikko yeda xifatiyaan xaakttana danddayees. I aaho birshshettaa koyyiyaa yoho gidiyoo gishshatawu xaafanchchay yooshshi qoppidi A utettay ayba hamotan gidana bessiyaakko kuuyyees giyoogaa Ha ogiyaan ufettaynne ohettay he mero- oosuwaadan naa''ay issippe keehi maayettidi, issoy issuwaappe darennan guuxxennan lagge shaahoy baynnan biyaaba. Leemisuwassi keehi dara qonccissuwan zuleyiyoobati daro corabaa denttiiddi takkiyoo hanotatussi, aakki aakki hara yohotakka yeliyaa allaalliyaassi qantta medhdhi xaafo utettay inetenna ixxana danddayees. Keehi aaho huuphe yohota aattanawu adussa medhdhi xaafo utettay doorettees. Issi keehi xuntta huuphe yohuwaa keehi aassidinne adussidi xaafiyoogee borssoba. Hegaadan hanana bessenna. Keehi yiira na'i (8 laytta na'i) ba aawaa kkotiyaa mayiyoo wode aara baana/ lo'ana danddayenna. Sa'aara gooshettidi zammaanaba kiyees. Hegaakka mala giyoogaa. Hegaa gishshawu utettay ay mala oosoy ay mala ogiyaan uttanaakko/ aadhdhanaakko kuyyees. Yaagidoy hegaassa. 
Danttoy attin medhdhi- xaafuwa gidiinikka chii- medhdhi- xaafoy aadhdhiyoo utettay yeeta xifatiyaa hanotaana. Tumaa odikko nu timirttiyan qanttanne adussa medhdhi- xaafota xeellanaassi koyyido gishshatawu denttidappe attin yeda xifatiyaay xaafettiyaa hara cora medhdhi- xaafo qammoti de'oosona. 
Medhdhi- xaafota eta qommuwan qommuwan shaakanaayyo daro xeelettiyaabati de’oosona medhdhi xaafoti denttiyoo huuphe yohon, bantta ohettan woykko bantta giddon oyqqidiban, xaafiyoo hiillan woykko utettan shauhettoosona. Ha bolla baggaara nuuni be'ido ogetun xeelettidi shaahetti eretti uttida medhdhi xaafo qommotuppe ane kaalliyaageeta be'i kanttoos.

5.2. Medhdhi-xaafo Qommota 
?	Baceessuwaawa medhdhi xaafuwa 
?	Saynissiyaawa medhdhi xaafuwa 
?	Wonjjalaa pilggetta medhdhi xaafuwa 
?	Aligooriyaa 
?	Aadhidaban wudiyaa medhdhi xaafuwa 
Ane ha qommo baggaara yuleyido medhdhi xaafota issuwa issuwa xaaxi waaxo gidiyaa qofaa keallido xeelloos. 
       1. Baceessuwaawa medhdhi – xaafuwa 
Baceessiyaa medhdhi- xaafoy dumma dumma hanotata boriyaa woykko toochchiyaa medhdhi- xaafo. Issi kawotettan, wogan, oosuwan hegaanne hegeeta malatiyaa yohota dumma dumma ogefun borees woykko toochchees. Ba denttido huuphe yohota kawushidi sa'aara goochchiyaa medhdhi xaafo giyoogaa. 
2. Saynisiyaawwa medhdhi xaafuwa
Qoydissiyaawwa medhdhi xaafuwaa giyaagee saynissi yaanne tekinooliijjyyaa dichchaara gayttida hanotan sinttanawu hanana woykko polettana danddayees giidi qoppidobaa asaa kahan wottanawu/ bessanawu xaafiyoo xaafo. Xaafanchchay ha''i wodiyaan awaaninane baynna woykko go'an ppe'ibeenna tekinoollojje mishshaa go'ettana danddayees. Taarikee polettiyoo sohoy taarikiyaa poliyaabati woykko eeshshaawuat. taarikiyaa giddon go'an pee'iyaa miishshati ubbay hachchin gididi nabbabbiyaa/ be'iyaa asawu zammaana/ ooratta gidana danddayoosona. Aybissi giikko hachchin de'iyaa eraappe woykko ha''i wodiyaan de'iyaa dichchay gakkibeenna xekkaa kantti biida ooratta saynissyaa eran sinttanawu hanana/ po'ettana giyoo ooratta pilggettaa bessees. Hegaassa A sunttaadankka saynisiyaawwa medhdhi xaafo geetettiday. Ha''in de'iyaa asay nabbabbiyoo wode gelennaba malatikkone ha birshshettaadan sinttanaabaa woykko tekinooloojjee gakkana danddayees yaagiiyoo hanotaa giddon gidana koshshees. I medhdhi xaafuwaa giddon haray atto shin issi polettiyaabay hanyooy /polettiyoy ha alamiyan gidenna agganakka danddayees. Leemisuwawu xaafanchchay cora pilaanetetuppe issuwa ekkidi sinttanawu asa na'i aani de'ana danddayees gidi taarikee polettiyoo sohuwa hanno gakkanawu asa na'i de'ibeenna soho oottana danddayees. 
      

                               3. Wonjjalaa pilggettaa medhdhi xaafuwa 
Ha medhdhi- xaafuwy A sunttaadankka xeelliyoo wode I donddo oottidi doommiyoobay issi geeman polettida wonjjalaa/ mooruwaanne A pilggiyoo hanotaa Wonjjalaa oilggettaa medhdhi- xaafuwaa xaafuwaa hiillan issi keehi gita wonjjalay koyro merettees. Ha wonjjalaa polida asa shankkatidi oyqqanawu naaqissiyaa issi mino badee/ xaacee  eeshshaawwadan gelees.                                                      Ha mooranchchaa shaakki eranawu oottiyoo/pilggiyoo hanotan daro geeshsha wonjjalaa oottibeenna asati sirettiyoogan barchchiyaa be'oosona. shin ha taarikiyan nabbabbi yaagee aybanne siribeenna asi woykko wanialaa poliis giidi qoppenna asi wonjjalaa polida asa gididi pilggida badiyaa baqqaara kuuyettees. Wurssettan naagettibeenna wurssiyoo ogiyaani nabbabbiyaasaa malaalissees. 
4. Aadhdhidaban wudiyaa medhdhi- xaafuwa
Ha aadhdhidaban wudiyaa medhdhi- xaafoy, chii- medhdhi xaafuwaadan tumanne beettiya tumatettata pilggiyoogan shaahetti erettana danddayiyaa cuccumettiyaa/ beettiyaa naqaashaa shiishshenna. Ha hani aadhdhidaban wudiyaa medhdhi xaafoy tumuppekka hanidi/ polettida hanotata baaso oottidi denddees. Gido shin ha tumu polettidabati puulattidinne orddidi beettanaadan medhdhidi gujjiyoobinne xoqqissiyoobi xayenna. Xaafiyaagee bariyyo siyettida sissaa gujjidi go'ettiyoo qaalatakka medhdhi xaafo malatissees. Xaafiyaasee Issibay polettiyoo wode de'ibeenna asata, 
Polettibeennabata, baynna wodiyaanne qatuwa ( woqa) medhdhidi gujjana danddayees. Aaadhdhidaban wudiyaa medhdhi- xaafon xoqqissoy woykko gujoy beettikkonne awu baasoy tumuppe hanidaban woykko polettidaban baaso gidees giyoogaa. 
                                          5. Aliigooriyaa 
Ha medhdhi xaafoy bari meraa bilan qosanne qoncce gididi mentte birshshettaa oyqqanaadan oosettidi xaafettees. I qassi barigiddon ammanuwaa, ayissuwaabaa (politics) woykko hara asaa maabara de’uwan denddana danddayiyaabata xaaxi oyqqiyaa medhdhi- xaafo. 

Ha no bolla baggaara be’ido medhdhi- xaafo qommotuppe haratikka corati de’oosona. Hanno gakkanawu nuuni be’ido medhdhi xaafo macarati bantta ohettan, utettan, xaafiyoo hiillan shaahetti uttidaageta. Eta yesuwan be’iyaaba gidikko qantta woykko asussa gididi shiiqana danddayees. 

Meezziyaa issuwa
    Kaallidi de'iyaa oyshatussi gamma gidiyaa zaaruwaa immite.
1) saynissiyaawa medhdhi- xaafuwaninne aadhdhidabaa bolli wudiyaa 
   medhi- xaafuwaa giddon de’iyaa gita dummutettaa qonccissada yoota. 
2) Adussa medhdhi xaafoynne qantta medhdhi xaafoy malatettiyoo 
   eeshshata hara xombbe maxaafatakka nabbabbada qantta xuufiyaa shishshite. 
3) Baceessuwaawwa medhdhi- xaafoy daro wode ay mala yohotun wudii?

                   4.1. Adussa medhdhi xaafuwaa eeshshata 
Kaalettiyaa oyshata 
1) Adussa medhdhi- xaafuwaa giyoogee aybee? 
2) Hagaappe kase ay doonaaninne issi adussa medhdhi xaafuwaa nabbabidetii? A huuphe 
     yohuwaanne taarikkiyaa xaaxi waako hanotan intte laggetussi kifile giddon shaakkite. 
3) Adussa medhdhi- xaafoy ay mala ogiyaan xaafettiyaa xuufee? 

   Mero oosota xaafanchchay bari kahaappe medhdhidi, guuggiyaappe pulttissidi shiishshiyoo era 
   ooso gidikkonne etawu denddoy tumanne beettiyaa asa na'aa de'o. Asaa na'aa galla galla 
   de'iyaa gaytotettan, asaaninne meretaa giddona oosettiiyaa gaytotettan merettiy aabatikka 
   medhdhi xaafotun qonccoosona. Eti asaa na'aa de'uwaa zaari bessiyaa denddoynne wurssettay 
   ha alamiyaa asaa de'uwan polettiyaaba. Ha bollan nu giido eeshshay adussa medhdhi- 
   xaafuwawu qassikka qantta medhdhi xaafuwawukka hanees. Eti naa''u bila xifateti woykko 
   medhdhi xaafoti naa''awukka denddoy asaa na'aa de'uwaa gidishin, naa''aykka xaafettiyoy 
   yedaana. Eti naa''aykka bantta giddon eeshshaawwdtanne hiillata kunttidi oyqqoosona. Tumaa 
   maayidi naa''u medhdhi- xaafatukka puulaa maayidi xhllqoosona. Na naa''u medhdhi- 
   xaafotakka xaafiyaa xaafanchchatussi issi mala xaafiyoo meezzee woykko aazzee de'ees 
   giyoogaa. Gido shin, bantta ohettaaninne utettan etawu dummatettay de'ees. Ha dummatettata 
    kaallidi xeellana. Ane koyrottidi adussa medhdhi- xaafuwaa xeelloos. 
Beni wodiyaan keehi erettidinne aahuwan xaafettida medhdhi- xaafaya oromansiya (romanee) yaagettiyaa xaapo. Ha oromansiyaa medhdhi- xaafuwaappe dariyaa xaafiyoo hiillan daro eeshshaawwata bari giddon oyqqidi orattatettan yiidaagee ingliizattuwan “ Novel” geetettiyaa ha adussa medhdhi- xaafuwaa. He wodiyaappe doommidi bari oorattatettaa eeshshaa dichchidi, pacciyaabaa gujjiiddi, moonettiddbaa giigissiddi diccidi hachchin de’iyaa meray utettaanne taauwaa hiillaa oyqqiis. 

Medhdhi- xaafoy nu biittaa toophphiyaa doomettidoy woykko yiidoy haaho gidenna/ mati yiis. Nu biittaa Toophphiyan koyro xaafettida medhdhi-xaafoy “ Xoobbiyaa” geetettees. A qassi xaafidaagee Gabreyesuusa Aforqqa. Ha asa oosoy koyro kochchnooro  gidoogaappe denddidaagan daroba kunttiyaaba gidenna aggana danddayees- aybissi giikko ha oosoy daro meezzetettibeennaba gidiyoo gishshawu. gidoppe attin nu biittaasi hagaa mala oosuwa oottiyaa hara eranchchatussi gita go'aa immana danddayiis. Haratikka qassi ha koyronne denddo gidida oosuwaa be’i simmidi aahuwan puulayidinne kumetta harotan hara cora oosota xaafanawu maa dettidosona. 
Hegaappe simmin issi sha'anne uddufun xeetanne ishatamanttaa heeraappe haa doommiy daro medhdhi- xaafoti cora eranchchatun oosettidoogee erettees. 
Adussa medhdhi – xaafoy hara bila- xifatetudan hara xaafettiyaa oosotuppe dummatiyoo A dumma ceshshati de’oosona. Nabbabbiyaa asati woykko I xaafettido asati naagiyo/ koyyiyoo corabati de'oosona. xaafanchchati hegeeta akeekana bessees. 
Adussa medndhi- xaafoy bari sunttaadanikka bari denttido qofaa aahuwan/adussan birshshiidddi shiishshiyaa medhdhi- xaafo qommo. i bariyyo denddo oottidi denttido qofaa/ huuphe yohuwa aassidinne loytti laalidi ghiishshanaayyo aadussa wodiyaa, aaho sohuwaa koyyiyaa xuufe. I keehi daro sinttan xaafettiyaa, daro tammu sha'atun qoodettiyaa qaalata bari giddon oyqqiyaa aaho era ooso. Adussa medhdhi- xaafuwassi daro laali odiyoo woykko taarikiyaa shemppi shemppidinne utti utti denddidi birshshi bessiyoo hanotay de'ees. Ane adussa medhdhi- xaafuwaa eeshshatuppe amaratu xeelloos: Adussa medhdhixaafuway yeletaappe biidi hayquwa gakkanawu bogettennan woppu giidi yootiya daro birshshettaa immiyaa issi issi tangguwa qonccissidi yootanawunne bessanawu wodeenne sohoy de’yooba. Ha adussa taarikiyaa I zulleyiyoo wode mexi issi hoolle xalaala gidennan malatettiyaa hara hoolletikka de'oosona. 
Ayyo danttuwaadan odanawu woykko aattanawu koyyidobaa qanttan minjjidi aattenna ayyo laalidi aahuwan aattiyoo heenottay aaho. I de'uwaa dumma dumma lo'onne iita gidida yohota shiihshees. Medhdhi xaafuwa eeshshaawati taarikiyaa adussatettaane aahotettaninne payduwan cora. Daro eeshshaawati cora oosota polishin bessiyoo aaho sohoynne wodee de’ees. Eeshshaawatu mule oonatettaa, eti gelidosaa, eti kiydosaa, ha oosoy polettidosaa I qonccissees. Aani minjja/ kulkka gidiyaa tucetti uttida qaalati de’okkena. Hegaa gishshawu xaafanchchay cora qaalata go’ettiditaarisciyaa giddon po’ettiddabata loytti miccidi bessees. I Qantta gidana mala xaafiyaage koyyenna. Eeshshaawati issi sohuwaappe hara sohuwaa kantti kanttidi taarikiyaa poloosona. Ha eeshshaawatuyyo garssa qofaynne boua hanoy aybakko nabbobbiyaagawu qoncce gididabaa misilees. Eeshshhaawati cora meto gurssaara kanttidi eti baxetiyoo baaxiyaa, olettiyoo olaa, etayyo xube gidiyaabaa giddo gelissiiddinne kessiiddi woppu oottidi birshshi birshshidi zuleyees. Ha adussa medhdhi xaafoy nabbabbiyaagaassa gidiinikka eeshshaawatuyyo bessennane 

koyettenna birshshettaa immiidi utteana. Nabbabbiyaagee oychchana danddayiyoobata, birshshettaa koyyiyoobata laalidinne qonccissidi yootees. 
Adussa medhdhni-xaafuwan polettidabatinne gaasotu ayfeetu issoy issuwara oyqettiiddi qoshettiiddi, daayyiiddinne aakkiiddi taarikiyaa wurssettaa gakkanawu injjetidinne  minnidi bees. Issi youwaa medhdhidi ayyo birshshettaa koyyiiddi. qassikka hara metuwaa medhdhidi A aassiiddi, laa’issiiddi macaraa kessiiddi bees. Adussa medhdhi- xaafuwaussi taarikiyaa issuwa issuwara ohettay keeri aahonne adussa. Eeshshaawatu paydoykka coranne malatettiyaa sima huuphe yohoti keehi cora gididoogaappe denddidaagan A giddon daro barbbuqettati de’oosona hegaappe denddidaagan cora karssi karssay merettees. Ha karssikorssaappe kessi ekkanawu eeshshaawati haniyoobaanne oottiyoo malaa ha oosoy loddu giidi shemppi shemppi ekkidi bessees. 

Hara eeshshay qassi ayyo issi hoolle xalaala gidennan hara cora hoolleti de’oosona aybissi giikko ayyo cora eeshshaawati taarikiyaa giddon de’iyoo gishshataassa. Hegaappe donddidaagan ha medhdhi- xaafoy adussanne aaho. Ha cora payduwan daro gididu eeshshaawati dumma dumma dere asaa kifiliyaappe shiiqiyoo gishshatawu dumma dumma dere asaa de’uwaa duussaa, wogaa iita hanuwa nne lo’o hanuwa aassidi besseesona. Hegaa gishshawu huuphe gidiyaa ano cuccumaappe kareera hara sima cuccumati merettoosona. Eti ha ano issi gita cuccumaappe dummatoosona siisnin ano cuccumaara aybinne gattiyaabi baa giyoogaa gidenna. Eti issi ogiyaaninne gidin hara ogiyaan ano cuccumaara daro gayttiyaanne A gasttissiyaageeta. 

Woqa dooruwankka adussa medhdhi- xaafoy taarikiyaa aaho manttiyaaninne wodiyan shiishshiyoogee ayyo eeshsha. Eeshshaawata wodiyan shiishshiyoogee ayyo eeshsha. Eeshshaa wata issi sohuwaappe hara sohuwawu yuushshi yuushshidi oosoti polettanaadan oottees. Ha taarikiyaa bariyaaka koyyikko keehi qantta qassi ixxikko keehiadussa oottidi bessana danddayees. 

Xaafiyoo hiillaa xeelliyaagan xaafanchchay taari kiyaa aahotettaappe denddidaagan dumma dumma oohotun aahuwan gelissiidi go'ettana danddayees. Zaaretti zaarettidikka aahuwan shiishshanawu qaaday aaho. 
Oduwa onttaa ( ooni) xeelliyaagan xaafanchchay issi bari koyyido onttaa xalaalaa dooridi koyyikko qassi walakkidi taarikiyaa giddon haniyaabaa woykko polettiyaabaa shohhayidi aattanawu A maatay naagettidaagaa. Adussa medhdhi xaafuwan taarikiyaa dumma dumma baggaara shiishshana danddayettees. Hegaa gishshawu issi medhdhi- xaafuwa xaafiyaa eranchchay taarikiyaa giddo gelidi hashetana danddayees woykko taarikiyaappe ubba kareera gididi xeellana danddayes woykko koshshikko issitoo gelana woykko kiyana danddayees. Hagaa xaafiyagee kuuyyees. Doonaa go’an eesonne qantta geetettiyaa yesitun xeelliyoo wode adussa medhdhi- xaafoy eesonne qantta gidenna. Hegaa gishshawu I keehi aaho eeshshawatunne qatuwaa birshshetta immees. Ane issi leemisuwaa hagaara oywettidaagan xeellos. Leemisuwassi Burunjje Bungge yetta danttuwan taayyo akeekettenna ixxida yettaassi koyro naa”u yataranxxoti de’oosona. hegeetikka; 
    “ Gattan toggiyaa gaammoy 
    Gaammuwaa yeliyaa maahee……..” 
Ha”I nuuni tobbiiddi de’iyoy danttuwaabaa gidana xayikkonne medhdhi- xaafoy qanttanne eeso gidenna yaasiyaagan amppidi guutta akeekaa demmoos. Ha bolla naa''u yafaranxxo xalaalati de’iyoo danttuwa geliwan “ gattan toggiyaa gaammoy,” yaagees. Ha yafaranxxuwa birshshettaa akeekanawu ishaa Bungga oychchaas. Ikka yaagidi zaariis. Beni wodiyaan nu aawati shankkaa shankkatoosona- mata heeraappe doommido. Kase 
wodiyaan guutta baratu giddonkka cora dumma dumma qummo do’ati de’oosona. Akeekite, baraa gidddon daro qommo do’ati geessoosona: Gaammoy, harddiiday, suylaalee, zeerusay, horppiina godariyaa gakkanawu giyoogaa. Shankkaassi keehi xoqqa xekkaa gakkina koyyiyaa asi “ bootta gattaa ( Nech xar) gakkanawu paraa toggi shankkatiidi simmees. “ yaagiis. 
Hegaappe simmin he bootta gattan toggida (shankkatida) asa asay woraabees. Aybissi giikko he bootta gattan de’iyaa do’aasi zawideena. Gidikkonne he asi keehi wolqqaamanne eranchcha gididoogaappe denddidaagan he shouwaa gakkanawu biidi shankkatiis giyoogaa. Hegaa gishshawu ha asi A gakkiyay baynna Gadaawa. I keehi wolqqaama asa giyoogaa. Kase asay haasayiiddi woykko gereeeriidi.
              “Gattan toggiyaa minoy baawa 
               Gaammuwa yeliyaa maahee baawa, 
Yaagees giidi taayyo qonccissuwaa immiis. Ha birshshettaa taani nu ishaa oychchennaakko eranaagee daro meto. I bar huuphiyawu ha yafaranxxuy daro asaa keehi metanaagaa akeekiis. Hagaamalabay adussa medhdhi- xaafuwan polettenna. Aybissi giikko, I eesonne qantta gidenna. I issi issibaa keehi laalidi dooyidi Aabbabbiyaagaa akeekissees. Hegaappe denddidaagan eeshshaawati bantta giddon yaa haa haasayettiyoo aaho qaadaa demmoosona. Hegaa gishshin ayyo haasayanawu sohoy, wodeenne, shenee de’iyoo gishshatawu hanenna haasayaa zaaretuwan woykko essiyoosi erettenna palamaa giddo eeshsha wata yeggidi aggi be’enna. Aattiiddi de’iyoo taarikiyaassi maado immenna, odoy sinttawu sinttawu coo gogganaadan oottiya, woykko nabbabbiyaagaa saletissiyaanne taarikiyawu puulaa xayssiya birshshetta immenna. Na bbabbiyaagaa saletissenna ogiyan eeshshaawata haasayisseesnne nabbabbiyaa izaawi denttana danddayiyoo oyshshata zaarees lo’iyaanne puulay de'iyoo laaletta birshshettaa oottees. 

                   Meezziyaa Naa''aa 
Kaallidi de'iyaa oyshata waattan waattan gididi tobboogaappe guyiyan gamma zaaro gidiyaagaa xaafidi intte asttamaariyanttussi sheedhdhanaappe kasetidi intte kifile laggetussi qonccissite. 
1) Adussa medhdhi xaafuwaa giyoogee Aybee? Intte qofaa kayan kayan qonccissite. 
2) Adussa medhdhi xaafuwan cora eeshshaawati beettiyoogawu ayba maadoy de'ees giidi 
     qoppeetii? Birshshidi yootite. 
3) Adussa medhdhi xaafoy keehi aahonne assi daro hoolleti de'oosona giishin woyganawu 
     koyettidaakko qonccissuwaa immite. 
4) Adussa medhdhi- xaafuwan go'ettiyoo doonaynne qantta medhdhi xaafuwan go'ettiyoo 
    hanotay aybin dummatana danddayiyaakko qonccissite. 
5) Hagaappe kase wodiyaan intte qommoora be'ido medhdhi xaafotuppe ay doonaaninne gido 
    nabbabbidi be'idobi de'ii? Intte laggetuura tobbite. 

5.3. Qanttanne adussa medhdhi xaafotu eeshshata
Tobbiyoo oyshata. 
-	Qantta medhdhi- xaafoy adussa medhdhi- xaafuwaappe aybin dummatees giidi qoppeetii? 
-	Qantta medhdhi xaafuwa eeshshati adussa medhdhi xaafo eeshshatuppe daro dummstoosona giidi qoppeetii? Aybin aybin dummatiyoonaa aybin aybin malatettiyoonaa? 
-	Hagaappe aadhdhida wodiyan ay doonaaninne gido issi qantta medhdhi xaafuwaa nabbabbideti? A kifille giddon intte laggetussi odidi sissite. 
Qantta medhdhi- xaafoy bari sunttaadankka adussa medhdhi- xaafuwaappe guuxxiyaanne xuntta gidiyaa xaafo gidiyoogaa bessees. Ayyo utettaa gidinkka ohettaa xunttetettay de'iyooga A sunttaappe akeekana danddayettees. Ha qantta medhdhi xaafuwaa koyro medhdhidaage Alamppo Edgaara gidishin I Amerkka biittaa asa. I qantta medhdhi- xaafuwaa yuushuwan corabaa oottida eranchcha. Nu biitti yiyoo wode qassi ha qantta medhdhi-xaafoy mata wode merettidaba woykko yiidaba. Qantta medhdhi-xaafuwa aybatettaa xeelliyaagan hara era oosotuyyo de'iyaa birshshettatuppe dummatidi qoncce gididan birshshetti de'iyooba gidenna. I bila xifatiyaadan, danttuwaadaninne adussa medhdhi xaafuwaadan dumma dumma xaafanchchatudan dumma dumma birshshettaa ekkees. Xaafanchchati banttawu de'iyaa xeelaadan, akeekaadan, bantta de'uwaadan h.h.m. dumma hanotatuura gattidi dumma dumma birshshettata immoosona.  Dumma dumma ogiyaan leemisuwawu I oyqqiyoo qaalatu payduwaadaninne shociyoo hoolliyaadan xeellidi hagee qantta medhdhi- xaafo hagee qassi adussa medhdhi xaafo goosona. 

Ha qofaa sihettanaayyo danddayettennaba gidikkonne ane daro eranchchati denttiyoo eeshshata ekkidi issippetettay de'iyoosaa gum''idi be'oos. Mayzzenna ano yohotun pacamiyoogaappe mayzziyaanne ano eeshsha gidiyaabata denttiyooge lo''o oge malatees. Hagaa xeelliyaagan Asfaa Zarihun shiishshiiyoo qofaa. 

   Hanno gakkanawu denddida qantta medhdhi 
   xaafuwaa birshshettati dariyaa baggan 
   shiiqi uttidaageeta gidiyoogee beettees. 
   ooni eri dummatetti de'ikkonne qoncciss
   uwaa immiyoo ogiyaaninne issoy aass 
   idi haray qassi xunttidi birshshiy oosaana. 
   gido shin ubba birshshettatikka qantta 
   medhdhi- xaafoy hara bila- xifate qomm-
   otuppe dummatidi erettiyoo eeshshata 
    qonccissidi bessoosona. 
    (Asfaa zarihuna /1998:229)
Xaaxiwaaxo qofaappe, hara huuphe yohotuppenne A utettaappenne ohettaappe denddidi qantta medhdhi xaafuwa eeshshato zuleyiyoogeenne hara medhdhixaato oosotuppe dummatiyoo anobuta maxi kessana danddayettees. Qantta medhdhi xaafuwaa eeshshata waayettennan akeekanawu kose guyye baggaara be'ido adussa medhdhi xaafuwaara gatti xeelliyoogea keha. Adussa medhdhi xaafuwan be'ido daro eeshshati ha qantta medhdhi xaafuwaa giddon de’enna aggana danddayiyoo gishshatawu qonccissuwaa immanawu lo'o qaada. Ane ha qantta medhdhi- xaafo eeshshata giyoogeeta kayan kayan birshshidi xeelloos. 

Qantta medhdhi xaafoy adussa medhdhi- xaafuwaadan laalidinne birshshi bessiyaaba gidenna. I danttuwaappe kaallidi danttuwaadan eeso, bari giddon darobaa oyqqiyaabanne minjja gidana xaykkonne danttuwaappe sima gidida ogiyaan qantta medhdhi-xaafoy eeso, A giddon de'iyaa qaalati bantta giddon corabaa oyqqiyaabanne minjja. I asussa medhdhi- xaafuwaadan issi issi suuppanne laafa gidida qofaassi wode immidi laali laali odanawu ayyo wodeenne sohoy de’enna. Aani qaalatu bessenna go'ettoynne taarikiyaa woppu gtidi shemppi ekkiiddi yootiyoo hanoti mulekka baawa. I biddiiddi yaagaa haagaabaa birshshiiddi takkiyaaba gidenna. I daro adussa wodiyawu nabbabbiyaage uttidi wodiyaa aattiyooba gidennan issi utettan nabbabbettidi wuriyaa xaafo ooso.
Qantta- medhdhi xaafoy qantta wodiyaaninne sohuwan bari taarikiyaa baasoyidi poliyaaba gidikkonne I bariyyo woykko wogan kumettappe attin qantta medhdhi- xaafo geetettiyoo gishshawu paca giyoogaa gidenna woykko qofay kumetta gidenna gqanaassa gidenna. 
Qantta medhdhi xaafoy adussa medhdhi- xaatuwaappe qanxxetti kiyidaba gidenna. Adussa medhdhi xaafuwa qanxxidi qanttawu laammana danddayettenna. Qantta medhdhi xaafuwaakku ywdidi woykko aassidi adussa medhdhi- xaafo oottana danddayettenna. I bari meran xaafeettidi ayyo ayyo bessiyaaba ubbay kumetta gidido. Kumetta gidido cuccumay de'iyoo ooso. Ha naa''u adussanne qantta medhdhi- xaafotu giddon de'iyaa dommatettay utettaanne bari garssan oyqqiyoo baappe attin issi qofaa aattiyoonne aattennaaagaana gidenna. Toti naa''aykka bantta eeshshaa asaanne asaa de'uwan de'iyaa dumma dumma yohota lagge bessiyoo wolqqay de'ees. Issi issi qantta xifate oosoti aduqqiyoogaadan woykko adussa xifatetu qaocaccamma qaammidi xaafettiyoogaadan qanttanne adussa medhdhni xaafoyqaammannanne aduqqana danddayenna. Issi medhdhi- xaafuwaa aduqissidi woykko qanttidi oottana malikko ctan beettanaadan koyettida mucurati woykko huuphe yohoti moorettana woykko balettana danddayees. Taarike muleera baassi de'iyaa meraa xayana danddayees. Ane qantta medhdhi- xaauwaa eeshshata kaallidi xeeuoos. Qantta medhdhi- xaafoy bari eeshshan eeson gidiyoo gishshatawu bari bootiyoo taarikiyaa harddofidi/ woxxidi eesuwan puluwaa gattees. Adussa medhdhi- xaafuwaadan keehi loddu giidi gooshshettiiddi wodiyaa ekkenna. Hegaassa qammo baggara issi utettan wurana danddayiyaa era ooso giidoy. 

Qantta medhdhi taafoy adussa medhdhi- xaafuwaadan taarikiyaa giddon palettiiddi de'iyaabaa dendduwaappe woykko yeletaappe biidi poluwaa/ has quwaa gakkanawu de'iyaaba ubbaa biddennaane shemppisremppi ekkidi A yootiiddi takkenna. Ano eeshshaawa gidiyaa issi aso dooridi qantta medhdhi- xaafoy A bolli wudiyoo gishshatawu bogettiiddi taarikiyaa wurssanawu eesotees. Ayyo mexi issi hoolliyaa shochcha xalaalappe attin hara miyyiyaara merettiya mara gidiyaabi baynna gishshatawu ayyo shiiqi uttida guutta ohettay de'ees giyoogaa. 

Qantta medhdhi- xaafoy meretan muttimuretti uttida kaalli kaalli yiyaa cora gaasonne wurssetta ayfe gidiyaa ohetti uttidabata adussa medhdhi- xaafuwaadan oyqqenna. Payduwan keehi guutta gidida bantta eeshshankka mino gidida ohetti uttida oosoti/ polettiyaabati jaamiiddi naagettiyaa mexiissi hoolliyaakko gakkidi essi aggoosona. Teixxa gididi qoncciyaan baettiyaa polettiyaabata ekkidi etawu polo issippetettaa immiiddi taarikiyaa giddon merettida issi metuwaalsi ogiyaa/birshshettaa demmidi bari taarikiyaa poliaggees. 

Qantta medhdhi xaafuwa cuccumay mexi issuwa. Bari yesuwan guutta gididi horddofiyaa ha medhdhi xaafuwaassi issuwaappe attin ara sima cuccumati de'okkona. Hara mara cuccumata I oyqqiyaaba gidikko A qanttatettaappe daridi a meeray mooretti aggees. I adussa medhdhi xaafuwaadan ano ceccumaa malatiya hara sima cuccumata oyqqenna. Hegee ayyo eeshsha gidenna. 
Eeshshaawata xeelliyaagan qantta medhdni xafoy adussa medhdhi xaafuwaadan kahi cora eeshshaawata koyyenna. Dere asaa shiishshidi abaa abaamaganniiddi wode ekkenna. I bari qanttatataadan guuttaa eeshshaawata bari taarikiyan go'ettees. Ha eeshshaawati payduwan guuxxkkonne bantta kiyido/ yiido deriyaa bessanawu etu paamanettiyaageeta. Eti payduwan guuxxiyoogee eta aybippenne diggenna. Woykko eti payduwan guutta gidiyoo gishshatawu etawu pacciyaabi baawa. Hegaa gishshatawu qanttamedhdhi xaafoy guutta eeshshaawata ekkidi ba aattanawu koyiddo kiitaa woykko huuphe yohuwa ha taarikiyan giddon hemetissees giyoogaa. Ha eeshshawatu banttawu imettida guutta soheen wodeen, etawu imettida issi de'uwaaninne mexiguutta taarikiyaa polanawu yaa haa qaaxxiyaageeta gidiyoogan qantta nedhdhi xaafoy minjjanne eesuwan polettiyaabagidiyoo gishshatawu ha eeshshaawati hauenna banbbuqettaaninne cabbo giddo gelidi baa xetana mala koyettenna. Hanennanne wurenna adussa taarikoyan gelcnna mala giyoogaa. Ha medhdhi – xaafuwan eeshshaawati mexi issi meto giddo gelidi appe kessiekkanawu baaxetiyoo hanota xalaalaa beessana keshshees. I adussa medhdhi xaafuwaadan eeshshaawataya metuwaan ha metuwan gelissidi bantta oosuwa polana mala oottenna. Issi keehi koshshiyaa yoho gidana xayikko hegaa yootiiddi wode aattenna. Ayyo mexi issi taarikeenne hoollee de'iyoo gishshawu payduwan issi woykko naa''u eeshshaawati ootti poliyoo taarike gidana danddayees. 

Qantta medhdni xafuwa woqay guutta. Qantta medhdhi xaafoy adussa medhdhi- xaafuwaadan eeshshaawata issi biittaappe harabiittawunne yuushshiiddi uttennanne taarikiyaakka hayquwa gakkanaashin dentti denttidiyootenna. Ha taarikee takkiyoo wodeenne I polettiyoo qatoy qatoy guutta. Qantta medhdhi xaatoy ba doommido taarikiya he doommido sohuwan polana besseesinne taarikiyaakka shombbayennan qanttidi yootees. Issi medhdhi xaafy qantta medhdhi xaafo geetettanawu taarikee doomettido sohuwan polana besseesinne qantta wodiyan taarikiyayooti polana bessees. 

Qantta medhdhi xaafwan adussa medhdhi xaafuwaadan eeshshaaway banaara woykko hara asaara woykko hara gishsha/muunne gidida baara yootettan danddayees. Hegaa giyoogee qantta medhdhi xaafuwan karssikarssay naa''u ogiyan denddana danddayees hegeetikka asi baanaara dom”ettiyoogaanne asi harabaarawoykko hara asaara dom”ettiyoo hanotaa. Korssikarssaa xeelliyaa hanotan guutta ano gididaban palamettiiddi woykko baaxetiiddi takkennan eesuwaarakka umbbubuettaakko gatti aggees. Karssikarssay maraa yeli yelidi haa cori coridi beenna. Taarikoyaa poliyaageeti issi xon”a palamaa woykko baaxiya giddo geli simmidi taarikee bogettiyoo gishshawu sohunkearakka he palamaappe/baaxiyaappe kiyidi sohuwaarakka polama/ xiyaa gidissana koshshe. 
Taari kiyaa giddon eeshshaaway issi tubiyaappe koyidi haraa metuwan/xubiyan gelana bessenna. Olaa kessinne, he yohuwaa sohuwaarakka umbbubuoettaakko gattidi eesuwan qassikka lekkane'u waakyo gdttiyoogee qanttamedhdhi xaafuwaassi bayra eeshsha. 

Qantta medhdhi xaafuwan doonaa go'etuwa xeelliyaagan eeshshaawatu haasayaykka gidin xaafanchchaa birshshettay siita gidana bessees. Daro laalidi adusa qonccissuwa immiyoogee qantta medhdhi xaafo gidennaa gishshatawu guutta doorettida qonccissiyaa siqintta qaalatun shiishshees. Eeshshaawati attana danddayenna keehi go’iyaanne koshshiyaa yohotu xalaalan haasayana /qofaa laammana/ mala oottana bessees. Wodiyaa coo xuuggiyaane taarikiyawu maado immenna shanddaa shaaraa eeshshanwati haasayanaaden oottana bessenna. Xaatanchchaykka hanennabanne nabbabbiyan asa maaddena ban leernisuwassi eeshshaawwaa meraa, geesaa A garssa eeshshaa birshshana bessenna. Qantta medhdhi- xaafoy kushshiyaabata xalaalaa qonccissi oessidi eesotiti powwaa gattanawu bana siitees. Hagaa gishshawu qantta medhdhi- xaatuwa doonaa go'ettiyoo hanotay siita. 
Yootuwa woykko xaafuwa onttaa xeelliyaagan ubba ontta qommotun go'ettan danddayettees. Gido shin adussa medhdhi- xaafuwaadan issi taarikiyaa giddon ubba ontta qommota laammi laammi go'ettanawu qantta medhdhi xaafuwaa eesoynne un''o hanoy injjetenna. Hegaa gishshawu onttaa qommotuppe xaafanchchay issuwa xalaalaa dooridi go’ettanaadan eranchchati zoroosona. Medhi- xaafuwa xaafiyoo hiillaa xeelliyaagan qantta medhdhi- xaafoy ubba qommo hiillata go'ettana danddayees. Gido shin adussa medhdhi xaafuwaadan bariyyo injjetidaadan aassiiddinne darissennan zaaretti zaarettidi go'ettanawu taarikiya wottaynne A utettaa hanotay yeddenna gishshawu un''onne qantta hanotaa go'ettana danddayees. 
                       Meezziya Heezzaa 
Kaallidi de’iyaa oyshata heezzan heezzan gididi tobbi simmidi oyshtussi gamma zaarota immite. 
1. Qantta medhdhi- xaafoy siqintta, siitanne eeso giida. Hagaa danttuwa 
   eeshshaara gatti xeellidi kuuyite. 
2. Qantta medhdhi- xaafuwassi mexi issi hoollee de’iyoo xuufe yaagiyaa qofaa adussa medhdhi 
    xaafuwaara geeddarissidi qonccissi yootite. 
3. Qantta medhdhi xaafoy adussa medhdhi xaafuwaappe qanxx/ cukki ekkoba gidana danddayees 
     giidiqoppeetii? Birshshidi qntte kifile laggetussi qonccissite. 
4) Hagaappe qommoora nu taamaariichchido  huuphe yohotun: adussanne qantta medhdhi 
   xaafotun medhdhi xaafuwa ufurettata be'ida. Ha medhdhi- xaafo ufurettata ha qonccisso 
   nibaabiyaappe maxi kessidi zuleyite. 
5) Issi inttena lo'ida huuphe yohuwaa dooraappe guyyiyaan issi  ichchshaappe darenna sinttan/ 
    yeechchan issi qantta medhdhi- xaafuwaa xaafidi intte asttamaariyaanttussi shiishshanaappe 
    kasetidi kifile giddon intte laggetussi nabbabbite. Appe tamaare naati ay cuccumaa 
     demmiyaakkonne oychchite. 
       5.4. Medhdhi – xaafuwa ufurettatanne hiillata
Ha qommo huuphe yohuwa be'anaappe kasetidi ane ha kaallidi de'iyaa oyshata heezzaa heezzaa oyqqida citan gididi tobboos. 
1) Ufurettata giyaa qaalaassi birshshettay aybee? 
2) Medhdhi xaafuwaa ufurettata giyoogeeti aybee aybee? 
3) Ha ufurettati medhdhi xaafuwawu ay go'a immoosona giid qoppeetii? 
4) Medhdhi xaafuwa hiillata giyoogeet aybatee? 
5) Medhdhi xaafuwaa ufurettatinne medhdhi xaafuwaa hiillatu giddon dummatetti de'ii? 
        
Asa na'a de'uwan dumma dumma hanotatinne, baaxee, tuggay waayee kumi uttiis. A de'uwan I koyyiyoobay A eeshshay de'iyaa cora gayttiyaabati de'oosona. xifate ooseotussikka baasoy asa na'aa de'uwan gayttiyaa dumma dummabata. Asa na'i dumma dumma batura leemisuwawu asi banaara. Bari moottaara asi asaara, asi meretaara gayttiyoo. Hanotatun merettiyaabaa xaafanchchay xaafees. Hagaappe denddidi issi xaafanchchay bana ufoyssida ayba yohuwanikka xaafana danddayees. Ha hanotan xaafanchchay aybibaa xaafoo giidi oychchiyoogaappe waata xaafoo yaagidi bana oychchana bessees abissi giikko

Ay huuppe yohuwaakka doorana danddayees. Hegee bessiis. Daro Ooratta huuphe yohotikka doorettana danddayoosona. Gidoppe attin aazee baynna ay asinne huuphe yohay besso gishshatawu awudenne awaaninne ekkidi xanti aggana danddayees giyoogaa gidenna. Meezzee de’iyoo xaafanchchaa. Gidinkka ha cora huuphe yohotuppe I keehi birshshi xaafana danddayiyoo bariyyo keehi erettiyaa huuphe yohuwa dooridi he qofan xaafees. Xaafiiddikka xaafiyoo hiillaanin loytti qoppana bessees. Issi xifatiyaa /medhdhi xaafuwa bessiyaa ogiyaan waati xaafidi nabbabbiyaagee ufayttanaadan dumma dumma hiillaa loyttidi bessana danddayetti giyppana bessees. 
Medhdhi xaatuwa ufurettatu hiillaa / tekinkiyaa geetettiyaaseeti issi xuufuya/ dirssatiyaa xaafanawu danddayissiyaabatanne giigissiyoo oqeta Eti ay medhdhi xaafuwa giddonkka beettana bessiyaanne xaafanchchati geissana bessiyaa geliyoo hiillati muleera xaafuwassi baaso gidana danddayiyaa miishshata. Ufurettatinne tekinketi/ xaafo hiillati issi medhdhi xaafoy ay ogiyaan xaafettin, ay dere asaa de'uwa yuushuwan simerettin ay aaho woykko xuntta gidin ha naa''u yohota bari giddon oyqqana bessees. Xaafyaagaa eray, medhdhi xaafuwaa puulaynne cinatettay hegaadankka nabbabbiyaagee he oosuwan ufayttiyoo hanota ubbay ha baaso gidiyaa tekinikiyaa/ xaafo hiillaa go'aana. 
Medhdhi xaafuwa ufurettatunne xaafiyoo hiillati woykko/ tekiniketu go'ay xaafettiyaa medhdhi- xaafuwudan sinqenttanne siitua dummatettay de'ikkonne ubba xuuto oosotun/dirsatetu giddon beettees. Leemisuwassi issi dirssate oosuwaa berinashuwaa wodekka koyruwan xeelettiyay ufurettatanne tekiniketa. Kaallidi eta aybatettaa go'aanne eti bila xifatiyawu immiyoo maaduwa xaaxi- waaxo gidida ogiyaan be'ana. 
Medhdhi- xaafuwassi ufurettati attana danddayenna keehi xoshshiyaaba. Eti ay dirssate oosotu giddonikka gelidi beettana bessiyaa xaafanchchayka akeekidi go'ettana bessiyaa medhdhi- xaafuwaappe paccana bessenna baaso gididaba. Ha ayfe gididabatun bari oosuwa minttidi essana danddayees. Leemisuwaassi issi keettaa keexxanawu koshshiyaabata ekkoos. Issi wolaytta keettaa keexxanawu: Godaa, meegaa, tuussaa, sussaa, zanddidaa, hootaa (zleaissi keettaa keexxanawu keehi koshshiyaaba. Issoy pacciichchikko haray A sohuhlan eqqidi/gididi hankkuwaa sohuwa kammana danddayenna. Heemmisuwaassi gattay pacciyaaba gidiyaakko gattaa sohuwan haray uttidi iraappe keettaa ashshana danddayehna. Issi issibaa duussa keettaa keexettawu woykko keettay keexetti wuranawu keehi koshshiyaaba. Ha leemisuwaadaanikka medhdh xaafuwaa ufurettoti issi dorssate oosuwassi woykko medhdhi- xaafuwaassi keehi koshshiyaa attana danddayenna miishsha. 
Keettaa keexxiyoo hanoy poletti makkin gidikkonne keetta gidduwa puulayanawu hara harabata keetta giddon wottiyoogee attenna. Ha qommo baggaara nu be'ido leemisuwan keettay baayyo koshshiyaaba ubba ekkidi keexetti simmin keetti de'anawu ufayssenna aggana danddayees. Ha''ikka ayyo issibay pallees. Hegeekko so gidduwa puulayiyoogaa. He keetta gidduwa asay ufayttidi de’iyoo sohoboottanawu, quruxuwa quruxidi, keetta giddon miishshata shaatiyaa, gosiyaa, buliyaa kaqqidi, mehiyaayyo zadaulwaa giigissidi, keettaa pitti geeshi meeshidi oydiyaa ubbaa gaissi giigissobare keetta giddoy puulaa maayeei.medhdhi xaafuwa tekiniketa/ xaafuwa hiillatagiyoogeeti hageetu malabata. Xaafanchchay pwslayanawu dumma dummabata go'ettidi nabbabbiyaa asi ufayttidinne yeemottidi powwaa gakkanaadan oottiyay ha xaafiyoo tekinikiyaa. 

Medhdhi- xaafuwaa ufurettata xaafanchchay ay ogiyaankka go'ettanaadan dirssatiyaa giddon eti beettanaadan xaafuwaa wogay wolqqanttees. Shin tekinikoyaa xeelliyaagan xaafunchchay go’ettin agginkka ayyo bayraba gidenna aggana danddayees. Gaasoykka I polettida oosuwaayyo gujonne bollaara tisttiyooba mala. Xaafanchchay ano gididi tuussadan go'iyaa medhdhi- xaafuwa ufurettata go'ettiichchiis. Medhdhi xaafuwa tekinkiya go'ettennaagee mule oosettida oosuwa woriyoogaa woykko mela ashshiyoogaa gidenna. Gidikkonne eranchcha gidida lo''o meezze de’iyoo ka'ida xaafanchchay bari xaafiyoo medhdhi- xaafuwan ubba medhdhi- xaafo tekinileta/ xaafo- hiillata gelissidi xaafees. Qassi lammachcha gidida xaafanchchay woykko daroaaze baynna asi bawu hanidaaga keena tekinikiya go’ettidi kanttana danddayees. He wodiyaanqassi A oosoy bollaara puulaa maayibeenna gishatawu nabbabbiyaa asa wozanaa baqqidi baakko eheenna aggana danddayees. Hegaa gishashawu xaafanchchay A tekinikiya go'etta giidi wolqqanttiyay xayikkonne bari daafuridi kessido era oosuwaassi dumma dumma tekinikiyaa / xaafo hiillaa go'ettiyoogee attenna. Keettaa daaturi keexxi simmidi so gidduwaakka puulayana xayikko lo'ennaagaadan ha mehdhi- xafuwa oosoykka wuridi nabbabbiyaa asa kushiyaan gelanaappe kasetidi xaafanchchay baaxetidi woykko bariyyo minettidi bari xaafiyoobaa kumetta oottidi xaafana bessees giyoogaa. 
Ane kaallidi de'iyaa medhdhi- xaafuwa ufurettata kayankayan birshshidi xeelloos. 
                 5.4.1. Taarikiyaa (story) 
Toarikiyaa gigoogee I bariyyo aybee? Taarikkee polettiyaabatu kasiyaa kaaliwa. Taarike polettiyoy ubbay issippe gidennan bantta polettiyoo wodiyan, sohuwaninne palettiyoo hanotan kasiyaa kaaluwaa naagidi issoy hanoogaappe/ polettoogaappe simmin haray qassi polettees/ hanees giyoogaa. Issi medhdhi- xaafuwa giddon taarlkee polettiyoy issoy issuwa bollan (kuurettidi) gidennan de'ishin issi taarikee poletti makkiyo wode haray kaallees. Hegaa gishshatawu xuufiya oosuwan taarikee issoy issuwa kaallidi yiyoogee awu maara giyoogaa. Leemmisuwaassi issi medhdhi xaafuwa giddon eeshshaaway yelettees, gitatees, siiqo de'uwaa giddo gelana danddayees. gelettees yelees, bari polan koyyidobaa polees hegaappe simmidi hayqqees. Gidikkanne ha ano gididabata daro laaletta woykko qonccisso hanotan taarikiya xaafanchchay aattees giyoogaa. Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon polettiyaabata co''u giidi issuwa kaalli laalli yiyaabata qonccissidi birshshetta hanotan xaafanchchay wottiaggees. Ha polettiyaabay ayssi polettii/hanii) Legawu gaasoy aybee giyabay zaarettenna. Polettidabata kasiyaa kaaluwan wotti aggiyoogaa. 
Medhdhi xaafuwa taarikiyaa xaafanaayyo he medhdhi xaafuwaa giddon beettiyaa ano eeshshaawatu biyoosaa, hanoyoobaa, haasayiyoobaa kaalli kaallidi biyooge qanttanne qoncce oge gidees. He taarikiyawu ano eeshshaawati oonakko eroogaappe guyyiyaan he medhdhi xaafuwa ano taarikee he eeshshaawatu matan polettees giyoogaa. Polettidabata maaran maaran ea ohuwan eta sohuwan wottid qotay laalettennan doomettaappe poluwa gakkanawu maaran hemettees. Ha meran giigida medhdhi- xaafay nabbabbiyaagaa haarees polettidabata ammanidi ekkanaadan oottees. Taarikiyaa kurete cora gididi kaalli kaalli yiikko he medhi- xaafoy adussa gidees. Qassi guutta kureti de'ikko ha oosoy un''o woykko guutta gidees. Ha hanotan dauqqananne qaammana danddayees giyoogaa. 
Qanttan akeekanawu taarikee allaalletti (oosoti) wodiyaanne sohuwa kosiyaa kaaluwa maaran daddohettidi awude hanidee? Awan hanidee? Giyo oyshata zaaranaadan daraasiyaassi koshshiyaabata. 
                   5.4.2. Taarikiya Dembbaa 
Asay merettaaranne bari mala asaara bollan gaytettidi gidin qofan karssikarssaa medhdhees. Hegaa gaasoy kaalettiyo baaxiya; he baaxee goobi goobi biyo hanotaanne wurssettan kuushshaa bessiya ufuretta. Ha ufurettay gaasuwanne kuushshaa poluwaabaa ay hanidee? Ayssi haridee? Waanidi hanidee? giya oyshatussi zaaro gidiyaabata enccuridi kuushshawu injjetiyaadan merettiya taarikiya puuluwa. Hegeekka kattaa zerettawu go'ettiyo shooqaara milatees. Taarikiya dembbay woykko Ingilizettuwan plot

Yaagiyoogee polettiyaabatu woykko haniyaabatu kasiyaa kaaluwaa naagidi issoy haraara baxibannettidi qofettida hoolliyaakko biyoo hanotaa. Taarikeenne taarikiyaa dembbay polettiyaabata baaso oottidi denddiyoo gishshawu malatettoosona. Eta dummatettay taarikke polettiyaabata xalaalaa ekkidi koyro hagee hanis naa”anttuwan hagee polettiis, heezzanttuwan hagee haniis wurssettan qassi hagaadan haniis yaagiiddi biyoogaa. Gidoshin taarikiya dembbay ha hanettiyaabatu kasiyaa kaaluwan issi polettiyaabay ba de’iyoosaappe denddidi kaalliyaa nuushshaakko/ ayfiyaakko waani gakkidaakko gaaso gididabaa yootiyaagaa woykko zaariyaagaa. Hanettidabay waanidi hegaadan hanidee? aybissi hanidee? woykko I hegaadan hananawu gaaso/ denddo gididabay aybee? yaagiya dumma dumma oyshata zaarees. Taarikiyaa dembbay issi polettiyaabay aybissi haniyaakko/ polettiyaakko gaaso/ denddo gidiyaabaa immees. Ha imettida gaasoy /denddoy hapolettidabaa ba de'iyoosaappe efiidi hara polettiyaabawu ayfe oottees. Kaallidi de'iyaa taarikiyaa hanitankka hara gaasoti woykko denddoti imettiiddi hara ooratta. Poletussunne wurssetta medhdhi xaafuwaa hoolliyaa gattoosona. Nedhdhi xaafuwan hagaadan gaasotinne wurssetta ayfeti issippe minni ohetti ohetti biidi medhdhi- xaafuwa taarikiya wurssettaa eesoyoosona/gattoosona. 
Taarike xalaalay ba barkki aybanne lo’enna woykko aybanne bessenna shin taarikiya dembbay gujettiyoowode nabbabbiyaagee auueekiyoo issi taarikee haraara lo”idi ohottidaba gidees. Taarikiya dembbay issi-ppe yiya taarikiya issuwa issuwaara gatti oyttan xalaalassi gelenna he gaasoy ehiyoo poluwaassi bessiyaanne nabbabbiyaagee/ra “ tumakka” giidi/da ekkiyoobakka gidana bessees. I medhdhi xaafuwaa giddon beettiya hanotatanne polettiyaabata, bantta heeraara gidin hara eeshshaa watuura gidin de'iyaa gaytotettaassi gum”I ekkiyooba gidiyaa cuccumaa issippe gattidi baxxanniyoo gishshatawu I medhdhi xaafuwaassi baaso gaana danddayettees. 
                    
 5.4.3. Eeshshaawaa 
Ha ufurettaay bessiyoy medhdhi xaafo giddon wooxxi qaaxxiya dumma dumma eeshshaa ekkidi tumukka nu alamiyaa giddon beettana danddayiya asa malatidi medhdhi xaafuwa giddon dumma dumma oosota/ taarikiyaa poliya asa. Medhdhi xaafo giddon eeshshawi oottiyoo woykko poliyo taarikee alame giddon qogetti woykko poletti erennaba gidennan asaa de'uwan hanana danddayiya oosota/yohota. Eeshshaawati xaafanchchay /eranchchay bari kanan qoppidi medhdhiyoo heeraadan de'iyaa asata. Eti nunadan metootoosona. Qoppoosona suntan meraanikka nuna malatoosona giyoogaa.
Xaafanchchay bari xaafiyoo medhdhi xaafuwa giddon bessiyoobati ha nu alame giddon I paalli dobafanne loyttidi be’idobata. I xaafiiddi tumu asay bari so giddon, bari moottan, bari ooso keettaninne dumma dumma sohotun poliyoobatanne eta gakkana danddayiya hanotata tumu asaa gishshaa ekkidi poliyaa eeshshaawata go’ettees. Taarikiyaa giddon polettiyaabati ubbay polettiyoy woykko haniyiy ha eeshshaawata giyoogeetuuna. 
Medhdhi xaafuwa eeshshaawati ha alamiya asaa gishshanchchta gidiyoogaappe denddidoogan nu moottan de'iyaa asa nu eriyoogaadan erana danddayiyoogeeta. Eta eta suntan, eeshshan, meran shaakkidi ereettees. 
 “ Eshshaawati medhdhi xxaafuwa alamiyan asho maayidi, eeshshaa ekkidi, etawu suntti imettido, de’iyoo sohoy giigido, yaa haa qaaxxiya, shemppiya, haasayiya, miya, uyiya tumu alamiya asadan de'iya, hayqqiya, namisettiya, saammettiya siiqettiyaa, ooyettiya, ufayttiyaanne kayyottiya medhdhi xaafo alame asa. Eeshshaawati medhdhi xaafoy merettido sohuwaninne wodiyan pulttida he wodiyaanne he sohuwa asa gishshaawa gidishin he wodiyan.

           de'ida qogaanne xaaxi waaxo xeelaa,
           wogaanne maabaraa meezziya ayaa-
           naamanne buquraawa hanotata 
           bessoosona. Daraasiya kahan mere 
           ttida he wodiya qofaynne asaa 
           issoy issuwara gayttiyo hanotay etan 
           beettiyo asa mala.”
          ( Asfaa zaarihuna/1992: 160/ ) 
Medhdhi- xaafuwa eeshshaawati asa malafidi gidennan asa gididi medhdhi xaafuwa giddon hashetanaadaaninne nabbabbiyaa asi tuma giidi ekkanaadan xaafanchchay naagettidi eta medhdhanawu woykko misilanawu bessees. Ane medhdhi xaafuwa eeshshaa wata kaallideiya ogetun xeelloos. 
      
     5.4.3.1 Eeshshaawati shiiqiyoo ogeta 
Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon de'iya eeshshaawati muumidi haasayennaggeeta gidana bessenna. Eeshshaawati la’an bantta doona gb’ettidi haasayana bessees. Xaafanchchay oychchana bessiyaasan oychchananne zaaran bessiyaasan zaarana koshshees. Nabbabbiyaa asi oysha denttanawu bessiya hanoti beettana koshshenna. “ ha eeshshaaway hagan haasayana bessennee?” yaagidi mehdhi xaafuwa nabbabbiya asi oysha giddo gelana bessenna. Haray qassi eeshshaaway medhdhi xaafuwa giddon loyttidi hashetana bessees. Eeshshaawa gididi medhdhi xaafuwan issitookka geeliichchida asi dumma dumma sohotuninne wodetun dum,madumma oosota poliiddi beettana koshshees. Medudhi xaafuwa giddon beettiya eeshshaawati eti gishshaawatido deriyaassi eqqana bessees. Issi asa gidennan issi dariya giddon hanettiyaabaa shiishshidi bessana koshshees. Hegaa bollaarikka eeshshawati nabbabbiyaageetun ammanettiyaagaa gidana bessees. Eeshshaawati asi hegaadan hanenna woykko oottenna giyoobaa polana bessenna. Xaafanchchay bari medhdhi- xaafuwa giddon I medhdhi gelissido gishshatawu bari koyyidobaa haasayissanawu woykko oottissanawu danddayenna. Hegaa gishshawu eeshshaawati issitookka etayyo imettida eeshshan kaaletettana besseesippe attin eranchchay bari koyyoogaadan, oottana danddayenna. Eta eeshshhsawu polotettay de'ana bessees. Taarikiya doontettaan etawu imettida eeshshay wurssettaa gakkanaashin etaara gidana bessees. Gido shin qassi eeshshaawaa hanotaa/ eeshshaa laammanawu keehi koshshiyoo hanotay woykko wolqqanttiyaa mino gaasoy de’iyaaba gidikkonne taarikiyaassi immiyo go'ay de'ikko eta eeshshay laamettana danddayees. 
Eshshaawatuyyo issuwawu issuwawu haraappe dummatiya eta eeshshay de'ana bessees. Bantta dumma dumma eeshshankka bantta deriya wogaanne meezziya qonccisana bessees.
