Eshshaawati haniyoobaaninne oottiyooba ubbabankka polo gididi merettana koshshenna. Hegee aybissi giikko ay asa na'a gidikkone bari eran, oosuwan qofan polo gidana danddayenna. Ay asanwunne lefa miyyee/ woykko paaiyaa de'ees. hegaa gishshawu eeshshaawati medhdh xaafuwa giddon polo gididi simerettana koshshenna. Hegaa gishshatawu mehdhi- xaafuwa xaafiya asi ha qommo baggaara nuuni be'ido eeshshaawati shiiqiyoo ogeta akeekidinne hasayidi xaafikko A oosoy nabbabbiyaa asan ammanettiyaagaa gidana danddayees. 
                           5.4.3.2.   Eeshshaawaa qommota. 
Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon beettiya mule eeshshaawatussikka taarikiya giddon lagge qaattay/ hanotay de’enna. Aybissi giykko issi medhdhi xaafuwa giddon eeshshaawati naa”u ginawu shaahettana danddayoosona. Hegeetikka: Hegeetikka: 
I)	Bayra /ano eeshshaawatanne 
II)	Sima/kaalo  eeshshwata 
Ane ha naa''u eeshshawa qommota kayan kayan akeekidi xeelloos. 
                             I. Bayra / ano eeshshaawata
Bayra woykko ano eeshshaawata giyoogeeti taarikiya doomettaappe biidi poluwa gakkanaashin ubba sohuwanikka simerettiya woygkko taarikiyassi daro so hubuan hashetiiddi beettiya taarikiya poliya asata. Eti medhdhi xaatuwa giddon beettiya hara asatu ubbaappe aaro qaaxxoosonanne corabaa poliddi beettoosona. Bayra eeshshaawa giyoobi taarikiya dendduwappe doommidi beettiyoogee ayyo attennaba gidenna. Issi eeshshaaway leemisuwassi taarikiyaasi gidduwa heeran yiidi keehi darobaa poliiddi beettana danddayees. Doomettan beetti beennaba gidikkonne. Ha eeshshaawi taarikiya doomettan de’ana xaykkonne bayra/ ano eeshsh
aawa gidennaadan A digiyaabi baawa. 
                                II. sima/kaalo eeshshaawata
Sima woykko kaalo eeshshaawata giyoogeeti issi medhdhi xaafuwa giddon guutta sohotuni poleltiyaabatun beettidi woykko hashetidi bantta allaalliyaa polinne sohuwaarakka xayi aggiyaageeta. Eti medhdhi xaafuwa giddon guutta sohotun hashetido gishshatawu eti taarikiya dichchaassi maaddokkona woykko medhdhi xaafuwa giddon maaddokkona giyoogaa gidenaa. Sima eeshshaawati medhdhi- xaafuwa garssan ano eeshshaawatuppe guuxxenna hanotan koshshoosona. Ha ano eeshshaawati sima eeshshaawatun kaatettidi bantta oosuwa poloosona. Sima eeshshaawatikka ano eeshshaawatudan medhdhi xaafuwaassi logge koshshoosona. Naa”aappe issoy baynnaba gidiyakko taarikee taarike gidennan aggana danddayees. Issi issi dirassatetun woykkouuedhdhi xaafotun issi issi wode sima eeshshaawati sunttetti simmidi, erefetti simmidi, taarikiya giddon aybanne qaattennan/ haasayennan woykko aybanne polennan silphphi giidi attiigiyo hanetay de’ees. Hagee gamma gidenna. Taarikiya giddon aybanne hashetenna eeshshaawi koyro gelana bessenna. Gelliichchidaba gidikko taarikiyaan hashetane bessees giyoogaa. Geellodan issi issi wode medhdhi xaafuwa giddon suntan erettenna izaawu woykko issi citan de'iyaa asati taarikiyaa giddon hashetiyo hanotati de'oosona. Hegeetikka sima eeshshaawatuura baggattoosona giyoogaa. 
Issi issi wode issi issi medhdhi xaafuwan woykko dirssatiyan ayyaanati, kiitanchchati, xalahee, azzaqa do’ati hegaanne hegeeta malatiyaageeti eeshshawadan shiiqiyo hanotay de’ees. Eti ooninne erin asa gidana xayikkonne medhdhi xaafuwa dirssatiyaa giddon eti misiuettana bessiyoy gamma asa eeshsha ekkidi gidana bessees. Eti asaa eeshshaa ekkidi asadan haadayiiddi, asadan hemettiiddi, qoppiiddi, Dosota poliiddi beettana besses. Eti asadan qossi shiiqaappe guyyiyan eeshshaawadan qoodettoosona giyoogaa. 
                    5.4.5. Karssikarssaa 
Kaaleto oyshata: Kaallidi de'iya oyshata naa''an naa''an gididi tobboogaappe guyyiyan etawu gamma zaaro gidiyaageeta xaafidi kifile giddon intte laggetussi shiishshite. 
I. Karssikarssa giyoogee aybee? Ayyo hara mise qaala gidiyaabaa demmana danddayeetii?  
        Zuleyitenne A birshshetta qonccissite. 
II. Issi medhdhi xaafuwa giddon karssikarssi baynnaakko medhdhi xaafoy medhdhi- xaafo 
geetettana danddayii? Ee giidaba gidikko waanidi? Chii giidaba gidikko ayssi? 
Karssi karssaa giyoogee I bariyyo aybee? karssikarssaa giyoogee issi medhdhi xaafuwa giddon de'iya naa''u asatu giddon merettiya phalqqettaa giyoogaa. Naa''u citan, woykko wolqqatun woykko asatu giddon haniyaa palamaa denttidi maayettennan ixxidi doonan gidin wolqqandom''ettiyoogaa. Doona palamaa gidikko naa''u gayttenna qofatun tollu/chikki  gildi woykko issoy issuwa qofaa ekkenna ixxidi dom''ettiyoogaa. Wolqqan qassi dom''ettiyaaba gidikko naa''u wolqqati mashshaa toora deuttidi worettoosona hayqettoosona giyoogaa. Ha  korssikarssay merettiiddi naa''u wolqqatu giddon qofaa, meretaa, eeshshaa, ammanauwa, xeelaa hegeetanne hegeeta malatiyaabatun gayttennaagan woykko dummatiyoogan baasettees. Asaa  naa de'uwa giddon keehi cora qofaa phalqqettati de'oosona. Asay bari de'uwa giddon bari amottidobaa kunttanawu, xayidobaa demmanawu, metuwa xayssidi saruwan de’anawu, bari de'iyoo hanotaappe kehiyaabaa demmanawu baaxetees. Ha hanotati ayba baaxeenne baynnan coo kuni aggenna. Hegaa giddon daro metoti de'oosona. issi izzawu bari koyyidobaa kunttaanawu baaxetiyoowode ayyo xube gidiyaabati meretti aggoosona. Hegaappe kiyanaassi eeshshaaway daro balbbuqettan gelees daro baaxetees giyoogaa. Ha balbbuqettaa xoonanaayyo qassi eeshshaaway galla galla minnidi baaxefana koshshees. He baaxiyaa geello dan xoonidi ba koyyidoba demidikka asa gididoogee bari demmidoban ufauttidinne alidi de'enna. Hara aaroba koshshawu kiyees. He koshshan qassikka hara karssikarssaa giddo gelidi baaxeteesikko. Haraakka demmidi hara ooratta amuwa, koshshaa denttees. Kaallidikka hara xube gidiyaabi merettees. Ha hanotan deiuwa camo hanotaynne de’uwa mal''oy qonccees. Asanaa amuwawu zawi baynnaagaappe denddidaagan gayttiya metuwassinne baaxiyassi paydoy de’enna. Mototikka dumma dummanne daro. 

Medhdhi haafuwa giddon de'iya eeshshaawati ha alamiyan de'iya tumu asa zaari beso gidiyoo gishshatawu asaa deuwappe xayenna daro mutti- murunobati gayttoosonanne dumma dumma paaceti tiran kiyi wodhdhoosona. Hedhdhi xaafuwa giddon karssikarssaa yaagiyoogee hageetu mala de’uwa baaxiya xoonidi kessi ekkanawu oosettiya woretaa giyoogaa. 

Mehdhi xaafuwa giddon tumu asaa deuwadan karssikarssay denddiyoo cora gaasoti deoosona. Cora gaasoti de''iisona. Leemissuwassi asa na'i barkka bari giddon yootettana danddayees. Hegaa giyoogee issi assi issi allaalliya polana gi qoppiyoo wode hara baggara qassikka A wozanay poloppa yaagees. Ha hanotan issi asa wozanay A “ootta. Oottoppe” giyoo hanotay asi banaara yootettiyo karssi karssaa bessees. 

Asi qassikka asaara woykko bari deriyaara yootettana / karssi tarssana danddayees. Issi asi hara asaara qofaa maayettennan woykko issi asi bari dere assaa wogaappe kareera polana kouuiyoobi de'ikko deree aara eqettiyo gishshatawu karssikarssay denddees. Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon shiiqiyaa karssikarssawu denddoykka ha ogiyan polettiya baaxetuuna. Ha karssikarssay baaxiya bollan de'iya asatu bollan woykko qoppiya kahan paaccana danddayees. 
Eeshshaawati banttaa gelidobaappe kessi ekkanawu, xooni kiyanawu woykko bantta qoppidosaa gakkanawu eti oottiyo baaxee medhdhi xaafuwassi puulaanne loo'otettaa mayzzees. 

Medhdhi xaafuwa gidaon naa''u qommo karssikarssati de'oosona gaana danddayettees. Hegeefikka: 
I)	Bollaa karssikarssaanne 
II)	Kahaa karssikarssaa geetettoosona. 
Ane eta birshshettaa kaallidi kayan kayan xeelloos. 

                             I. Bollaa karssikarssaa
Bollaa karssukarssaa giyoogee aybee giikko. Medhdhi- xaafuwa giddon issi eeshshaaway hara eeshshawaara woykko eeshshaawatuura bollan gayttidi leemisuwassi bollan dom''ettidi, baaxetidi, sugettidi, kunddidi, tooran cadettidi, bollaa xiirettidi medhdhiyo karssikarssaa. Ha karssikarssaay ehiyo wurssetta ayffe xeellin beettiyaaba giyoogaa. Ha karssikarssa qassikka gaxa karssikarssi giidikka xeesettees. 


                   II. Kaaha giddo karssikarssaa 
Kaha giddo karssikarssaa giyoogee issi hanotay woykko issibay woykko issi eeshshaaway medhdhi xaafuwa giddon hara eeshshawaa bolli gattiyoo qohuwan eeshshaaway he hanotan bari giddon woykko bari kaha giddon bari equwaara/ fangguwaara, ammanuwaara gatti qofan shikki giidi aggoo aggoppoo? Oottoo oottoppoo? Yaagidi bari giddon barkka karssikerssiyoo hanotaa. Ha hanotay issi eeshshaawaa kaha giddo xalaalan polettiyaaba gidiyoo gishshatawu giddo korssikarssaa geetettidikka xeesettees. 

Medhdhi- xaafuwa giddon daro wode bollaa/ woykko gaxa karssikarssaappe kaha giddo karssikarssa gidiyaakko lo'o hegawukka gaasoy bollaa karssikarssaa wode eeshshaaway bollan masunxxana woykko harggana woykko hayqqanakka danddayees. He wodiyan A taarikee eqqanaadan woykko gidissanaadan oosettees. Gido shin kaha giddo karssikarssoe giddikko, eeshshaaway bari giddon de'iya qofan merettidabaa ixuwa gidin siiquwa sheniya sheniya gidin amuwa bari kahaa giddon wottiiddi denttiiddikka hara poluwawu kanttana danddayees’ Ha ogiyan taarikee kaalliganaadan oottiyoogan kaha giddo karssikerssay doorettees. Hegaa giishin medhdhi xaafuwa giddon bollaa karssikarssay dolashiiqana bessenna giyoogaa gidennan bollaa karssikarssaa gelissiyoo wode taarikee dumma dumma bouaa karssikarssay eyiyo gaasotun eqqeennaadan/ xubettennaadan keehi naagettidi gelissana bessees. 

Bollaa karssikarssaa gidin kaha giddo karssikarssaa gidonkka medhdhi xaafuwa giddon karssikarssaayyo A hemetaay de'ees. Daro wode medhdhi- xaafuwa nabbabbuwa doomiyoo wodeppe- biidi poluwa gakkanawu de'iya nabbabbiyaagaa hulluuqqoy issi mala gidenna. Ay medhdhi xaafuwakka nabbabbiyoo wode doomettaa heeran ooyyonne nabbabbuwawu de’iya huuluugoy woykko koshshay issi mala gidenna. 

Doomettaa heeran nabbabbuwawu de’iya hulluuqoy woykko koshshay keehi laafa. Aybissi giikko medhdhi xaafuwa giddon de’iya eesjsjaawati biron paacciya karssikarssa giddo geliic hchibookkona Nabbabbuwa sugisugi biyo wode karssikarssaa kaalli kaalli biyo wode taarikkiya giddo keehippe nu geli geli biyo wode keehi wudidi nabbabbiyoogaa doommi aggeettees. Aybissi giikko nabbabbuwa gujji gujjii nu byo wode karssi karssay wolqqaami wolqqaamidibiyo gishshatawu nabbabbiyaa asaa yeemoyees. He gaappe denddidaagan nabbabbiyaagee medhdhi xaafuwan de'iya taarikee kaallidi ay hananeeshsha giiddi bari qofaa ubba nibaabiyan wottidi polo wozanan nabbabbees. He wodiyan karssikarssay minni minni biidi woykko wolqqaamidi umbbubulettaa woykko climax giyo sohuwa gakkees. 

                                 5.4.6. Umbbubulettaa
Umbbubulettay medhdhi- xaafuwa giddonde’iya eeshshaawati karssikarssiiddi takkidi eti gakkana danddayiyoo keehi xoqqa gidida yeemoyiyaa sohuwa. Hegaappe simmiyo wode karssikarssay leeppi leppi bees. Ha suragettiiddi takkida karssikarssay leppe leppi yiyoo hayotay lekkeme'uwa (resolution) geetettees. Ha xekkan nabbabbiyangaa yeemoyidabay wodhdhi wodhdhidi minnida karssikarssay leppiiddi biidi poluwa/ wurssetta gakkees. Alabbabbiya asawu de’iya yeemoykko wodhdhi aggees. 
 
                                  5.4.7. Lekkeme'uwaa
Xaax waaxiyoo wode karssikarssay medhdhi xaafuwa giddon puulay. Shonggay de'ana malanne nabbabbiya assi yeemo giddo gelana mala wolqqaama maaduwa immees. Hegaa gishshawu I issi medhdhi xaafuwawassi tuussa giyoogaa. Daro lo''onne wolqqaama karssikarssay de’enna medhdhi xaafuy nabbabbiyagan yeemoyennanne ayyo puulaykka de’ana danddayenna. Hegaa gishshatawu karssikarssay ay medhdhi-xaafuwaawunne de’uwa immees giyoogaa. 
Issi xaafanchchay bari xaafigo medhdhi xaafuwa giddon karssikarssaa waati medhdhanaakkonne waati go'ettamaakko kaalettiyaabata akeekoos. Issi xaafanchchay bari xaafiyo medhdhi xaafuwa giddon mino karssikarssaa wottana bessees. He karssikarssan bollaa karssikarssa woykko kaha giddo karssikarssa gidana danddayees. He karssikkrssaa giddogelida eeshshaawati bantta gelido baaooe kassi ekkanawu wolqqaama baaxiya baaxetishin bessana kishshees. Aybissi giikko ha baaxee medhdhi xaafuwassi immiyo puulay keehi gita. Shin eeshshaawatuyyo imettiya karssikarssoy eta wolqqaappe keehi daridi woykko eta eraappe keehi guuxxidi beettana koshshenna. Ee shshaawatu eraaranne wolqqaara biya wollo laggetiya korssikarssaa xaafanchchay immana bessees. He imettiya karssikarssykka asaa han de’uwan gayttiyaaba woykko nu alamiyaa bollan polettina danddayiyaaba gididi nabbabbiyaa asan ekettiyaabanne tumuba woykko ammanttiyaaba gidana bessees. Wurssettan ha karssikarssaa giddon daro baaxiya baaxetidinne paacetti kiyida eeshshawati karssikarssaappe kiyiyoo wodiyan etu eeshshay woykko kase de’iya hanotay laamettishin xaafanchchay qonxxiyan bessana koshshees. 
                         Meezziya oyddaa 
Kaallidi de’iya oyshata pude baggaara ne tamaaridaban amppada nerkka etuwa gamma zaaro gidiyaabaa xanta shiishshada ne kifille laggetussi qobnccissand akeekissa. Yaatada ne oosuwa ne asttamaariyanttussi/ renttussi sheedhdha. 
1) Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon aappun qommo eeshshaawati beettana  danddayiyonaa? Qonccissa. 
2) Medhdhi xaafuwa eeshshaawati shiiqana bessiyoo ogeta birshshada yoota. 
3) Medhdhi xaafawa taarikiyaninne taarikiya dembbaa giddon dummatetti 
   de'ii? Qonccissuwashshishs ha. 
4) Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon issi eeshshaaway issi asa woykko payduwan 
   keehi guutta gidida asata gishshshatidi beettenna koshshennay aybissee? 
5) Medhdhi xaafuwa ufurettati ay medhdhi xaafuwankka beettana koshshiyoogee aybissee? 
6) Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon xuufuwa hiillaa woykko tekinikiya go'ettiyooge 
   ufurettati attana bessennaagaadaanikka keehi koshshees gaada qoppay? Aybissi? Qonccissa. 
7) karssikarssay issi medhdhi xaafuwassi tuussa giida. Ha qofan neeni maayettay? Aybissi? 
8) Karssikorssay naa''u qommo giidi qommo baggaara tobbiddoogaa hassayaasa. He naa''ati 
   oonee oonee eta birshshettaakka yoota.
9) Bollaa karssikarssaappe jaha giddo karssikarssay doorettiyo gaasoy ayba gidana danddayii? 
    Qonccissada akeekissa. 
10) Karssikorssaay medhdhi xaafuwa giddon minni biidi keehi wolqqaamiyoo bolla xeeray ayba 
      geetettii? Ha suraaettiiddi takkida  karssikarssay leppiiddi biyo hanotay qassi ayba geetettii? 
      Birshshada yoota. 
11) Issi xaafanchchay bari medhdhi xaafuwa giddon karssikurssaa waati medhdhanaakkonne 
    waati go'eettanaakko ne qofaa imma. 
                    5.4.8. Woqa (wodiyaanne qatuwaa) (Setting)
Woqa giya qaalay naa''u qaalata bari giddon oyqqi wottiis, wodiyaanne qatuwa yaagiyaageeta. Wo – yaagiya pitalee wodiyaassi eqqiyaagaa gidishin qa qatuwassi eqqidaba. Sa'a bollan polettiya aybiyyonne wodenne pollettiyo qatoy/ sohoy de'ees. Polettiyaabi aybinne woqappe kare gidana danddayenna. Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon eeshshaawati bantta poluwa oottiyoo sohoynne taarikiyaa oottiyoo wodee, layttay, aginay de'ees. 
Ay oosuwa polin, woxxin, paallin, waassin, kunddindenddin ha poloy oosettiyo sohoynne wodee de'ees. Hagee medhdhi xaafuwa giddon woqa geetettees. 
Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon eeshshaawatu eray, qofay eti kiyido dere asaa wogaa era, qofaa malatana mala xaafanchchay woqaabaa loyttidi erana bessees. Nabbabbiya asi erenna woqa gidana bessana. Nabbabbiyaagee/ ra eriyoo wodenne soho gidana bessees. Hegaagidikko ay banne metootennan issi poloy awan oosettiyaakko wodee qassi awudekko eridi hagee hiqqa biittan hiqqa wode hanees giidi ubbabaa bari de’uwaara gatti xeelliyo gishshatawu medhdhi- xaafuwawu lo”o akeekay de’ees. Eeshshaawatu oonatettay, eti gelido hanoy poloy he heeraara gattidi woykko malatissidi gilgissidi shiishshiyoogee xaafanchchaa hummunna. Xaafanchchay kari dere asaa giddon bariyyo be’idobaa, paacci xeellidobaa, bari wozanaa miidabaa, A yiilloyidabaa, nabbabbiyaagee be’ana malanne siyana mala bari be’idoogaadan woykko siyidogaadan gidennan hegaa qolchchiya /aadhdhiya ogiyan nabba bbiyaagaa bessana/ sissana bessees. Hagaa xaafanchchay aaho hanotan qonccissidi xaafana koshshees. 
Medhdhi xaafuwa giddoy xaafanchchay go’ettiyo qafoy asa na’I de’enna soho woykko de’ana danddayenne soho gidana koshshenna. Eeshshawuatuyyo oosuwa polanawu imettiya sohoy asa na’I tumukka de’an danddayiyoo woykko de’iyoo sohonne nabbabbiyaageekka tuma giidi ekkiyo/ ammanettiyo soho giyo pilaaneetetu giddoppe asa na’I hanno gakkanawu de’iddo biittaa bolla xalaalaana. Hara pilaaneetettu bolli asa na’I de’ibeenna sinttanaagee erettenna ixxikkonne. Shin xaafanchchay qatuwa merkuriya bolla woykko Jupiiteriyaa bolla giidi yootiyaaba/ xaafiyaaba gidikko A oosoy ammanettennaba gidees. Aybissi giikko he qattoy asa na’I de’enna soho gidiyoo gishshatawu. Medhdhdhi xaafuwa giddon eeshshaawatussi imettiyaa sohoy katama gidin, gaxaree, manttiya gidin giyay xeesetti xeesetti nabbabbiyaagawu/ rissi qoncciyan yootettana koshshees. 
Qatuwaadan wodee medhdhi xaafuwagiddon qoncciyaan odettiyoogee wolqqa gidenna. Wodiya yootiyoogee qatuwaadan keehi koshshenna aggana danddayees. Xaafanchchay medhdhi xaafuwa giddon hiqqa laytti hiqqa aginan hiqqa gallassi, hiqqa wodiyan giidi ubbabaa odennan aggana danddayees. Nabbabbiyoogee kumetta taarikiya xeelli simmidi ha taankee polettidoy woykko polettana danddayiyoy hiqqi wodiyaana giidi barkka gakkana danddayees. Issi oosoy woykko medhdhi- xaafay attamettidi kiyido layttay he maxaafay a xaafetti wuridi attametti kiyido layttappe attin medhdhi xaafuwaa giddon de’iya wodee A gidenna woykko gidennan aggana danddayees. Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon hanida taarikee polettido wodiyaa eranawu maxaafay attametti kiydo layttaa xeelliyooge daro wode bala. Tumaappe haasayikko issi nabbabbiyaagee issi medhdhi xaafuwa nabbabbuwa doomettaappe biidi poluwa gakkanawu tarike/ poloy hanido wodiya gallassaara saatiyaara cranna danddayenna ixxikkonne liqqa layttaa heera giidi ginaa erana danddayees aybissi giikko he wodiya qonccissiyaabay issuwan gidin hara ogiyan medhdhi xaafuwa giddon qoncciyoogee attenna. Ubba qonccennaba gidiyaakkonne nabbabbiya izaawu he poloy woykko taarikee oosettido wodiyaa ginaa hiqqa heera giidi erenna ixxikkonne matana danddayees. 
                    

  5.4.9. Cuccumaa 
Caccumay woykko inggiliizettuwan (theme) giyooyee medhdhi xaafoy woykko dirssatee nabbabiyaa asassi aattiyo kiitaa. I bari giddon oyqqido ano qofay cuccumaa giyoogaa. Xaafanchchy ekkidi denddido issi tumubaa asaa bessanawu medhdhi xaafuwa hiillaa giddo gelissidi shiishshees. Baynna eeshshaawata medhdhi kessidi asatettaa mayzzees, eeshshaawatu giddon dumma dumma karssikarssay denddanaadan oottees, eeshshaawati karssi karssaa giddoppe kessi ekkanawu oottiyo baaxxiya shiishshees. He baaxiya wurssettan issi ayfiya bessees. Shin ha ubbaa giddon xaafanchchay aattana koyyidi cuccumay issippe doomettaappe poluwa gakkandashin ohettidi yees. Cumay menttuwa ano qofaadan medhdhi xaafuwaassi doomettan, woykko giddo ginaa heeran woykko wurssettaa heeran beettiyaaba gidenna. Cuccumay medhdhi xaafuua dirssatiya doomettaappe biidi wurssettaa gakkanawu de’iyaa kifihee nabbalbetti wur simmin beettiyaaba. 

Medhdhi xaafuwa nabbabbiyoogan dubbushshiiddi /ufayttiiddi issi tumachcha gidiya xaafanchchay aattanawu koyyido ano yohuwa/ kiitaa akeekeettees. Nabbabbi wurssiyoo wodiyaana kumetta kiitay Ay kahawu aadhdhiyoy. 
Issi medhdhi xaafuwa xaafiya xaafanchchay / eranchchay haattappe maatappe denddidi woykko xaafana xalaalawu xaafenna. Issi eranchchay issi medhdhi xaafo dirssatiya xaafiyoo wode issi I be’idobay, paaccidobay, de'uwan asa naa gakkana danddayiyaabaa nabbabbiyaa asi akeekanaadan halchchuwan denddidi xaafees. Issi ano yohuwa bari giddon oyqqennan, issi I bessanawu koyyidobaa woykko aattanawu koyyido huuphe yohay de'ennan, issi I era immi kanttanawu koyyidobi de’ennan. Issi bala gididabaa nabbabbiyoo.asa bessanawu koyyennan ubba coo xaafettenna. Issi xaafarchchay issi medhdhi xaafuwa ay huuphe yohun gidikkonne xaafiiddi cou giidi ayyo xaafiyo amala de’in xaafenna. Issi I be'idobay, issi I aattana koyyido tumubay, asaa de’uwan I bessana koyyidobay de’ees giyoogaa. Nabbabbiyaageekka/rakka bari nabbabbuwa wurssoogaappe simmin denttiyo oyshi xayenna. Ha medhdhi xaafa dirssatee ay tamaarissanawu koyyidee? I bari giddon oyqqido huuphe yohoy woykko ano kiitay aybeeshaa? Ayba era beesikanttana koyyidee? Yaayidi ogchchees. Hegaappe simmidikka ta hanno tamaaraas. Ha medhdhi xaafoy taayo hanni mala kiitaa aattiis yaagidi kuuyyeesippe attin nabbabbiyaagee nabbabbi simmidi nababba wurssaas giidi aggi beenna. Nabbabbido assi nabbabbi wurssoogaappe guyyiyan ba tamaaridobaa bari kahan yuishshi aattidi qoppees giyoogaa. 
Issi medhdhi xaafuwa nabbabbi wurssi simmidi issi asi tamaariyo huuphe yohoy haray tamaariyoogaappe issi ogiyaan gidin haran dummatana dandayees. Issi medhdhi – xaafuwaassi de’iya xaaxi waaxo cuuaummay mexi issuwa gidikkonne sima tumubatikka de’ana danddayoosona. Hegaa gishshawu ay asinne issi dirssatiya/ medhdhi xaafuwa nabbabboogaappe gimmin issi I/A tamaariyoo huuphe yohoy de’ees giyoogaa. 
Issi medhdhi xaafuwa cuuccumay naa''u dumma ogetun aadhdhana danddayees. Issi xaafanchchay bari oosuwa giddon cuuccumaa qancciyan woykko geeman aattana danddayees. Hegee ayyo maata. Gido shon qonaiyan imettidu cuuccumay nabbabiyaa asi harabaakka woykko hara tumaakka pilggidi gakkennaadan azallissiyoo gishshatawu qoncce ogee daro doorettenna. Issi medhdhi xaafuwa yiddon de'iya cuuccumay asi nabbabbi wurssi simmidi pilggi denniyooba gidiyaakko keehi lo'o. aybissi giikko issi na bbabbiyaa asi cuuccumay koyro erettiichchikko keehi ufayttidi woykko maalaalettidi nabbabbennan agganadanddayees. Shin cuuccumay geema gidikko nabbabbiyaa asi sammettidi ay kiitaa aattancc haniishsha giiddi yeemo mala hemotan gididi nabbabbees. Hegaa gishshatawu medhdhi xaafuwa giddon cuuccumay geema ogiyaan uttiyaakko doorettees. 

Issi xuufe oosoy woykko medhi xaafoy adussa gidin qantta gidin aaho gidin xuntta gidin, aani aadhdhiya mexi issi ano ccuuccuma xalaalay aani aadhdhana bessees. Issi medhdhi xaafay asaa naa de'uwa aahtettaa denttidi ay keehi aahonne cilmma gididabaa bari giddon denttikkonne de'uwan danddayettenna asaara gayttiya ubbabaa bessana. 
Medhdhi xaafuwa cuuccumaa ohettaa xeelliyagan he wodiyabaa/ xaafettiiddi de'iya wodiyan de'iya hanotaaohetti uttida cuuccumaa ekkidi yaana danddayees. Hegaa mala medhdhi xaafoy he xaafettido wodiyaappe aadhdhii chchikko ayyo nabbabbettana qaadi darenna. Issi wodiyan de'iya hanota xalaalaan ano/ huuphe oottidi xaafettettida dirssatee woykko medhdhi xaafoy he hanotay woykko xaafettido cuuccumay geliiyoo wode he medhdhi xaafuwawu sintta wodiyawu nabbabettiyo qaadi keehi laafa. Hagaa mala cuuccumay kaallidi yiya woykko de'iya wodiyaassi dere go’aa imm enna. Hegaa giyshshawu issi medhdhi xaafuwa xaafiya eranchchay bari xaafiyo dirssutiya cuuccumba aassiddi ha''i wode xalaalan nabbabbettiyaaba gidennan sintta wodiyawukka kantti kiyiyaanne sintta yeletaakka go’iya woykko era immiya cuccmaa xeelli be’idi dooriyoogan bari medhdhi xaafuwa wodiyan keehettennaba/ teqettennaba oottana bessees. Paro daafuran, daro wodiya immidi, miishshaa kessidi Anabbabbuwawu gattido era oosoy hagaa mala hanotan xubettidi hada kiyana bessenna. Hegaa gishshatawu xaafanchchay issi meshshshi xaafuwa doommanaappe kasetidi daro akeekan huuphe yohuwa dooranawunne cuucwmaakka loytti be'idi doommikko daro lo''o. Hegaa gidana xaykko A daafuray mela gidana danddayees. 

Hegaadaanikka issi xaafettiya medhdhi xaafo oosuwa cuuccumay mexi guutta asatu xalaalaa bollan wudiyaaba gidikko woykko issi keehi xuntta woykko un''o gidida metotuuninne hantatun cuuccumaa wottikko hara aaho deriyawu maaddenna ixxana danddayees. Medhdhi xaafuwa cuuccumays ubba asaa metuwa baaso oottiyaaba, kumetta asaa naa metuwanne A de'uwan eysha gidana danddayiyaa metota/ yohota baaso oottidi cuuccumaakka A giddoora ehaana bessees. Hagaa mala yohota bari kantti kiyidi sinttan wodiyan kaallidi de’iya yeletaanikka be;ttiyo aaho qaadaa demmees. Gaasaykka he medhdhi xaafoy denttiyoo yohoy issi qammawu woykko issi layttawu woykko arama wodiyawu takkidi xayi aggiyaaba gidenna. Asaa naa de'uwaara loytti onefti uttida huuphe yohoy asa na''i de'ido wode ubban tishshi giidi xaphuwa yeddidi de' aggees. Hachchin de'iyaa asay nabbabbikkonne haachchi asawu ceeggenna. Issi issi leemisot gidana danddayiya kare biittaa era oosota ekki xeellikko hachchi ishatamu laytti woykko xeetu laytti hegaappekka bolla wodiyawu takkida oosoti ha/hain de'iyaa asi nabbabbikkonne hachchi asawukka oorattanne aattiyoo cuuccumay ga''enna. Ane “ Romio and Jullel” yaagiya era oosuwa be'idaba gidikko hassayite. Hagaaa giishin medhdhi xaafuwa oossoti he wodiyaan haniiddi de'iyaaban wudidi xaafana bessenna giyooga gidenna. Medhdhi xaafuwa xaafiya xaafanchchay bari qoppidp ay huuphe yohuwaaninne xaafanawu ayyo maati dees woykko I la'a de'ees. Xaaxi waaxiyoo wode issi kumetta asaa metuwan adussa wodiyawu denddana danddayiyaa huuphe yohuwan xaafettida oosoy A wodiyaappe aadhdhidi sintta adussa wodiyawu nabbabbettiiddi de'ees. Nabbubbiyaa asawukka immiyoo go'ay aaho. 
      
                5.4.10. Ontta (Oonee haasayiyay? 1ro 2ntto 3ntto  asa) (Point of view)
Ontta giyoogee medhdhi- xaafuwa giddon taarikiya yootiya asi ay sohuwaa bollan gididi yootidakko qonccissiya ufurettaa. Taarikiya yootanchchay ay sohuwan gididi yootii? I taarikiya giddo geli eqqidi oosuwaa poliyoo hanotan hashetidi beettiiyye bana taarikiyaappe kareera wottidi hara eeshshawati poliyo poluwa kaalli kaallidi yootii? Ha hanotaa/oyshaa zaarees giyoogaa. Leemisuwassi galla galla aadhdhiya oduwa ekkidi xeelliyaaba gidikko issi oduwa aattiyaa asi issi biitta xeesidi hiqqa biittan cora asay ogiya kiyidi bantta kawotettaa ayisuwa wogaa eqettidosona. Hagaadan dorobaa oduwa yootiya asi odees. I hagaa yootiyoo wode barina he hanotaa giddon wottidi gidennan kare baggaara nunadan xeellidobaa woykko siyidobaa amppidi yootees. I eqettanawu ogiya kiyiya asaara zuppetibeenna. Ha oduwan leemisuwawu I gellidi hashetidaba gidiyaakko nu hagaadan hanida kaallidi ----------- hagaadan haasayida ------yaagidi yootana. Hodde ontta giyoobi xaatanchchay taarikiya yootiyoy eeshshaawcctuura issi oosuwan hoshetidaadan hanidiyye gaxan kiyi uttidi ha gaadem hanidosona,------------------- yaatidssona giidi yyotiyo sohuwa giyoogaa. Hegaa gishshetawu xaafanchchoy bari medhdhi xaafuwa giddon go'ettana ontta doori kuuyyana koshshees. Ane kaallidi daro wode go'an ppe'iya ontta qommota kayan kayan xeelloos. Hegeetikka:-
I)	Koyro onttaa gophphiyaa /xekkaa xeelaa ( 1st person point of view) 
II)	Ubbaa eriyaagaa xeelaa (omniscient polnt of view) 
III)	Paca eraawaa (limited omniscient point of view) 
        
 I) Koyro onttaa gophphiyaa/xekkaa (first person point of view)
Ha onttay xaafanchchay medhdhi xaafo dirssatiya giddon. Bana eeshshaawatuura powwa oottidabadan oottidi haasayiyo hanotaa. Ha onttan xaafanchchay eeshshaawatudan oosuwan hashetees. Medhdhi- xaafuwa giddon xaafancchchaa taani yaagiiddi haasayees. Taani hagaa malabaa qoppaas; ta yaataas; taati ufayttaas; hanidaban taani doro yiillotaas. H.h.m. haasayota denttidi haasayana danddayiyoy ha onttaana. 
                II. Ubbaa eriyaa onttaa (Omniscient point of view)
Ubbaa eriya onttay bessiyoy issi medhdhi xaafuwa xaafanchchay taari kiyappe kareera gididi hanidabaa woykko polettidabaa nabbabbiyaage efawu aattiyoo onttaa. Ha onttan xaafanchchay koyro xekkaa xeelaadan (first person point of view) taani woykko nuuni hagaadam oottida woykko honida giidi yootenna. Xaafanchchay poluwaappe kare baggaara gididi hagee hagaadan haniis hagaa mala assi hagaamala oosuwa oottiis. Asati yootettidosona; sigettidosona yaagiiddi yootees. Qommon giidiigaadan odanchchay ubbaa eriyaagaa giidoy I eeshshaawati hananabaa, qoppiyoobaa, haasayana, maana, uyanabaa ubba erees. Nabbabbiyaageekka odarchchay yootiyooba ubbaa siyidi tuma giidi ekkees. 

Ha onttan odanchchay mule ubbabaa eriyoogaappe denddidaasan eti poliyoobaanne polanaba ubbaa qonccissidi yootees giyoogaa. 
III. Paca eraawaa onttaa (limited omniscient point of view)
Paca eraawa onttay (xeelay) ubbaa eriya onttaadan mule ubbabaa erenna. Ubbaa eriya xeelaappe I dummatiyoo ogeti ubbaa eriyaa xeelay eeshshaawati medhdhi- xaafuwa giddon oottiyoo mule ubbabaa erlyoogaa gidishin paca eraawa xeelan odaychchay medhdhi- xaafuwa gidddon eeshshaawati poliyoobaa, qoppiyoobaa, haasayiyoobaa, qachchiyoobaa, haniyooba wurssi wrwnna hanotaa bessees. Ubba qassi ano woykko bayra eeshshaawatu qaattaappe kareera haratubaa dorin erana danddayeenna hanotay de’iyo ontta. Bayra eeshshaawatuppe haraa darin qonccissennanne etabaa daro yootenna erenna gishshatawu giyoogaa. 
                   5.11.    Doonaa go'etuwa 
Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon xaafanchchay lo'o qaalata goettidi puulaa mayzzidi xaafana koshshees. Xaafanchchay nabbabbiya asaassi geliyanne A kahaa giddon misiliya medhdhana danddayiya qaalata go’ettiyoogee keehi puulaa mayzziyaaba. Eeshshaawati gelido hanotaa, etawu de'iya eeshshaa, hulluuquwa hegaadankka taarikee polettiyo heeraa/ moottaa ubbaa qonccissiyay doonaa. Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon de'iya eeshshaawata issuwa issuwaara gatti haasayissiyoy, eta ammanuwa, pilggetta oosuwa, taarikiya giddon qonccissiyay de'uwa lo'otettaanne iitatettaakka dooni qonccissees. Lo'o doonaa go'ettidi qonccissidinne laalli bessiyoo eray baynna xaafanchchay ay gita yohuwa bolli wudidi bari era oosuwa oottikkonne ayyo dumma dumma wolqqaama qaalata doori ekkidi bari oosuwa asaassi geliya qoncce ogiyanshiishshana xayikko nabbabbiyaa gaayyo maaddiya tumanchchabaa aattana danddayenna. Issi xaafanchchay keehi xiqqa gidida doonaa go'ettiyoo eray/hiillay de'ana bessees. Dirssatiya coo doonaa go'ettidi xaatiyooga xalaala gidennan he xaafanchchay xaafiyoo doonan de'iya leemiso haasayata, bila haasayata, zina haaxayata dumma dumma sohutun gelissi gelissidi xaafiyaakko keehi daro lo'o. He mehdhi xaafoy xaafettiyoo doonay cora asay nabbabbanawu qaadaa immiaagaa sidiyankko daro lo'o. Leemisuwassi issi medhdhi xaafuwa hayqqiiddi de'iya doonatun xaafikko woykko hayqqida doonatun leemisuwassi Gi'iizettuwan xaafiyaaba gidi baakko A ooni nabbabbanee? Ha''i wodiyan A nabbabbiya asi de'enna. Arama woosa keettatu qeeseti coo naa''u heezzu qaalata giyoorippe attin. Hara baggaara qassi issi medhdhi xaafoy ingiyizettuwan xaafettiyaakko qassi keehi cora nabbabbiyaa assi de'ees giyoogaa aybissi giikko Irgillizettoy awaa biittaaninne nabbabbettana danddayees. 

Ha pude baggaara be’ido medhdhi xaafo ufurettati medhdhi xaafuwa dirssatiya giddon dumma dumma shaahetti uttiyaaba gidokkona. Eti ubbaykka issoy issuwara maarettidi/ walakettidi issippetettan medhdhi xaafuwa koolidi loyttoosona. Issoy aadhdhidi beettiyoo wode haray maaddenna banne laafaba idonna. Eta issippetetta issi xifate oosuwawu shonggaa immidi asaa naa de’uwa zari besso oottiyay. Eti ubbay mino issippetettan oyqqettidi asaa naa de’uwa xifate oosuwa giddon gitayidi woykko aassidi bessoosona. 
                      Meezziya usuppunaa 
Kaallidi imettida oyshata oyddu oyddu tamaariy oyqqiya citaa medhdhidi tobboogaappe guyyiyan gamma zaaruwa xaafidi intte asttamaariyanttussi/ renttussi shiishshite. Issi issi oyshatussi gidiya qonccissu immiyoogaa dogoppite. 
1) Hagaappe bolla baggaara onttaa qommota birshshidi be'ida. Eta heezzaa giddon de'iyaa 
    dummatettaa birshshidi intte kifile laggetussi qonccissidi yootite. 
2)	issi medhdhi xaafuwa giddon doonaa go’etay ay mala gidana bessiyaakko qonccissa. 
3)	Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon Bayra/ anonne sima/ kaalo eeshshaawatu giddon de’iya dummatettaa aassada yoota. 
4)	Medhdhi xaafuwa ufurettati medhdhi xaafuwa oosuwassi keehi koshshiyabata gidanaadan oottiya ano gidiya gaasota yootite. 
5)	Issi medhdhi xaafuwa giddon de’iya taarikee amanttiyalaa gidiyoogeenne gidennaagee aybin likettii? Birshshidi yootite. 
6)	Medhdhi xaafuwa cuccumay mexi issi wode hanidaba woykko issi galla polettidccba xalaaalan wudiyoogaappe issi aahonne ubbaasaa de’uwan polettiya hanotan wodiyaakko keehi lo’o. Ha qofaa qonccissidi xaafoogaappe guggiyan intte kifile laggetas sissite. 
7)	Medhdhi xaafuwa koyro xekkaa xeelaaninne ubbaa eriyaagaa xeelan de’iya dummatetta birshshshi yootoogaappe guyyiyan et amino miyyiyaanne lefa miyyiya qonccissidi xaafi shiishshite. 

 4.3.2. Medhdhi xaafuwa xaafo hiillaa (tekiniketa) 

Denttetto oyshata. 
Kaallidi de'iyaa oyshata waattan waattan gididi tobboogaappe guyyiyan ubbaykka maayettiyo gamma zaaro gidiyaageeta xaafidi shiishshite. 
1) Medhdhi xaafuwa tekinikiya woykko xaafo hiillaa giyoogee aybee? 
2) Medhdhi  xaafuwa giddon tekinikiya go'ettiyoogawu maaday aybee? Tekinikiya issi 
    xaafanchchay bari medhdhi xaafuwa giddon go'ettenna ixxiyakko aybi merettes giidi 
   qoppeetii? 
3) Medhdhi xaafuwa tekiniketa giyoogeeti awugeetee zuleyiidi qonccissite. Tekinikiya woykko 
    xaafo hiillaa giyogee medhdhi xaafuwa ufurettatun kooletti uttida medhdhi xaafuwa oosay 
   bariyyo bessiya puulaa utettaa naagidi lo'iyanne asa wozanaa oyqqana danddayiya ogiyan 
   nabbabbiyaa asawu aadhdhanaadan danddayissiya medhdhi xaafuwa mal''ettiyaa qimaame 
    woykko maxine mala giyoogaa. 
Ha medhdhi xaafuwa shiishshiyo hiillati medhdhi xaafuwa ufurettatudan nu aytiyan beettiyaaba gidokkona. Eti hiilla gidiyo gishshawu qosa gidida ogiyan geloosona. Medhdhi xaafuwa xaafiyoo hiillata issi nabbabbiyaa asi shaakki / maxi kessana danddayenna. A wozanan wotti nabbabbenna asi eti taafo hiillata /tekiniketa shaakki erennan kanttidi baana danddayees. Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon de'iya tekiniketa eranawu daro pilggettaanne hassayan kashshees. 

Medhdhi xaafuwa tekiniketi A puulaa mayzziyanne nabbabbiyaa asa amo giddo yeggiyaba gidiyoo gishshafawu medhdhi xaafo giddon xaafanchchti akeekidi gelissana bessees. Shin waati go’ettanaakkonne ay ogiyan go'ettanaakko xaafanchcha bariyyo kuuyyees. Medhdhi xaafo tekiniketi ufurettatudan ubbaykka koshshoosona giyooba gidenna ixxikkonne xaafanchchay bariyyo hanidoogaa keena danddayikke muliya assi ixxikko aranaa ge’ettana bessees giyoogaa. Medhdhi xaafuwan daro qommtekiniketa/ xaafo hiillatu go’ettikko ufunettatu go’ettuwaara shiiqidi xaafo oosuwassi puulaannl de’uwa mayzzees. 
Tekinikeei /xaafo hiiuati ufurettatudan xaafo oosotussi lagge koshshana xayikkonne medhdhi- xaafuwa shiishshuwawunne puulaa mayzzanawu keehi koshshiyaaba. Ane medhdhixaafuwa tekiniketa/ xaafo hiluata kaauidi issuwa issuwa xeeuoos. 
                        I. Haasayaa (Dialogue)
Medhdhi xaafuwan woykko dirssatiya oosuwan haasayan (dialogue) giyoogee xaafanchchay barixaafo oosuwa giddon eeshshaawatuyyo eta haasaya gidenna haasayaa immidi hegaa eti haasayanaadan oottiyo hanotaa. Eeshshawati medhdhi xaafo giddon bantta koyyido ay yohuwaanne leemisuwassi bantta sintta qofaa, bantta polidobaa, polarawu halchchidobaa, xayidobaa, demmidobaa, ufayttidoba hegeetanne hegeeta  

Malatiyabata denttidi haasayana danddayoosona. Issi eeshshaawoy haro eeshshaawaa baakka denttidi haasayana danddayees. Gido shin eta hccasayay eti kiyidi yiido dere asaa wogaa gishshatiyaaba gidana bessees. Haray atto shin xaafanchchay bari immiyo qonccissuwaappe aaruwa eeshshaawatu haasayawu aaho qaadaa immidi eta haaswyissana
Bessees. Hegaa giishin ubba ayba allaallccnne baynna pattenna hada haasayan eeshshaawatu wodiya xuuggana woykko taarikiya shongacissana keshshes giyoogaa gidennan allaallee de’iyonne birshsh/nettaa immiya hanotan qoncce gidida eeshshaawatu haasayaa gelissana koshshees. Ha tekinikee medhdhi xaafuwa eoshshawuata nabbabbiyaageetawu qoneeissiyo ogetuppe issuwa. 
                   II.  Qonccissuwa (Description)
Qonccissuwa (description) Ingilizetuwan yaagiyo tekinikee /xaafo hiillay medhdhi- xaafuwa giddon xaafanchchay go’ettiyoo doona. Xaafanchchay bori medhdhido eeshshawatu meraa, eeshshaa, oonatettaa, eti gelidonne de'iyoo hanotaa, eti de'iyoo sohuwaa ubbaa eti de'iyoo dere asaa wogaappe dummayenna hanotan bessiyoo dere asaa wogaappe dummayenna hanotan bessiyoohiilla. Ha tekinikoya go'ettidi xaafanchchay haniyaaban, taarikiya giddon polettiyaabaa nabbabbiyaagaa guuggiyan mishlidi wottanauwu, bantta kahaayuwan medhdhnanawu, eeshshshaawatu meraa, geesad, qaattaa, hulwuquwa siyettanaadan oottanawu go’ettiyo hililla. He gaa gishshawu xaafanchchaa doonaa go'etoy,qaalatu dooroy xaaxi waaxo hanotan doonaa go'etay hagaa giddon beettees giyoogna. 
                         III. Sinttaa Malaataa (Foretell)
Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon malaataa giyoogee issi polettanaappe, hananaappe woykko gakkanaappe kasetidi haasayiyoogaa woykko belsiyoo hanotaa. Medhdhi xaafuwa taarikiya giddon karssikarssay aybi gaason waani denddanaakko woykko eeshshaawata ay mala paacee/ hanotay 

gakkana de’iyaakko xaafanchchay dendduwan kasetidi nabbabbiyagawu/rissi issi biradhdhiyoo hiilla. Hageekka medhdhi xaafo tekiniketuppe issuwa gidiyoogaadaanikka xaafanchchay co”u giidi mule polettana/hanana de’iyaabee wurssidi koyroora odirggonna. Woykko eeshshaway wurssettan hagaadan haniyoorin taarikee politti aggana de’ees woykko hataarikiya wurssettay hagaa mala gidana de’ees giidi ubba wurssi odenna. Hegaadan geello xaafanchchay qoncciyan “hagee hagaadan polettana de'ees” taarikiya wuroettay hannitton hahuna de’ees qiidi yootiyaakko nabbabbiyaa asi nabbabbiiddi aybissi waayetii. I ( malaatay) daro hiillan qoncciyan gidennan qosan akeekidi nabbnbbiya asa xalaalawu qonccanaadan ootiya tekonikiyan xaafettana bessees. Keehi daro akeekan wozanaan wottidi mabbabbana xayikko ayba malaatinne he asawu beettenna aggana danddayees. Ha xaafo hiillay mednddhi xaafo dirssatiya giddon qofa qoshuwan woykko mexi issi qaalan. Woykko is qantta oduwan, woykko aymo mera uttana danddayettees. 
                       IV. Zaari - oduwa (flash back)
Zaarioduwa (flash back) giyoogee medhdhi xaafuwa giddo issi eeshshaawaa taarikiya xaafanchchay guyye biidi I xase hanidobaa, oottidobaa, ayyo de’iya ceshshaa, A beni hanotaa guyye denttidi yootiyoo hanotaa. Xaafanchchay bari oosuwa gum”idi hachchin de’iya eeshshaawatubaa zaari oduwaa tekinikiya go’ettidi eta beni/kase taarikiya yootees. 

Medhdhi xaafuwa xaafanchchay zaari- oduwa tekinikiya go’ettana bessiyoo gaasoti cora. I ha”in de’iyaa eeshshaawati poliyo poluwawu baasoy aybakko qonccissees; Eeshshaaeaa kase hanoy/ oosoy ha”in de’iyanne kaalliya taarikiyawu maadoy de’ama damddayees. Eeshshaawaa aadhdhida taanikee issitoo issito denddendau cotaua danddayenna hanotan daro maadees. 

Zaari odoy woykko hani aadhdhida eeshshaawatu hanoy/ oosoy aahuwa yootettidi ha”in de’iya taarikiya cuullana bessenna. He beni hanidabaa yootiiddi kasebaa zaari oduwaa dentti yootiiddi aetiaggana bessenna. Xaafanchchay zaari oduwa eesuwan yooti wurssinue ha”I yootiiddi taarikiyaakko simmana bessees. Ha tekinikee daro medhdhi xaafota wozanan wottidi/ akeekidi nabbabbikko beetees giidi aggi be’iyaaba gidennan medhdhi xaafuwan dumma dumma sohotun simmi simmidi yaana danddayees. Gido shin killi baggaara nu denttido qofatu balana bessenna. Medhdhi xaafoy bariyyo de’iya puulaa/ meraa xayana bessenna zari oduwa gaasuwan. Ay medhdhi xaafuwaaninne kumettataarikee zaarioduwan worana danddayenna. Taarikiyawu aaho baggay zaari odo gidikkonne hachchiigawu yeennan yaara yaa attenna. 
                        V. Yeemuwa (Suspense)
Ha tekinikee Inggiliizettuwan suuphence geetettiyoogan erettees. Yeemuwa giyoogee medhdhi xaafoy woykko xifate oosoy nabbabbiya asa hulluuquwa haaridi amubbian yeggiyo hanotaa. Medhdhi xaafuwawu woykko xifate oosuwawu pula giyoyikka ha tekinukiya giyoogaa. Medhdhi xaafuwa yeemuwayyo baaso gidayaageeti taarikee issoy issuwaara oyqetti uttiyo gaasuwanne wurssetta ayfiya medhdhi xaafuwa giddon beettiya korssikarssa minotettaa, gakkiyo xoqqa xekkoane xaafanchchay go’ettiyo doonaa. Issi medhdhi xaafuwan yeemoy (suspenee) merettiyoy nabbabbiya asi nabbabbiiddi eeshshatuura erittiyoonne eta xuuraa, metuwa, waayiya, wurssi eridi/ hashetide eeshshaawatuura dabbotiyo woykko matettiyo wodiyaana. Ha ogiyan medhdhi xaafuwa yeemoy nabbabbiyaageeta amoyiyoogan kaallidi aybi polettana dii? aybi hanana de’ii giidsiiddi nabbabbidi wurssanaadan oottees giyoogaa. Issi asi salettennan utti be’idi bari uttidosaappe denddennan nabbabbi wurssunaadan oottiyay ha tekinikiya. I issi medhdhi xaafoy woykko xifate oosuwa issi assi nabbabbanaadan dafiya bayra medhdhi xaafuwaassi puulaa immiyaabanne

 dafiya wolqqa giyoogaa. Ha yeemoy medhdhi xaafuwa doomettaappe biidi wurssettaa gakkanaashin karssikarssaly leppiyo wodenne goobiyoo wode dariiddi issippe bees. Taarikee biidi umbbubulettaa gakkiyo wode keehi xoqqa xekkaa gakki simmidi karssikarssay eqqiyo wodenne lekkeme’oy yiyoo wode taarikee wuriiddi de’iyo gishshawu yeemoy leppidi irxxi aggees. 
Nabbabbiyaagaa hulluuguwa oyqqennanne denttettenna medhdhi- xaafoy nabbabbanawu saletteesinne qimaamee woykko maxinne baynna katta mala. 
                   VI. Gishshatuwa 
Medhdhi- xaafuwan gishshatoy woykko inggiliizetto birshshttan symbol giyoogee issi xiffate oosuwa giddon issibay gishshatidi aedhdhiyoo hanotaa. Gishshaa immiyo hanotan issi gishshatidabi Awu gishshaa immidabaa giddon beettees. Gishshaa immiyaagee gishshatidabaabaa qonccissees. Ha geluwan malaataa glidi denddido qofay nu mlayfiyan be’iyo issi malaata leemisuwawu qoodaa timirttiyan ( x, -, t, 1) haageeti malaatata. Nuoni haasayiiddi de’iyoy ha malaatatu malabata gidenna. Ha geluwan malaataa giyoogee issi asa woykko issi miishsha sohuwan gididi medhdhi xaafuwa giddon beettiyo hanotaa. Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon gishshatoy issi misihe meran woykko miishsha meran uttiyaaba gidenna. I xaafanchcha/ era oosanchchaa doonan yotettiyaaba, 
Medhdhi xaafuua gidonheezzu gishshaatettau qommoti beettoosona. Hegeetuppekka koyroy salo sa’a gufantto/uniuersal giyoogaa. Ha gishshaytay issibay issibawu gishshatidi he sohuwan beettidoogaa salo sa’a gufanttan de’iya ay asinne eroyoo hanota giyoogall. Hegee Nu alamiyan de’iya laappun haruurotun deliya ay biittatuunikka Toophphiyan, Inggiliizen, Awurooppan, Amerkkan gidin Afirkan biitta ubban erettida gishshatettay de’iyooba. Leemisuwaassi Ay biittankka Haraphphoy sarotettaa leemiso gidiyoogan erettees hegaadankka hara hala malaalati alame ubbay issi birshshettaa imiyoobati de’oosona. yaaniyoo gishshawu 

hagaamalabati salo sa’a quganto gishshata giyoogaa. Daro xifate oosuwa oottiya xaafanealhati gujo leemisuwawu xeellikko worqqaa bonchcho banne maachcha giidi go’ettoosona zo’I ekkya oiishshaa gidikko siiquwa qonccissiyaaba giidi ekkoosona, xumay, urqqay qassi issi metto, tugganne waageeba gididoogaa bessees. Hagaamalabati nabbabbtya asawu birshshettaa immanawu wagssenna ubbay akeekana danddayees. 
Naa”anttoy qassi dalgga manttiyaawd heeraawwa, meezzetido ( pegional ) gishshaa geetettees. Hagaa mala gishshay mexi issi heeraninne he manttiyan de’iya asaa giddo xalaalan erettiyaa gishshatettaa. I he heeran de’iya asaa de’uwara, gmma nuwara, wogaara, meezziyaara oyqetti uttidaba. Etawu bantta heera asa xalaalan akeekettiyo gishshatettaa qaaday de’ees. Hagaa mala gishshati bantta heeraappe haakki haakkidi biyo wode eta birshshettay xuumiidai bees; ubba erettenna exxana danddayiyo hanotayka de’ana danddayees. Leemisuwassi issi asi oge malaa biishin garawu mali woykko godare malabi sinttaara ogiya shaakkidi biyaaba gidikko nu heeran iita qaada gishshatettan ekkana danddayees shin qassi hara manttiyan hagawu hara birshshettaa immiya gishshay de’ana danddayees. Issi asi huuphiyaappe tohuwa gakkanawu karerraba xalaalan maayyiyaaba gidikko immana danddayees. 
Heezzantto gishshatuwa qommoy issi izaawu gishshaa (personal symbol) geetettiyoogan erettees. Ha gishshatay issi xaafanchchay bariyyo medhdhi ekkidi issibaa haraban gishshayidi bar medhdhi xaafuwa giddon wottiyoo hanotaa. Ha gishshatidabay heeran woykko dalgga manttiyan gidin salo sa’a gufantton erettiyaaba gidenna. Hagaa mala gishshatiyaabatu birshshettaanne eti aybawu eqqidaakko eranawa daafurssees/ erettenna. Aybissi giikko I gishshatidobaa woykko he gishshat idabay aybissieqqidaakko eriyay xaafanchcha xaalla, Haggaa mala gishshatidabaa birshshidi/ shaakkidi eranawu daro akeekaanne pilggettan koshshees. Bala birshshiko issi asi balabaa gamma giidi ekkana danddayees. Ubba 
xaafanchchay mule qoppikkabeennabaa gishshataa giidi ekkana danddayiyoo gishshawu naagettana koshshees. 
                   Meezziya laappunaa 
Kaallidi lmettida oyshata hagaappe qommo baggaara imettida nibaa biyaaranne neeyyo kase de’iya eraara gattada gamma zzaro gidiyaagaa xaafada shiishsha. 
1) Modhdhi xaafuwa giddon zaari bessoy dumma dummd sohoton gelana  
   danddayees giida. Shin ayyo xifate oosuwa giddon geliyo gaasoti/ 
   maatoti aybakkonne qonccissada xaafada shiisha. 
2) Ne heeran beettiyaa batuppe heeraawa woykko meezetido 
   gishshatiyaaba gidana danddayiyaa neeni eriyobata shiishshada eti 
   aybbaa aybua gishshatidi medhdhi xaafo giddon eqqana/ gelana 
   danddayiyaakko qanccissa. 
3) sintta malaataynne gishshatiyaabay aybin dummatiyaakko qonccissuwa 
   xaafada shiishsha. 
4) Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon sinttabaa malaataa tekinikiya go’ettiyoogee 
   xifate oosuwaassi gidin dabbabbiyaa asawu ayba maaduwa immii? 
   birshshada xaafa. 
5) haasayaynne qonccissoy medhdhi xaafuwa giddon eeshshaawata 
   nabbabbiyageetuura ereti ssiyoo hanota yaagiya qofaa qonccissada 
   xaafaa ne kifile giddo de’iya laggetu sinttan nabbabbada sissa. 






USUPPUNTTO SHEMPPUWAA 
6. BILA XIFATIYAA BORI NASHUWA

Timirttiyaa sintta qofata: 
Ha timirttiya wurssoogaappe guyyiyan tamaare naati: 
?	Bori nashuwaa giyoobi aybakko qonccissidi yootana
?	Bori nashuwaa qommotanne eta eeshshata shaakkana
?	Bori nashuwa go'ata zuleyana
?	Dumma dumma medhdhi xaafotanne bila xifate oosota bori nashshana






   6.1. Bori nashuwaa aybatettaa 
Ha shemppuwan borinashowa giyoogee aybakko, mehdhi- xantuwa bori- nashoy aybawawu maaddiyakkonne dumma dumma bori nasho qommoti awugeetakko xeellana. Bori nashuwa giya qaalay 

waatta qaala. A giddon naa''u qaalati de'oosona. Koyro qaalay bori- giyaagaa. Bori giyoogee. Toochchidi woykko iita/ lo''o gidenna giiddi qofaa immiyoo hanotaa beessees. Nashuwa- giyoogee sabbiyoogaa gitayidi haasayiyoogaa woykko gamma giidi kenttiyoogaa giyoogaa. Hegaa gishshawu bori- nashsuwa yaagiyoogee.
Issi xaafettida medhdhi- xaafuwa woykko xifate oosuwa bala/iita/ giidi yootiyoogaa sidishshin nashuwa giyoogee qassi issi xifate oosuwa aani bali de’enna, I gamma giidi sabbiyoo hanotaa qonccissees. Hegaa gishshawa issi asi issi xifate oosuwa woykko issi mehdhi xaafuwa bari nabbabbiyoo wodiyan bari guuggiyan qoppidi bari eran yiggi xeellidi hagee bala hagee gamma yaagidi boi- neyshi kanttana danddayees. Medhdhi- xoofuwa/ xifate oosuwa bori nashshanawu xeelettiya huuphe yohoti de’oosona. medhdhi- xaafay iita-geettetti borettiya woykko gumma geetetti- nashettiyo yiggixeelettiyobati de'oosona. Hegeetun likettees/ xeelettees. 
Dumma dumma wodiyan daro eranchchati medhdhixaafoti woykko xifate oosoti borettiyoobata giidi – zu-leyidi/keessidi wottidobati de’oosona. Issi xaafettida oosoy eta zaari bessena kehshees giyoogaa. 
Biri nashuwa ootti kanttiyo ogeti bila xifatiya yiggi xeelliyoo miishshatuuna. Nashuwawkka hagaadan. Shin dumma dumma wodiyan dumma dumma eranchchati medhdhi- xaafuwa biri- nashawawu kessido yiggi xeelliyoobati de’oosona. Gido shin eti dumma dumma wodotun demmatidosonanne dummatoosona. 
Bori-nashoy issi xifate oosuwa okkidi he bila xifatiyabaa lo”o era oyqqiyoogan xifatiya meraa shaakki eriyoogan bila xifatiya yiggi xeelliyoo kane bata paacci xeelliyoobatun wottidi he oosuwa minonne shuqi/kefa miyyiya xeelliyaagan xekkaa immiyoo hanotaa woykko eratettan kamida paacei xeeluwa woykko prddiyoogaa giyoogaa.                                               

6.2. Bori- nashuwa Go''aa/maaduwa 

Xifatiya oosuwa giddon bori- nashuwaassi daro maadoy woykko go’ay de’ees. Ha go’ay/ maadoy de’iyo bori- nashoy ay asinne immiyo mela bori nashuwa gidennan xifate oosuwan meezetda daro eranchchatu borinashuwa go’aa immiyaagee medhdhi- xaafuwubawa woykko xifate oosuwawa eri baynna asi bori- nashshana danddayennanne I/A bori nashshikkonne ayyo go’i de’ehnan aggana danddayees. Gido shin qossi eranchcha xaafanchchaa borinashoy medhdhi- xaaafuwa xaafidaagawu gita maaduwa immees. Beri nashoy issi xifate oosuwa bolli polettiyo wode heezzu bollati maadettoosona koyruwan xaafiyaageeti, naa”anttuwan nabbabbiyageeti, heezanttuwan, biitta xifate duretay. Ha heezzu bollati bori nashuwappe waanidinne qassikka aybaa maadettiyaakko kaallidi huuphiyan huuphiyan eta reellana.
Tobbiyoo oyshata.  
Kaallidi de’iya oyshata ne loggetuura heezzaa oyqqiya citaa medhdhada tobboogaappe guyyiyan efuwa gamma zaaruwa shilshshada xaafa. 
1) Bari nashuwa issi asi ay ogiyan aattin xaafanchchay go’ettii? 
   birshshadu yoota. 
2) medhdhi xaafuwa beri nashoy nnbbabbiyaagaa aybin maaddii? 
3) xifate oosuwa bori nashoy issi biittau bila xifateya ay ogiyan maaddii? 
   Qonccissa. 
          I. Xaafanchchatussi immiyo maaduwaa 
Qommo baggaara medhdhi- xaafuwa woykko xifate oosuwa bori nashoy xaafanchchawu maaddees giida. I waanidi xaafanchchaa maaddii giikko, medhdhi xaafuwa woykko i=xifate oosuwa medhdhiyaagee/ xaatiyaagee xaafanchchan.Bori nashshiyaagaa oosoy qossi xaafanchchaan xaafettida oosota boriyoogaanne nashshiyoogaa woykko pacci xeelliyoogaa. Bori- nashshiya agawunne xaafanchchawu keehi mino goytotettay de’ees 

giyoogaa. Xaafiyoo oosoynne issi xaafa oosuwa bori nashshiyoogee dumma dumma oosota. Xaafanchchay xifate ooso xaalaalaa oottana danddayiyoogaadan, bori nashshiyaagee xaafettida oosota bori nashshiyoogaa xalaalaa oottana danddayees. Eti bantta ooso xalaalaa oottiyaa asa. Gido shin issi issi wode issi xaafanchchay bori nasho oosuwakka oottana danddayees qassikka bori nashshiyaagee medhdhi- xaafuwa woykko hara xifate oosota oottana danddayees. Hagaa mala asi naa”u dumma qaray de”iyoogaa. Hegaamala oosoy nashettana bessees. Xaaxi- waaxiyoo wode ha naa”u dumma oosanchchati bantta oosuwan shaahettokkana/ etawu mino gaytotettay de’ees giyoogaa. Mehdhi-xaafuwa xaafanchchaay xifate oosuwa xaafennaakko bori nashshiyaagee xifatiya bori- nashshana danddayenna. Bori nashshiyaayee de’iyoo gishshatawu. Xaafanchchay barioosuwa shiishshi bessidi bori- nashissees. Woykko A oosoy paacetti xeelettiyoo qaadaa demmees giyoogaa. 
Hegaa gishshawu xaafunchchaykka bori nashshiyaagaa bori- nashshiyaagaa qassi xaafanchchay maaddees giyoogaa. Shin xaafanchchay imettiya bori- nashuwaappe aybaa go’ettii woykko maadettii yaagiya qofa ane kaallidi xeelloos. Koyruwan issi xifate oosoy xaafanchchaa guuggiyaappe kiyiyaa era ooso. Ha xifate ooso pancettiyoo wode qassi A zokkossan xaafanchchay de’ees. Hegaas gishshatawu ha xifate oosuwara xaafanchchaykka issippe denddis- oo- gee attenna. Ha xaafanchchaa oosoy muluranne puuli de’iyoo ooso gididi beettikko bori nashuwa oottiyaagan ooso xalaala gidennan xaafanchchaykka nashetti kanttiyoogee attenno. Megaa gishshawu xaapanchchay. Bori nashuwaappe demmiyoo go’ay A sunttay A lo’o oosuwadan asaa giddon eretettiyoogaa. Naa”anttoy bori nashuwa giyoogee- issi asi coo suure gidenna ogiyaan denddidi leta miyye xalaalaa booddiyoo hanota gidenna. Issi xidate oosuwaassi lefa miyyee awugee mino miyyee awugee giidi naa”aakka ekki xeellidi beettiyaa akeekuwaara de’iyaa paacci xeeuwa ootti simmidi lefa 

miyyeenne mino miyyee shaahetti erettanaadan oottees. Hegaappe simmin xaafanchchay bari mino miyyiya mintti tishshi oottidi baanawunne lefa miyyiya qassi guuttidi/ aggidi giigissiiddi paxa puulaara de’iya asaa wozana shammiya xifate oosuwa ootti kessanawu keehippe maaddees. 
    Heezzanttuwan, bori nashuwa oosoy issi xifate oosuwan. eeshshan, utettaaninne meran xeelettees. Leemisuwaassi issi bori nashshiyoogee issi adussa medhdhi xaafuwa bori nashshanawu koyyikko issi adussa medhdhi- xaafoy ay malatana bessiyaakko I xeelettana bessiyoo huuphe xeellettiyaabatati de’oosona. Qantta medhdhi xaafuwawukka hegaadan. Hagaadan haniyoo wode issi bori nashshiyaagee ha xifate oosotu eeshshata birshshiddi cora dumma dumma xifate ooso mararati kumttana bessiyoobata aaro eriiddi baanaadan bori- neshoy go’ees giyoogaa. Oyddanttuwan bori- nashuwaappe xaafanchchay maadettanabay, issi xaafanchchay ay xekkan beettiyaakko, biroon doommiya bakko/ lammachchakko, ginaa heeran de’iyaabakko woykko daro meezzee  de’iyoobakko shaahetti erettiyoogee daro maaddees. Issi bori nasho oosuwan beettiya xifate ooso xalaalay xeelettenna. I hara xifate oosotuurakka paacci xee;ettidi ay xekkaa ekkiyaakko malaateesinne minnidi ginttanawu oottanawu go’aa immees. Wurssettan, dumma dumma xaafanchchatussi etawu etawu haratuugaappe dummati ekkiya eti xaafana koyyiyoo ogeti de’oosona: Issi issi xaafanchchaa qonccissuwa darissoosona: Tssooti issooti adussa qofa qahshota go’ettoosona. Issooti issooti eeshshaawatu haasayaa darissidi xaafishiishshooso na’to issooti issooti qassi hara xaafanchchatu xaafiyo hiilla xalaalaa laatti ekkidi bne hiillan go’ettsshin beettees. Bori nashoy xaafanchchatu qotaa gogettaara, issi qoppennan gayttiyaabaa shiishshi besuwara woykko etawu de;iya de’uwaa xeelaa xifatiya baggaara xaafenchchata zaari phppliiyoogaan eti bessanawu gaettiiddi biya minonne lefa miyyiyaanne lo’o/ mino miyyiyo bessiyoogan sinttawu baanaadan akeekaa immana danddayees. 

             II. Nababiyaa asawu immiyo go''aa 
Issi xifate oosuwa ubba nabbabbiya asi xeellidi lage akeekccanne era demmlnna aggana danddayees. Nabbabbiya asaa meezzee dummatiy oogaadankka bantta dumma dumma de’o aazziyaara gatti xeelliyoo wode eta akeekay dummatana danddayees. Issi issi xifate oosotun keehi ciima gidiya qofaynne xuura gidiyaabi de'ana danddayiyoo gishshatawu ubba xaafettido aswu (nabbabbiya asawu qoncce gidennan aggana danddayees. Hegaa gishshawu issi bori- nashshiyaagee hegaa mala qoncce gidennabata, xuura gididabata woykko hittifiro gididabata qonccissidinne nabbabbishin naababbiyaagawu gelibeennabata qonccissidi akeekanaadan oottiyoogaa. 
Dumma dumma xaafanchcnwu dumma dumma dooriyoo qofaa zuleyiyoonne xaafiyoo hiillay de’ees. Bori nashshiyaagee bari- oosuwa oottieyoo gishshatawu nabbabbiyaageetti dumma dumma xaafanchchatu xaafuwa hiillaa, halchchuwaanne aadhdhanawu koyottida aaho yohiwa shaakki eranaadan maaddees. 
Heezzanttuwaan, Bori-nashoy xifate oosotussi xekkaa immanawu maaddees. Hegaa gishshatawu nabbabbiya asati bori- nashsuwa kanttidi lo’onne mino geetettida xifate oosota malaatees. Nabbabbiyagaanne nashettiya xifate oosuwa gattiyaagan bori- nashoy nabbabbiyageetawu gita maaduwa lmmees. 
                III. Issi biittaa bila xifatiyaayyo dureta 
Bori nashoy issi biittaa bila- xifatiyaa duretaayyo daro maaduwa immees. Issi issi biittawu A ayyo ayyo A bila xifatiya duretay de’ees. Xaafettida bila xifatiya idin odettida bila xifatiya gidinkka. Ubba qassi xaafettida bila –yifariya xeelliyaagan I dicci diccidi biyoy he biittagiddon de'iyaa xaafanchchatu mino oosuwaana. Xaafiyaageeti xaafiyo gishsha xalaalan xifate oosoy diccenna. Ha xaafettida xifate oosota bori- nashshiyogee kaneba. Hegaa gishshatawu bori nashoy issi biittan dicciddi de’iya xifate oosoy murutan diccanaadan daro maaddees.                      

Bila xifatetu paacci xeeloya amaara xaafanchchatuwninne amara biittatu xifate oosotun eqqi aggiyaaba gidenna. Hara biittatu bila xifatiya duretaanne dagattaa paacci xeelliyoogan eti de’iyoo xekkaa woykko ay keena diccidaakko yiggi xeelles. Hegaa gishshatawu issi biyttaa giddon de’iya xifate hiillaa lefa miyyee giigiiddi baanaadaninne murutankka diccanaadan go’ees. Murutan diccogaappe guyyiyan kare biittaa xifate oosotuura annaacettana danddoyees. Hagaadan haniiddi issi biittaa xifate oosoy keehi dicciyoo xekkaa gattees. Hagaa mala hanotay qassi issi biittan de’iya bila- xifate diccanaadaaninne hara hara xaafanchchati merettanaadaaninne diccanaadan gita go’aa immees. Xaaxi waaxiyoo wode bila xifatiya bori nashoy minni minni wolqqaa kedsi kessidi biyoogee issi biittawunne xaafiya izaawatuyyo gita maaduwa immees giyoogaa. Ha ogiyan bila xifate oosoti bantta xekkaa naagidaageeta gidiyoogaa bolli etan beettiya balabati xayi xayi boosona giyogaa. 
            
  Koyro meezziya 
Kaallidi shiiqida shatussi qantta tobbiyaappe simmidi gamma zaaro gidana intte giyogeeta xaafidi shiishshite. Issi issi oyshatussi aaho qonccissuwa xaafi shiishshite. 
1) Bori- nasho oosuwassi bila xifatiya yiggi xeellanawu kaneba gidiyaabati 
   awugeetakkonne zuleyite. 
2) xaafanchchaa oosunwaninne bori nashshiyaagaa oosuwan dummatetti 
   de'ii? Issoy haraa oosuwa oottana danddayi danddayennee? Waanidi qonccissa. 
3) Bori nashoy nabbabbiyaagawu xaafiyaagawunne bila xifatiyaayyo immiyo go'aa hagaappe 
   qommo baggaara imettida qantta noottiya bolli ne qofaa gujja xaafada kifile giddon intte 
    laggetussi qonccissuwa shiishshite. 
4) xaafanchchay bori nashshiyaagaa qasesi bori nashshiyaagee bila xifatiya xaafanchcha gidana 
    danddayii? Qonccissite. 
5) Bori- nashoy hummunaawa paacci xeelonne pirddiyo hanota yaagiya  qofay aybaa qonccissii? 
     Birshshadi xaafite. 

             6.3. Bori nashshiyaagaa poluwaanne asatettaa 
Tobbiyo oyshata 
Kaallidi de'iya oyshata tubbidi gamma zaaruwaa immite. 
1) Bori nashshiyaagaa asatettay waanana bessiyaaba malatii? 
2) Bori- nashshiyaagaanne xaafiyaagaa asatettay malatettana bessii? Ay ogiyan? 
3) Issi bori nashshiyaagee bari oosuwaappe kasetidi ay mala era oyqqana bessees giidi qoppeetii? 
    Tobbite. 
Bori nashshiyaagee eraara de'iya asa. Bori- nashshiyoo eraykka bariyyo coo yiyaaba gidennan qalame timirttiya eraara keehi oyqqetti uttidaba. I saynisse oosuwaaranne gita eraara oyqqetti uttidaba. Ane kaallidi de’iya bori- nashshiyaagaa yiggi xeelliyo huuphe yohota issippe xeelloos. 
Ha kaallidi de’iyaageetuppe issuwaanne paccinchchennan kunttiyaagaa bori- nashshiyaagaa giidi ekkeettees. 

1. Bori nashuwa eraynne awu koshshay diyogaa
Issi asi haattappe maatappe coo denddidi bori- nashshiyaaba gidana danddayenna. Koyro issi asawu eray de’ana bessees. Eroykka de’anawu koyro issi izaawussi bori- nashuwa  oosuwassi keshshay de’iyoo asa gidana bessees. Issi asawu koshshi de’ennan  issibaa polana woykko oottana giidi denddenna. Bori nashoy guuggiya ooso, I daro wodiya, abbiya, hakkaa, miishshaa yarshsh issiya keehi wolqqaama ooso. Hagaa mala metuwaaranne waayiyaara de’iya oosuwa asi bari koshshan oottiyoobappe attin asi/ harabi sugido gishattawu hanana bessenna. Issi asi asan sugettidi woykko haraban sugettidi bari koshshaappe kareera ha oosuwan geliyaaba gidikkogyfana danddayenna. Bori nasho oosoy izaawu oottana A baggaara de'iya meto ubbaa xoonana baaxetana giidi asi bana ammanttidi geliyoo ooso. Issi asi gallassaa qammaara utti be'idi dumma dumma nu biitta giddonne kare biittaa xaafanchchati xaafido oosota nabbabbiyoogaa, pilggi xeelliyoogaa, kaallidikka bari baynna suure pirddaa immiyoogaa gidiyoogan ayyo imotaanne koshshaa koshshees giyoogaa. Koshsha xalaalakka gidennan gita eraanne abbiya koyyees. 
Bori-nashoy xuufiyaa xuuraa qonccissiyoogan xaafanchchaay wottana koyyido cuccumaa pilggidi demmiyoogan, xifatiya ogiya shaakkiyoogan, xaafanchchay xaafiyo hiillaa pilggiyoogan wudiyoo gishshawu ha polota oottanawu daro era koshshees. Hanotata kanttidi xeelliyo, issi yohowa hara yohuwaara gattiyoogan yiggi xeelliyoogaa birshshiyoogaaninne qaari bessiyo dumma qaray/ eray de'ana bessees. 
                                  2. Gammanne suure pirddaa iimmiyagaa 
Bori- nashoy issi bila xifatiyaa oosuwa lefanne mino miyyiya xeelliyaagan gamma woykko suure pirddaa immiyoogaa. Daannatettay qassi gamma gidiyaanne zuppe maadoy baynna la'a gidiyoogee naagettees. Issi xaafanchchaa dosiyoo gishawu woykko ixxiyo gishshawu woykko eriyonne erenna gishshatawu maaddettennanne qophettenna. Haray qassi issi medhdhixaafuwan woykko bila- xifatiya cuuccumay bori- nashshiyagaa qofaara malatettido gishshawu woykko phalqqetta gidido gishshawu pirdday geellattannabessenna. Hagaa mala issi baggi uttidi pirddiyobi bori- nasho geetettenna. Hageetu mala gidikko etan gammatetti beettenna. Eta buzo hulluuqoy phoolidoba gidiyoo gishshawu xaafanchchaa ooso gidennan borinashshiuagua hulluuqoy phooliyooba gidiyoogan geella giyogaa. 
Bori nashshiya ay asinne I eriyo xaafanchchaara gaytotetti de'iyo gishshatawu pirddaa loyttana bessenna. Bori nashuwan ayyo siyettiya sissaa /hulluuquwa qoncciissana bessenna. Bori nashshiyaagee ixxiyo xaafanchchaa oosuwa boridi qassi dosiyo xaafanchchaa oosuwa nashshiyoogee hummunaawaba gidenna woykko 

A oosoy maaddiyooba/nashshiyooba gidokkona. Hegaa gishshatawu issi bori nashshiyagee tumanchcngidiyogan /itaa woykko borettiyabaa boridi qassi gamma gidiya lo'obaa lo'o giidi tuma gidiya pirddaa immiyaasa gidana beses. Bori- nashshiyagee baayyo siyottiya buzo hulluu quwappe haakkidi tuma gidida ba xalaalaa wottana koshshes. 
                                        3. Aaho bila- xifatiya era keelidaagaa 
Bila xifatiya oosuwa pilggiya bori-nashshiyaagee aybaappenne kasetidi I oottiyo oosuwa aybatettaanne waatada ootto giyagaa erana bessees. Bori nashshiya gee ba erenna yohunwaninne akeekibeenna xuuraa giddo gelidi akeekibeenna yohuwa bolli aynne gaana danddayenna. Hegaa gishshawu bila-xitatiyaa bolli bori-nashshiyaagee bari qofaa immanaappe kasetidi bila xifatiya aybatettaa, A meretaabaa, dicnchaanne laamiyaabaa, utettaanne ohettaa baa, eta qommotanne shiishshiyo hiillatunne bila xifatiya maearatunne tekiniketu-------- h.h.m. dumma dammabatu bolla ciimma eray de'ana bessees. Ubba borinshshiyaagee xaafanchchaappe aadhdhiya bila xifatiyabaa eranaadan naagettees. Bori- nashshiyagee ay bila xifate oostunikka keehi minonne gita eray de'an koshshees. Issi xaafanchchaa lefa miyyiya woykko balaa maxi maxidi kessiyogan giigisso qofaa immana danddayiyaagee koyro dyyo bilaxifatiya eray de'iyo wodiyaana. Qantta medhdhi xaafuwan woykko danttuwa bori nashuwa oottanawu koyro qantta medhdhi xaafoy woykko danttoy aybakonne eta xaafiyo ogeta, seerata erana bessees. Danttuwa yiggi xeelliyobatun qantta medhdhi xaafoy paacettenna. Bori- nashshiyagee dumma dumma bila xifatiya kaalettiya eeshshatu eray de'iyo asa. 
                       4. Bila- xifatiyaappe kareera hara bagga eraykka de'iyoogaa 
Ha bila- xifatiya oosoy cora dere asaa duussaara ohetti uttidaba. Mexi issi (xon''a) bagga gidida eraa xalaalaa oyqqidi asaa na'aa de'uwaa hanotaa akeekanawu daro wayissees. Issi era baggi bana danddayidi haraara gayttennan de'iyaabi baawa. Issoy hara era bagga gidiya yaraara dumma dumma ogiyan gaytotettaanne maaduwa oottees.                   
Bila xifatee woykko medhdhi xaafoy bari giddon asaa taarikiya oyqqees; heegaayyo qassi issi dere asaa giddon de'iya asaa taarikiya erana bessees. Issi izaawa shaakkidi A amuwa, koshshan, hulluuquwa eeshshaa akeekidi boohchchiya xaafiyoogee keehi xoshshiyaba. Qaalata dooridi puulaynne shonggay de'iyo ogiyan xifate oosuwa shiishshanawu ubbay eriyoo haasayaa gidin diratto birshshettata shaakkanawu xaafettiyo doonaa giraameliya wogata naagidi shiishshanawu…h.h.m. era keehi maaddees. 
Xaafanchchawu hageeti dumma dumma erati A oosuwawu maaddoosona bori nashsh hiyagawukka keehi koshshoosona. 
Issi bila xifatiya oosoy ay wodiya asata gishshatidi eqqidee? He wodiyan de'ida asaa wogaa, maaraa mankkaa bari giddo gelissidee? Xifatiy wogaa, seeraa utettaa, kaallidee? Giyo oyshata hegaadan hara oyshatakka denttiiddi hageetu yuushuwan shiishshanawu dumma dumma era macarata/ daashshata erana bessees. 
                  5. Bori-nashuwa oosuwa meezzee de'iyoonne A heeran loohida asa 
Bori- nashuwa eray barkka issi keehi gita pilggettaa yara. Bori- nashoy issi timirtte qommodan tamaareti loohanawu bessiya hannanna. Hegaa gishshawu bori- nashshiyaagee tamaare soo ge'idi bori nashuwa oosuwan loohida asa giyogaa. Ha hannannan loohiya asi koyrottidi bori nashoy aybakkonne bori nashshiyaagaa giyogee aybakkonne shaakki eriya asa. Bori nashshiyo seeraa, ottiyo ogeta bori nashsho eran bessiyanne bessennabati aybakko shaakki eridi he oosuwan geliya asi hagee loohidaagaa. Ha llohuwa bollaanikka bari hummunnccaninne asatettan minnida meezzee de'iyo asa bori- nashshiyagaa giyogee. Meezzee woykko timirtteenne loohiyo hanotay baynnasan tamaaridanne xoqqa biri nashshiyo eray beettenna. 
Eranchcha bori- nashshiyaagaa geetettiyagee hagaappe qommo baggaara nu denttido yohotanne hara koyettiyabatakka kunttiya asa. Eranchcha bori nashshiyagee dumma pilggi xeelliyo eraynne koshshay de'iyo gammanne yiggi xeeluwara de'iya tumu pirddaa immiya bila- xifatiyanne harabatu eraynne akeekay de'iyo, xaafanchchatussinne eta oosuwawu bonchchuwa immiya, xaatanchchatu balawunne lefa miyyiyawu giigisso qofa gidiyabaa immiya shiishshiyanne ogiya oyttiya, xaaxi waaxiyo wode ba yiggi xeelliyoobatun gammanne tuma gidiya borinashuwa immana danddayiya asa. 
                                6.4. Bori- nashuwa qommota
Bori- nashay odussa wodetussi takkidanne bari garssan daro laameti polettishin yiida timirtte qommo. A aybatettaw, A halchchuwawunne I koshshiyo hanotaabaa, A qommuwabaa daro aadhdhida wodetun dendida bila xifatiya xeelatudan bori-nashshiyagaa xeelaadan dumma dumma ogetun birshshettiiddinne dumma dumma meraa oyqqiiddi yiida era. 
Bori- nashuwa qommota xeelliyagan bila-xifatiya shiishshuwa bollan be'idoogaadan ubbaykka bari wodiyaadan bari wodiyaadan wudiyoo baggaynne sintta qofay hegaadankka bila xifatiya bori- nashoy I hanido/ polettido xeelaadan dumma dumma bori nasho qommoti beettidosona. Dumma dumma bori-nashuwa qommoti de'ikkonne issoy issuwappe keehi dummatiyaaba gidokkona. Issoy haraara amarabatun gayttees; woykko issoy haraa giddon mitettana danddayees. Eta issippetettay amaridabatuunappe attin mule ubbabaana gidenna. 
Hanno gakkanawu be'ettidaageetane oosuwan pee'ida daro bori-nasho qommotu giddoppe dumma dumma bori-nashshiya geetuuninne xaafiyageetu giddon zaaretettidi xeesettiyaageetu giddoppe guuttata ane issippe xeelloos. 
                 6.4.1. Eeshshaa Bori-nashuwa 
Ha borinashoy ano oottidi xeelliyoy woykko denddo ootti xeelliyoy is dare asaa ayyaanaamanne ayyaanaama gidenna eeshshaa hanotaa oyqqees.  Ha bori nasho qommoy beni benippe doommidi de'iyaagaa. Ha eeshsha bori nashuwa nu giyogee issi wodiyan de'iya dere asay bari am manawuwaranne wogaara hanotata gattiyogan koolido lo''o geetettiya eeshshata issi bila xifatiya oosoy ay keena bessi? yaagiyagaa bayra yoho oottidi xeelleesinne pilggees. Issi bila xifatiya oosoy bari giddon lo'o eeshsha bessiyaabanne tamaarissiyaaba gidikko hegee keehi lo''o ooso giyogaa. Hagaappe kareera eeshshaa pilggettaa bori nashoy bila-xifatiya oosoy waanidi shiiqide? Yaagiya tekinikiyara oyqettida hanotata qoppenna. 



               6.4.2. Kahaayyo bori- nashuwa 
“ Ha kanaayo borinashoy issi odetiyabappe /theory/ denddidi xaafanchchaanne eeshshaawatu guugge giddo hulluuguwanne kahaa pilggiyaagau.” /Asfaa zarihuna 1992:362/ Issi bila xifatiya giddoy keehi pilggettiyakko xaafanchchaa oonatettaanne eeshshaa I shiishshido bila xifatiya giddon oottido qonccissuwappe woykko I eeshshaawata misilidogaappe beettan danddayees yaagiya ammanuwan xaufanchchaa oonatettaa koyyiyoogan wudiya bori nasho qommo. Ha bori nashuwa qommoy xaafanchcha buzo oosuwappe konttidi A de’o taarikiya pilggettawukka aadhdhana danddayees. Bila xifatiya cuucumawunne I xaafettido hiillawu ha bori- na shuwa qommoy soho immenna. Ha bori nashuwassi bayranne ano allaalle xaafanchchaa cozanaanne oonotettaa demmiyogaana. Xaafanchchay bari xifate oosuwan qonccissiyo woykko eeshshaawatussi immiyo eeshshay bari qosettida oonatettaa, xeelaa woykko hanotaa qonccissanaassa yaagiyogan xifate oosuwa gidennan xaafanchchaa oonatettaa qonccissiyogan wudiya bori nasho. 
             6.4.3. Deretettaa bori-nashuwa 
Deretettaa bori nasho giyogawu bayra wudiyoobay bila-xifatiya oosoy bari giddon oyqqiyo dere asaa yohoy bari aattiyo biitaaninne bessiyo asaa de'uwan geliyo hanotaana. Hagaappe kasee baggan be'idoogaadan ay bila- cifatiya oosuwawu ano yohoy asaanne dere asaa. Bari garssan bila-xifatee issi dere asaa wogaa guyyeppe kaalli siida mayzziyan ma''iyan de'iyaaba zaari bessana koshshees. Deretettaa bori nashuwa bayra xeelay woykko wudiyoobay bila xifate kiyidonne I merettanawu gaasonne pultto gidida dere asaa de'uwa mereay ay keenaa beettidaakko yaagiya oyshaa bariyo allaalle oottiyoogaa. Hagaa garssan xaafanchchaykka he wediyanne I kiyido dere asaappe pulttido ba gidiyoogee issippe be'ettiyaba. Hagaa mala bori-nashshuwa polanawu bori nashshiyagee bari huuphe he bila xifatee oosettido woykko kiyido wodiyanne dere asaa hanotaa, meezziya eranaadan koyettees. Bila xifateenne asaa de'oy issoy issuwappe shahettenna hanotay minnidi pilggettees. 
                    6.4.4. Bila xifatiya utettaa/qottaa bori nashuwa 
Ha bori nashuwa qommoy bayra oottidi xeelliyoy issi bila xifatee shiiqido hiillay. Utettay woykko meretay ay macatiyakko yaagiyaagaa. He xifote oosuwa giddon beettiya asatu duussaa honotaawu, dere asaa tunatettaa haasayanawu/ denttanawu ayyo halchchoy de’enna. I ano oottido denddiyoy woykko I kaseiyoy bila xifatiya utettaara gayttiyagan beettiya puulay shiqiyoogaa xalaalaana. Utettay giigin poolay kiyidi beettiyoy doonaana gidiyo gishshatawu hageekka pilggettees. Qaalatu go'etay giraamerireenne geliyoo ogeti go'an pee'iyoogaakka xeellees. Asatettaabaynne ammanttiyaa taarike kidiyogeenne aggiyoogee hagan daro qotissiyaaba gidenna. Haray atto shin A ohettawukka guuttappe attin daro sohuwa immenna. 
Bori nashuwa qammoti cora gidiyogaa hagaappe qommo baggaara be'idi kauttida. Hagan nuuni be'iiddi deiyogeeti coo be'i kanttanaassappe attin haratiuka deoosona. He ubba bori nasho qommotikka kaalliyo etayyo buzo gidida denddo qofaynne wudiyobay de'ees. Gido shin eta aakkin xuumminikka eti issoy issuwara dabbotiyo ogetikka de'oosona. 
Hagaappe pude baggaara dumma dumma qommotun shaahettidi beettiya bori nashuwa merati eti wuddidi pilggiyo yoghota xeelliyaagan be'ettidi sunttettidaageetappe attin issi imettitida bori- nashuwa ciimmatettaanne goobatettay, keehi ka'ibeenna woykko yelagatetta bessiyageeta gidokkona. 

Leemisuwassi deretettaa boretettaa borinashuwa ogiyan issi bila xifatee shiiqidi de'ishin A borinasho oosoy yedanne asi coo daattettidi xaafidoba gidana danddayees. Ha ciimmatettaanne aahotettaa yiggi xeeuiyo yohotun xeelettiyo wodiyan qassi bori- nashoy ay mala agiyaeenikka shilqikko naa''u ogiyan shaakkidi be'ana danddayottees. Koyroy hada bori nashshiyaagaa ogidishi naa''anttoy qoassi eran kumida bori nashuwa.
                                 6.4.5. Hada bori nashuwaa
Hada borinashoy bori-nashuwa era gidin bila-xifatiya eri baynnan de'ishin issi bila xifatiya oosuwa siyidi gidin, nabbabidi woykko xeellidi he xifatee A wozanan ayssido hulluuquwa kaallidi (woykko ayyo malatidabaa) eziggi siyidi aattiyo bori- nashuwa. Issi bila xifatee woykko medhdhi xaafay bari ohettan gidin utettan laafa gidikkonne qassi nabbabiyaagee naababishin A hulluuquwara woykko A de'uwa meezziyara malatettido gishsha xalaalawu hagee malaaliya xifate ooso aani issi wottiyoobinne de'enna. A xaafida xaafanchchay keehi minonne eranchcha asa giidi nashshi kanttana danddayees. Hara baggaara qassi issi medhdhi xaafoy woykko issi bila xifatee keehi lo'o gididi A oosoy ha nabbabiyaagawu injjiya darenna ixxido gishshatawu woykko ayyo akeekettennan ixxido gishshata xalaalawu hagee pattenna laafa ooso ha bila xifatiya xaafida xaafanchchay lammachcha daro aazzee baynna laafa giyo hanotay ha bori nasho qomuwan xaaxi waaxettees. Hagaa mala ogiyan imettiya bori nashoy bori- nasho eran gelidi gophphetiyaaba gidenna. Hagee issi izaawu bariyo siyettida sissan amppidi coo haasayiyo hadaba giyoogaa. Hagaa mala bori nashoy ooni erii geellodan televizhiniyan, eraadooniyan h.h.m aadhdhana danddayees. He wodiyan qaadaa demmida asi baayyo soyettidabaa haasayana danddayees. Hagaa mala eri baynnan immiyo bori nashoy bila xifatiya oosuwa appe bollaara xaafanchchaa dendduwa qohidi bari oosuwa minni oottenaadan xaafanchchaa hulluuquwa onggees. Hagawu qohiya bagaa dares. Xaaxi waayiyoo wode bila- xifatiya bori- nahuwa eri baynnna asi issi bila- xifatiya oosuwa nabbabidi cooo immiyo bori nashoy hada bori nasho geetettees. Hagaa nala akeeki baynna bori nashoy xaafanchchaa hulluuquwa qohiyo hanotay dei'yo gishshatawu naagettana bessees. 
                6.4.6. Eranchchaawa bori nashuwaa 
Enranchchaawa bori nashuwa giyoogee bori nashuwa eranchchan imettiya eranchchaawa gidida qofaa. Bori nashshiyaagee bori nashuwa eray de'iyoonne aani loohida asa. Hegaa mala asi. Aattiyo bori nashoy eranchchawu bori nashuwa geetettees. Hagaappe qommo baggaara bori nashowa giyogee aybee giya baggan denddida yohota ubbaa kunttana danddayiya bori nashuwa giyoogaa. Ha asan aadhdhiya bori nashoy gamma gidida pirddaynne dumma dumma yohot qofan gelido pirdday beettiyooba. Ano gidida bila xifatiya yiggi xeelliyobata shiishshidi A xeelliyoogan shiiqida bila xifadiya xeellidi akeekaaninne daro hassayan pilggidi aattiyo bori- nashuwa. Bila xifatiya giddon beettiya lefa miyyetussi maado gidiya qofata shiishshiyaanne malaatiya bila-xifatiya gita eray de'iyo asa. Bori nashshiyagee xaatanchchatussi bessiya bonchchuwa immiyaasanne bari hulluuquwaa(bariyo siyettiya sissa xalawan kaalettennan yaa baggan gidin ha baggaa maaddennan bari oosuwa kaaletuwunne seera xalaalaa xeellidi pirddaa immiya loohida asa. Ha asan imettiya bori nashoy nabbabiyagawu, xaafanchchawu nne bila xifatiya oosuwawu gita maaduwa immuees. Eranchchaawa bori-nashoy ha''i wodiyan dumma dumma xombbe  gidiya maxaafata xeellidi naqaashata shiishshiyogan ha bori nasho qommoy gita era cuccunttees. Gaasoykka ha oosoy eranchchan oosetti woykko xaafetti simmidi gamma gidiya ogiyan pirdday imettiyo ooso. 



























LAAPPUNTTO SHEMPPUWAA
                                       7. DIRAAMAA
Ha shemppuwaa sintta qofata:  Ha shemppuwaa tamaaridi wurssidoogaappe 
simmin tamaareti: 
?	Diraamaa birshshettaa qonccissana
?	Diraamaa kane qofaa qonccissana
?	Diraamaa qommota shaakkidi erana
?	Diraamaa ufurettata yootana











7.1. Geluwaa
Ha shemppoy  diraamaa bila eraara eretissanawu doommees. Ha shemppoy ichchashu sohotussi shaahettees. Koyro shaahoy diraamaa kane qofaabaa tobbiyaaba gidishiin naa''anttoy qassi diraamaa qommota qonccissees. Heezzantto shaahoy diraamay bari giddon oyqqiyoobatubaa yootees.  Oyddanttoy qassi loohiyaageeti ootti be'iyoo dumma dumma oosotu woykko meezzetu bollinne wurssettay loohiyaageeti aaro nabbabuwawu go'ettana bessiyaa miishshata bessiyaa zuliyaa oyqqees.

7.2. Diraamaa Kane qofaa (The concept of Drama)
Diraamay bila xifatiyaa mera gididi xeelliyaanne siyiyaa asaa/galchchaa sinttan eeshshaawati bollan beettidi poli/ootti bessiyooba. Diraamay woykko kaassay (play) eeshshaawati haasayiyoobaaninne oottidi bessiyooban nuuyyo taarikiyaa yootees. I medhdhi xaafuwaadaanikka benippe doommidi keehi adussa wodiyaawu de'idaba/takkidaba. 

Diraamay koyro merettidoy Beni Giriise (Greece) yaagiyoo biitteena. Gidoppe attin I ay wode doomettidaakko hiqqa wode giidi eriyaa woykko yootana danddayiyaa asi de'enna. Diraamaa doomettawu dumma dumma cora tiyooreti (theories) de'oosona. Ha tiyooretuppe issoy leemusuwaassi woygii giikko “ooni erii geello diraamay dichchaa doommoy beni beni wode doomettan de'iyaa ammano baala bonchchuwaara ohettidabatun asay bari godatuppe anjjuwaa demmanawu ootti bessiyoobaara ohettidi yiis”. Yaagiyaagaa. (The World book ensiclopedia, Vol.5). Hara tiyooree qassi “Diraamay issi hayqqida Gooba asaa goobatettaa gayranawu yootanawu duufuwaa lanqqen sabaa yettaa shiishshiyaa yexxiyaa citaara ohettidi yiis.” Yaagees. Xaaxi waaxo hanuwaan diraamay asaa naati bantta meretan issi hanida taarikiyaa yootanawu asaa naatu gomppaa giddon gita siiqoy de'iyoogaa bessees gaana danddayettees.  

Tumu haasayan diraamaa “drama” yaagiyaa qaalay yiidoy Girike biittaappe gidishin ayyo birshshettaykka “oottiyoogaa, bollaa qaattan oottidi bessiyoogaa woykko ootti poliyooba giyoogaa” (to perform or to act). Ha denddo gidida bayra ano qaalay odiyoobay diraama giyoobi asi bari bollaa qaattaa/kaassaa go''ettidi oosuwan bessiyooba giyoogaa. Hara qaalan diraamaa giyoogee bila hayyo xifate qommo gididi haasayaanne poluwaa (action and dialogue) bari giddon haphphees giyoogaa. Diraamay chii medhdhi xaafuwaaranne danttuwaara geeddarettana danddayees aybissi giikko I bari giddon aaho hayse malabaa haasayaa xaaxi waaxiyoo gishshatawunne qassikka I kuriyaan kuriyaan shaahettidi xaafettana danddayiyoo gishshataasa. Ane kaallidi diraamaa qommota xeelloos.

7.3. Diraamaa qommota
Diraamaani bayratettan erettiyaa heezzu dumma dumma  qommoti de'oosona, hegeetikka: miichchiyaa diraamaa “comedy”, kayyo poluwaara de'iyaa diraamaa “tragedy” nne kayyonne miichchabanne woykko “tragicomedy” geetettiyoogan erettoosona. Kaallidi de'iyaa baggay hageetu dummatettaa loytti qonccissi yootees.


7.3.1. Ufayssiyaa/Miichchiyaa Diraamaa “Comedy” 
Ufayssiyaa/Miichchiyaa diraamaa “Comedy” yaagiyaagee kaassa gididi A wurssettay ufayssiyaaba woykko miichchiyaaba gididoogaa. Hegaakka giyoogee issi diraamaa giddon de'iyaa bayra/ano  eeshshaawaa qaattay/poloy ufayssiyaa hanotan wurees giyoogaa. I asaa naa ufayssanawunne hombocissanawu halchchettidi oosettiyaaba. Hegaa giyoogee miichchiyaa diraamay miichchiyaaba xalaaliyoo bari giddon oyqqees giyoogaa gidennan issitoo issitoo qarettiyaanne miichchennabaykka gelees. Gido shin ha diraamaa giddo bayratettan keehi aaho hanotan beettiyaa gee miichchiyaa hanotaa giyoogaa.  

7.3.2. Kayyo poluwaara de'iyaa Diraamaa “Tragedy”
Kayyo poluwaara de'iyaa diraamaa giyoogee diraama qommo gididi diraamaa giddon beettiyaa bayra eeshshaawawunne a kaafiyaa hara xeelliyaa asaa wurssettan kayyuwaaninne afuxissiyaa ogiyaan polettiyaaba. Ha kayyoyiyaa hanotati xeelliyaageetu wozanaa kayyuwaaninne yashshan kunttoosona. Qanttan Kayyo poluwaara de'iyaa diraamay minttiyooy/tishshissiyooy issi kayyoyiyaa/lo'enna woykko ufayssenna poluwaana. Ha diraamaa qommuwawu kayyo poloy de'iyaaba gidikkonne bari giddon issi issi ufayssiyaa/miichchiyaa wodetakka oyqqees. Ha ufayssiyaa/miichchiyaa hanotata wurssettan iitabawu/kayyoyiyaabawu laamettiyay. Ha diraama qommuwawu lo'o leemiso gidiyay “Sophocles’s Oedipus the King and Shakespeare’s Othello.” Yaagiyaa diraama.

7.3.3. Ufayssiyaanne/Miichchiyaanne kayyoyiyaa diraamaa (tragicomedy)
A sunttaappe nuuni akeekana danddayiyoogaadan ha diraamay ufayssiyaa/miichchiyaa diraamaanne kayo poloy de'iyoo diraamaa walaha giyoogaa. Qommo baggaara nu be'idoogaadan kayyo poluwaara de'iyaa diraamaa giddon issi issi ufayssiyaa/miichchiyaa wodeti de'ana danddayiyoogaadankka ufayssiyaa/miichchiyaa diraamaa garssaanikka issi issi kayyoyiyaa wodeti de'oosona. 
Ha diraamay doomettidoy laatamantto xeetu layttatu giddon Ibsen and Ionesco yaagiyaa diraama asatuuna. Etikka asa naa de'oy kayyoba xalaala gidennanne qassikka ufayssa/miichcha xalaala gidenna yaagidi palamoosona. Asa naa de'uwaa hanotay issi erettennabanne ha naa''u ufayssiyaanne kayyoyiyaabatun kumidaba yaagoosona. 


Oyshaa
Heezzaa heezzaa oyqqiyaa citan gididi hagaappe kasa intte be'ido miichchiyaa diraamaa (Comedy drama) hassayidi issoy issuwawu kayan kayan yootite. 

7.4. Diraamaa eeshshata
Diraamaa hara bila era oosotuppe shaakkiyaa dumma dumma A eeshshati de'oosona. Hegeetuppekka koyroy diraaman eeshshaawati issi medhdhdi xaafo oosuwaa tumu asatun woykko eeshshaawatun malatissidi daraphaa bolli kiyidi bollan beettidi ootti bessiyoogaa. Naa''anttoy galchchay shiiqidi xeelliyoo woykko be'iyoo eeshshaa (the presence of spectators). Heezzanttoy qassi diraaman haasayay poluwaara issippe hanettiyoogaa (performance through dialogue and action) Ooninne bari galla galla de'uwan bari qofaa gidin ay hanotaakka hara asaara haasayan shaakkiyoogaadan diraamaanikka haasayay woykko qofaa shaakkiyoogee poluwaara issippe beettees. Qassikka diraamay tamaaridaagawu gidin tamaaribeennaagawu lagge akeekettana danddayees; ayssi giikko I haasayaara issippe polettiyaaba gidiyoo gishshatawu xeelliyaa/eziggiyaa galchchay bari ayfiyaan xeellees qassikka bari hayttanikka siyees. Qassikka diraamay asaa sinttan be'ettiyaaba gidiyoogaadaanikka wurssettawu eesotees; asaykka A wurssettaa ayfiyaa uttidosankka be'i aggees. Wurssettankka, diraamay cita ooso (it has collective nature). Issi diraamay issi asi barkka ootti bessiyooba woykko poliyooba gidennan bari giddon cora dumma dumma ootti bessiyoo/haasayaa eray de'iyoo eranchchata xaaxi waaxees. 

7.5. Diraamay bari giddon oyqqiyoobata
Issi diraamaa xeelliyoogee xaafettidaagaa nabbabiyoogaappe keehi dummatees.
