Diraamaa be'anawu shiiqikko diraamaa ootti bessiyaa eeshshaawatu equwaa, eta bollaa qaattaa (facial expression) be'aasa, eta haasayaa siyaasa qassikka eta qaattaa ne ayfiyaan xeellaasa; Hegaa bollakka qassi he polettiyoo sohuwaa poo'uwaa hanotay, yetta cenggurssay diraamaayyo dumma puulakka mayzzees. Yaaniyoo gishshawu diraamaa woykko kaassaa nabbabiyaa asi ha ubbaa bari kahaan qoppana bessees. Diraamaa meretaabaa daro akeekanawu diraamay bari giddon oyqqiyoobata xeelliyoogee go''iyaaba. Hagaappe kaallidi diraamay bari giddon oyqqiyoobatuppe bayratiyaageeta ane xeelloos.

  7.5.1. Karssikarssaa (plot)
Diraamay bari giddon oyqqiyoobatuppe issoy karssikarssaa. karssikarssaa giyoogee issi diraaman woykko medhdhi xaafuwa giddon de'iya naa''u asatu/citatu giddon merettiya phalqqettaa giyoogaa. Na''u citan, woykko wolqqatun woykko asatu giddon haniyaa palamaa denttidi maayettennan ixxidi doonan gidin wolqqan dom''ettiyoogaa. Doona palamaa gidikko naa''u gayttenna qofatun tollu/chikki giidi woykko issoy issuwa qofaa ekkenna ixxidi dom''ettiyoogaa. Wolqqan qassi dom''ettiyaaba gidikko naa''u wolqqati mashshaa toora deuttidi worettoosona hayqettoosona giyoogaa. Ha  korssikarssay merettiiddi naa''u wolqqatu giddon qofaa, meretaa, eeshshaa, ammanuwa, xeelaa hegeetanne hegeeta malatiyaabatun gayttennaagan woykko dummatiyoogan baasettees.
Karssikarssay bari giddon oyqqiyoobata















Asaa  naa de'uwa giddon keehi cora qofaa phalqqettati de'oosona. Asay bari de'uwa giddon bari amottidobaa kunttanawu, xayidobaa demmanawu, metuwa xayssidi saruwan de'anawu, bari de'iyoo hanotaappe kehiyaabaa demmanawu baaxetees. Ha hanotati ayba baaxeenne baynnan coo kuni aggenna. Hegaa giddon daro metoti de'oosona. issi izaawu bari koyyidobaa kunttaanawu baaxetiyoowode ayyo xube gidiyaabati meretti aggoosona. Hegaappe kiyanaassi eeshshaaway daro balbbuqettan gelees, daro baaxetees giyoogaa. Ha balbbuqettaa xoonanaayyo qassi eeshshaaway galla galla minnidi baaxefana koshshees. He baaxiyaa geello dan xoonidi ba koyyidoba demidikka asa gididoogee bari demmidoban ufauttidinne alidi de'enna. Hara aaroba koshshawu kiyees. He koshshan qassikka hara karssikarssaa giddo gelidi baaxeteesikko. Haraakka demmidi hara ooratta amuwa, koshshaa denttees. Kaallidikka hara xube gidiyaabi merettees. Ha hanotan deiuwa camo hanotaynne de'uwa mal''oy qonccees. Asanaa amuwawu zawi baynnaagaappe denddidaagan gayttiya metuwassinne baaxiyassi paydoy de'enna. Metotikka dumma dummanne daro. 

Medhdhi haafuwa giddon de'iya eeshshaawati ha alamiyan de'iya tumu asa zaari beso gidiyoo gishshatawu asaa deuwappe xayenna daro mutti- murunobati gayttoosonanne dumma dumma paaceti tiran kiyi wodhdhoosona. Hedhdhi xaafuwa giddon karssikarssaa yaagiyoogee hageetu mala de'uwa baaxiya xoonidi kessi ekkanawu oosettiya woretaa giyoogaa. 

Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon tumu asaa de'uwadan karssikarssay denddiyoo cora gaasoti deoosona. Leemissuwassi asa na'i barkka bari giddon yootettana danddayees. Hegaa giyoogee issi assi issi allaalliya polana gi qoppiyoo wode hara baggara qassikka A wozanay poloppa yaagees. Ha hanotan issi asa wozanay A “ootta; oottoppe” giyoo hanotay asi banaara medhdhiyoo karssikarssaa bessees. 

Asi qassikka asaara woykko bari deriyaara yootettana / karssikarssana danddayees. Issi asi hara asaara qofaa maayettennan woykko issi asi bari dere assaa wogaappe kareera polana koyyobi de'ikko deree aara eqettiyo gishshatawu karssikarssay denddees. Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon shiiqiyaa karssikarssawu denddoykka ha ogiyan poolettiyaa baaxetuuna. Ha karssikarssay baaxiya bollan de'iya asatu bollan woykko qoppiya kahan paaccana danddayees. 
Eeshshaawati banttaa gelidobaappe kessi ekkanawu, xooni kiyanawu woykko bantta qoppidosaa gakkanawu eti oottiyo baaxee medhdhi xaafuwassi puulaanne loo'otettaa mayzzees. 
     
   7.5.2. Eeshshaawaa 
Ha ufurettaay bessiyoy medhdhi xaafo giddon wooxxi qaaxxiya dumma dumma eeshshaa ekkidi tumukka nu alamiyaa giddon beettana danddayiyaa asa malatidi medhdhi xaafuwa giddon dumma dumma oosota/ taarikiyaa poliya asa. Medhdhi xaafo giddon eeshshawi oottiyoo woykko poliyo taarikee alame giddon qogetti woykko poletti erennaba gidennan asaa de'uwan hanana danddayiya oosota/yohota. Eeshshaawati xaafanchchay /eranchchay bari kanan qoppidi medhdhiyoo heeraadan de'iyaa asata. Eti nunadan metootoosona. Qoppoosona suntan meraanikka nuna malatoosona giyoogaa.
Xaafanchchay bari xaafiyoo medhdhi xaafuwa giddon bessiyoobati ha nu alame giddon I poli dobatanne loyttidi akeekidobata. I xaafiiddi tumu asay bari so giddon, bari moottan, bari ooso keettaninne dumma dumma sohotun poliyoobatanne eta gakkana danddayiya hanotata tumu asaa gishshaa ekkidi poliyaa eeshshaawata go'ettees. Taarikiyaa giddon polettiyaabati ubbay polettiyoy woykko haniyoy ha eeshshaawata giyoogeetuuna. 
Medhdhi xaafuwa eeshshaawati ha alamiya asaa gishshanchchta gidiyoogaappe denddidoogan nu moottan de'iyaa asa nu eriyoogaadan erana danddayiyoogeeta. Eta eta suntan, eeshshan, meran shaakkidi ereettees. 
 “Eshshaawati medhdhi xaafuwa alamiyan asho maayidi, eeshshaa ekkidi, etawu suntti imettido, de'iyoo sohoy giigido, yaa haa qaaxxiya, shemppiya, haasayiya, miya, uyiya tumu alamiya asadan de'iya, hayqqiya, namisettiya, saammettiya siiqettiyaa, ooyettiya, ufayttiyaanne kayyottiya medhdhi xaafo alame asa. Eeshshaawati medhdhi xaafoy merettido sohuwaninne wodiyan pulttida he wodiyaanne he sohuwa asa gishshaawa gidishin he wodiyan. de'ida qogaanne xaaxi waaxo xeelaa,wogaanne maabaraa meezziya ayaa naamanne buquraawa hanotata bessoosona. Daraasiya kahan merettida he wodiya qofaynne asaa issoy issuwara gayttiyo hanotay etan beettiyo asa mala.”  (Asfaa zarihuna/1992: 160) 
Medhdhi- xaafuwa eeshshaawati asa malafidi gidennan asa gididi medhdhi xaafuwa giddon hashetanaadaaninne nabbabbiyaa asi tuma giidi ekkanaadan xaafanchchay naagettidi eta medhdhanawu woykko misilanawu bessees. Ane medhdhi xaafuwa eeshshaa wata kaallideiya ogetun xeelloos. 
      
  7.5.3. Eeshshaawati shiiqiyoo ogeta 
Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon de'iya eeshshaawati muumidi haasayennaggeeta gidana bessenna. Eeshshaawati la'an bantta doona go'ettidi haasayana bessees. Xaafanchchay oychchana bessiyaasan oychchananne zaaran bessiyaasan zaarana koshshees. Nabbabiyaa asi oysha denttanawu bessiya hanoti beettana koshshenna. “ ha eeshshaaway hagan haasayana bessennee?” yaagidi medhdhi xaafuwa nabbabiya asi oysha giddo gelana bessenna. Haray qassi eeshshaaway medhdhi xaafuwa giddon loyttidi hashetana bessees. Eeshshaawa gididi medhdhi xaafuwan issitookka geeliichchida asi dumma dumma sohotuninne wodetun dum,madumma oosota poliiddi beettana koshshees. Medudhi xaafuwa giddon beettiya eeshshaawati eti gishshatido deriyaassi eqqana bessees. Issi asa gidennan issi dariya giddon hanettiyaabaa shiishshidi bessana koshshees. Hegaa bollaarikka eeshshawati nabbabbiyaageetun ammanettiyaagaa gidana bessees. Eeshshaawati asi hegaadan hanenna woykko oottenna giyoobaa polana bessenna. Xaafanchchay bari medhdhi-xaafuwa giddon I medhdhi gelissido gishshatawu bari koyyidobaa haasayissanawu woykko ootissanawu danddayenna. Hegaa gishshawu eeshshaawati issitookka etayyo imettida eeshshan kaaletettana besseesippe attin eranchchay bari koyyoogaadan, oottana danddayenna. Eta eeshshhsawu polotettay de'ana bessees. Taarikiyaa doomettan etawu imettida eeshshay wurssettaa gakkanaashin etaara gidana bessees. Gido shin qassi eeshshaawaa hanotaa/ eeshshaa laammanawu keehi koshshiyoo hanotay woykko wolqqanttiyaa mino gaasoy de'iyaaba gidikkonne taarikiyaassi immiyo go'ay de'ikko eta eeshshay laamettana danddayees. 
Eshshaawatuyyo issuwawu issuwawu haraappe dummatiya eta eeshshay de'ana bessees. Bantta dumma dumma eeshshankka bantta deriya wogaanne meezziya qonccisana bessees. Eshshaawati haniyoobaaninne oottiyooba. Ubbabankka polo gididi merettana koshshenna. Hegee aybissi giikko ay asa na'a gidikkone bari eran, oosuwan qofan polo gidana danddayenna. Ay asanwunne lefa miyyee/ woykko paaiyaa de'ees hegaa gishshawu eeshshaawati medhdh xaafuwa giddon polo gididi simerettana koshshenna. Hegaa gishshatawu mehdhi- xaafuwa xaafiya asi ha qommo baggaara nuuni be’ido eeshshaawati shiiqiyoo ogeta akeekidinne hasayidi xaafikko A oosoy nabbabbiyaa asan ammanettiyaagaa gidana danddayees. 
Medhdhi xaafuwa giddon beettiyaa mule eeshshaawatussikka taarikiyaa giddon lagge qaattay/ hanotay de'enna. Aybissi giikko issi medhdhi xaafuwa giddon eeshshaawati naa''u ginawu shaahettana danddayoosona. Hegeetikka: 
I)	Bayra/ano eeshshaawatanne 
II)	Sima/kaalo  eeshshaawata 

Ane ha naa''u eeshshawa qommota kayan kayan akeekidi xeelloos. 

7.5.4.1. Bayra / ano eeshshaawata
Bayra woykko ano eeshshaawata giyoogeeti taarikiya doomettaappe biidi poluwa gakkanaashin ubba sohuwanikka simerettiya woykko taarikiyassi daro sohotun hashetiiddi beettiya taarikiya poliyaa asata. Eti medhdhi xaafuwa giddon beettiyaa hara asatu ubbaappe aaro qaaxxoosonanne corabaa poliiddi beettoosona. Bayra eeshshaawa giyoobi taarikiya dendduwappe doommidi beettiyoogee ayyo attennaba gidenna. Issi eeshshaaway leemisuwassi taarikiyaasi gidduwa heeran yiidi keehi darobaa poliiddi beettana danddayees. Doomettan beetti beennaba gidikkonne. Ha eeshshaawi taarikiya doomettan de'ana xaykkonne bayra/ ano eeshshaawa gidennaadan A digiyaabi baawa. 
7.5.4.2. Sima/kaalo eeshshaawata
Sima woykko kaalo eeshshaawata giyoogeeti issi medhdhi xaafuwaa giddon guutta sohotuni polettiyaabatun beettidi woykko hashetidi bantta allaalliyaa polinne sohuwaarakka xayi aggiyaageeta. Eti medhdhi xaafuwa giddon guutta sohotun hashetido gishshatawu eti taarikiya dichchaassi maaddokkona woykko medhdhi xaafuwa giddon maaddokkona giyoogaa gidenaa. Sima eeshshaawati medhdhi- xaafuwa garssan ano eeshshaawatuppe guuxxenna hanotan koshshoosona. Ha ano eeshshaawati sima eeshshaawatun kaatettidi bantta oosuwa poloosona. Sima eeshshaawatikka ano eeshshaawatudan medhdhi xaafuwaassi logge koshshoosona. Naa''aappe issoy baynnaba gidiyakko taarikee taarike gidennan aggana danddayees. Issi issi dirassatetun woykko medhdhi xaafotun issi issi wode sima eeshshaawati sunttetti simmidi, eretti simmidi, taarikiya giddon aybanne qaattennan/ haasayennan woykko aybanne polennan sirphphi giidi attiigiyo hanotay de'ees. Hagee gamma gidenna. Taarikiya giddon aybanne hashetenna eeshshaawi koyro gelana bessenna. Gelliichchidaba gidikko taarikiyaan hashetana bessees giyoogaa. Geellodan issi issi wode medhdhi xaafuwa giddon suntan erettenna izaawu woykko issi citan de'iyaa asati taarikiyaa giddon hashetiyo hanotati de'oosona. Hegeetikka sima eeshshaawatuura baggattoosona giyoogaa. 
Issi issi wode issi issi medhdhi xaafuwan woykko dirssatiyan Ayyaanati, kiitanchchati, xalahee, azzaqa do'ati hegaanne hegeeta malatiyaageeti eeshshawadan shiiqiyo hanotay de'ees. Eti ooninne erin asa gidana xayikkonne medhdhi xaafuwa dirssatiyaa giddon eti misatana bessiyoy gamma asa eeshsha ekkidi gidana bessees. Eti asaa eeshshaa ekkidi asadan haasayiiddi, asadan hemettiiddi, qoppiiddi, dosobaa poliiddi beettana bessees. Eti asadan qossi shiiqaappe guyyiyaan eeshshaawadan qoodettoosona giyoogaa. 
             7.5.5. Haasayaa / Dialogue
Medhdhi xaafuwan woykko dirssatiya oosuwan haasayan (dialogue) giyoogee xaafanchchay bari xaafo oosuwa giddon eeshshaawatuyyo eta haasaya gidenna haasayaa immidi hegaa eti haasayanaadan oottiyo hanotaa. Eeshshawati medhdhi xaafo giddon bantta koyyido ay yohuwaanne leemisuwassi bantta sintta qofaa, bantta polidobaa, polarawu halchchidobaa, xayidobaa, demmidobaa, ufayttidoba hegeetanne hegeeta  malatiyabata denttidi haasayana danddayoosona. Issi eeshshaawoy haro eeshshaawaa baakka denttidi haasayana danddayees. Gido shin eta hccasayay eti kiyidi yiido dere asaa wogaa gishshatiyaaba gidana bessees. Haray atto shin xaafanchchay bari immiyo qonccissuwaappe aaruwa eeshshaawatu haasayawu aaho qaadaa immidi eta haaswyissana
Bessees. Hegaa giishin ubba ayba allaallccnne baynna pattenna hada haasayan eeshshaawatu wodiya xuuggana woykko taarikiya shongacissana keshshes giyoogaa gidennan allaallee de’iyonne birshsh/nettaa immiya hanotan qoncce gidida eeshshaawatu haasayaa gelissana koshshees. Ha tekinikee medhdhi xaafuwa eoshshawuata nabbabbiyaageetawu qoneeissiyo ogetuppe issuwa. 
              7.5.6. Cuccumaa/Theme
Caccumay woykko Aristootile qofaa (thought) yaagiyoogee inggiliizettuwan (theme) giyooyee diraamaa xeelliyaa woykko nabbabbiyaa asassi aattiyo bayra kiitaa. I bari giddon oyqqido ano qofay cuccumaa giyoogaa. Xaafanchchy ekkidi denddido issi tumubaa asaa bessanawu eeshshaawata go'ettidi bessees. Cuccumay dicci diccidi biyoy karssikarssaa kasiyaa kaaluwan, eeshshaawatu meruwaan, eeshshaawatu haasayaaninne xeelliyoobatuuna. Xaaxi waaxiyoode issi diraamaa giddon beettiyaa dumma dummabati diraamaa cuccumaay merettanawu baaso gidoosona.
Giddoppe attin eeshshaaway ba gelido karssikarssaappe kessi ekkanawu oottiyo baaxxiya shiishshees. He baaxiya wurssettan issi ayfiya bessees. Shin ha ubbaa giddon xaafanchchay aattana koyyido cuccumay issippe doomettaappe biidi poluwa gakkandashin ohettidi yees. Cuccumay diraamaa ano qofaadan diraamaayyo doomettan, woykko giddo ginaa heeran woykko wurssettaa heeran beettiyaaba gidenna. Cuccumay diraamaa doomettaappe biidi wurssettaa gakkanawu xeelli wurssi simmin beettiyaaba. 
Xeelliyaageekka diraamaa xeelliyoo wode dubbushshiiddi, miicciiddinne ufayttiiddi issi tumanchcha gidiyaa bayra kiitaa aattanawu koyyido ano yohuwa/ kiitaa akeekees. Xeelli wurssiyoo wodiyaana kumetta kiitay/cuccumay Ay kahawunne aadhdhiyoynne qoncciyoy. 

                      7.5.7. Daraphaa ohettaa (staging)
Diraamay daraphaa bolli kiyidi ootti bessiyoo/poliyoo ooso. Issi diraamay daraphan polettiyoo wode daraphaa giyaa qaalaa giddon dumma dummabati xaaxi waaxettoosona. Hara qaalan daraphaa giyo qaalay bari giddon xeelliyoo wode beettiyaabata oyqqees, hegeetikka eeshshaaway daraphaa bollan eqqiyoo/uttiyoo sohuwaa, bollaa qaattaa (gestures), daraphaa bollan yaa haa simerettiyoo hanotaa (movement on the stage), maayuwaa maayiyoo hanotaa, cenggurssaa, daraphaa zokkossaa, daraphaa bolli beettiyaa yaa haa qaattana danddayiyoo miishshata h.h.malatiyaageeta.
